1.1 Wunaumau missinnin noh matta aonk wuttuwonganit matchetou, asuh matta neepau8k, ummáyeuout matchese[a]enuog, asuh matta ápegk wutappuonganit mamanowontamwaénin.
1.2 Qut wuttinn8waonganit Jehovah wuttapeneaum8onk, kah wuttinn8waonk missantam kesukodtaeu kah nukkonáeu.
1.3 Kah ogqueneunkqussu mehtugqut ahketeámuk ut kishke sepupogqut, noh ummeechummuonk uppaudtunk nehenwonche utt8wutchu: kah 8neepog matta pish n8kshaun8h, kah wame uttoh ásit pish misségen.
1.4 Matta neane matchetukeg: ut ogqueneunkqussuog wossadtea[u]munit, uttiyeu t8[u]nontog waban.
1.5 Newutche matta neepauóog matcheetupanatogig wussittum8onganit; asuh matcheussecheg ut ummukkinneonganit wunnomwaeussecheg.
1.6 Newutche 8wahteóun Jehovah ummayash sampwesecheg: qut ummayou matcheetupanatogig pish awakompanóm8.
2.1 Tohwutch penuohteáog musquantamohettit, kah missinninnuog unnantamo[h]ettit tahn8che teaguas.
2.2 Ketass8tamwog ohkeit chipaphéaog wuhhogkauh, & n[a]nánuácheg ken8nittuog ayeuuhkonittue Godut, kah ayeuuhkonittue sasequnónche, n8waog.
2.3 Paskuhkommuttuh wutahtagkups8ongash, amauhteátuh uppémunohtean8ash, wutch kuhhogkanónut.
2.4 Noh apit kesukqut [h]ahánou: Manit ummómontauoh.
2.5 Onk pish nahhoh ken8[n]uh musquantog: pish wutchepheuh m8cheke musquantog.
2.6 Qut onch nuppon nukketass8tamom n8netupanatamwe ut wadchumut Sion.
2.7 N8wahteauwáhuwam k[e]santamóonk Jehovah nuttugkup, ken nunnaumon, yeu kesukok k8naumóniyeu[m]sh.
2.8 Wehquetumah, onk kittinnumoush penowohte[á]og wutche k8kompuhchasuash, kah aongkóe anohk[e]8g wutche kutahtóonk.
2.9 Pish kussukquttahwhôog nashpe móohshogque a[n]wohhou, pish kuss8kquohkonot onatuh ahkuhqutteaénin 8wisquadt.
2.10 Waantam8k yowutche, woi ketass8tamwog, netuhtau8k kenaau wussittamwaenuog yeu ut ohkeit.
2.11 Waussum8k Jehovah nashpe wabesuonk, weekontam8k nashpe nunnuksh[u]onk.
2.12 Chipwutt8unáp8k wunnaumónain, ishkont musquantog, kah kuppaguanimw8 wutche mayut: umm8squantam8onk nashqunak webe oggu[h]se[?]ese, 8nanumó[ȯ]g n[]nag paubuhtanumoncheg.
3.0 {Ukketeohhomaonk} David, to[m]wutauont wutch anaquabit} Absolomwoh {wunnaumonuh.}
3.1 Jehovah, toh nuttin k8hk8tne neg wadtaméhitcheg monaog neg ayeuohkôsitcheg.
3.2 Monaog weatimoncheg nukketeahogkonuh: matta ahtôou aninnummoadtuonk ut Godut. Selah.
3.3 Qut ken woi Jehovah, nutógquneg, nussohsumôonk, kah noh tohshinuk nuppuhkuk.
3.4 Nummauunitteau God nashpe nummishontowáonk, onk nunn8tunk wutch 8netupantamwe wadchumut. Selah.
3.5 Nussepsinup, kah nukkoueep, nutt8kep, newutche Jehovah n[a]naihuk.
3.6 Matta woh n8wabesuónuh piogqut muttanonganogkussuog missinninnuog, weenuhkoi[e]hettit.
3.7 Neepaush Jehovah, wadcháneh woi num-Manitt8m, newutche ken kuttógkom wame nummatwomog ut wutompikkonn8w[ó]ut: kuppohquetahham weepittash matcheetou.
3.8 Wadchanittuonk wutchaiyeum8 Godut: k8naneteáonk ut kummissinninnu[m]tu. Selah.
4.0 {Nohtumuhpequodt ut} Neginoth, {ketohhomaonk} David.
4.1 NOOtah nanompussumunon, woi num-Manitt8m n8nomwaeusseonk, kussohwhuneup, kobhóseon, kitteamonteanum[e]h, kah n8tash nuppeantam[ó]wonk.
4.2 Woi kenaau wunnaumonoh wosketompaog, toh utt8che kukquinnuppémw8 nussohsumówonk en akodchinat? kah k8womantamumw8 tohn8che usseonk, kah kenátinnehamw8 pann8waonk? Selah.
4.3 Qut wahteau8k, Jehovah wutchippeponamonuh wáneetupanatamunutcheh, Jehovah nunn8[t]unk wehquetumauog.
4.4 Wabesek, kah hque matchesek, n8wagk nehenwonche ketahh8wóut ut kutappinneôut, kah chequnussin8k. Selah.
4.5 Sephamók God wunnomwausseae sephauseonk, kah 8namptók Jehovah.
4.6 Monaog n8waog howan nahtinukqueog wanegik? Jehovah tohshinumaiinnean 8wequ[á]8m kuskesuk.
4.7 Kummagun weekontamowonk ut nuttahhut, m8cheke onk mônakish 8weatchiminneoash kah 8ske[n] winneum8.
4.8 Na neese wunnohteáe nusseepsin kah nukkouem, newutche webe ken Jehovah, kutáyimah nánauwantamóe wunáyeuonk.
5.0 {Nahtompuhpequodt}, Nehiloth: {Ukketoohhamaonk} David.
5.1 NOOtash nukkutt8wonganash, woi Jehovah, natwontash nunnatwontamowonk.
5.2 Kukkeihtash n8wadtauatonkqussumauwonk, nuk-Ketass8tom8m, kah num-Manitt8m, newutche ken kuppeantamoush.
5.3 N8wodtauatonkqussuonk woh ken8tam nompoáeu, woi Jehovah: nompoáeu kussampwunnumauunun nuppeantamóonk, kah nuttushpoquáim.
5.4 Newutche ken Manit, matta kuttapeneaum8h matcheseonk, onk matta k8weetomuk8h matcheseonk.
5.5 Mattammag[u]og matta pish neepau8og anaquabea[n], kussekeneau wame anakausitcheg matcheseonk.
5.6 Pish kuppaguanóog nag pann8wacheg: Jehovah ukkogkoánum[a]u sheuteaén[ú]h kah as8kekodteanúh.
5.7 Qut neen nuppetutteam keekit, newutche mónatasah kummonaneteaonganash: kah k8wabissuónitteonganit k8wôwussumush, en nogque k8netupanatámukkomukqut.
5.8 Sagkompaguneh, woi Jehovah, en k8nomwausseonganit, newutche nummatwomog: sampweteaush kummay ut anaquabeh.
5.9 Newutche matta wunnomwayeuonganinno ut wutt8n8wóut, wuttinnomaiyeú[m]8wóut matcheseongash: ukquttungan8 wôshwi weenohkeyeu8, nanwonyeum8wog ut weenann8w[ó]ut.
5.10 Páguas naghog woi God, penushahettich nashpe nehenwonche ukken8nittuonganuwóut: pogkenok newutche monakish ummatcheseongan8óash, newutche kukkeitohteanánittuwáhukquog.
5.11 Qut wame yeug paubuhtanumukqueaneg, weekontamohettich, nagwutteáeu weekontamóe mishont8wahettich, newutche nag kukkinhamauog: onk nag womontogig k8wesuonk weekontamowónukqush.
5.12 Newutche ken Jehovah k8nanum wanomwae ussecheg: nashpe k8womóussúonk k8weenuhkau, onatuh ogqunneg.
6.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt} Neginoth, {ut} Sheminith: {Ukketoohhamaonk} David.
6.1 Woi Jehovah ahque áuskomeh ut kummusquantamowonganit, onk ahue sasamakoúheh ut kussópetáe kummusquanetam8wonganit.
6.2 Monanumeh, woi Jehovah, newutche n8chumwes: woi Jehovah, neetskeheh, newutche nussaú8kon.
6.3 Nukketeahogkou wonk m8cheke onkuppunnau: qut ken, woi Jehovah, aquompak.
6.4 Quinnuppish, woi Jehovah, pohquahwus nukketeahogkou: woi wadchaneh, newutche kummonaneteaonk.
6.5 Newutche nápumukish matta kummequanumitteoh: ut weenohket howan tabuttantamunkquean.
6.6 Nussauanum nutáiukkóntowáonk, qunnenuhkon nutaiyum nutappen pomons8wémou, ut nashpe nussuppequash nutogquehchippadtóh nutappin.
6.7 Nuskesukquash mohtupaemoash wutch mauonk: nano wussesekshau newutche wame nummatwomog.
6.8 Amaeitaegk wame anakauseógish matcheseonk: newutche Jehovah n8tam nummauongane wadtauatongqussuonk.
6.9 Jehovah n8tam n8weehquetumowonk, Jehovah neemunnum nuppeantamowonk.
6.10 Nummatwomog wame akodchehettich, kah onkapunahettich: quinnuppehettich, kah akodchhettich teanuk.
7.0 Shiggaion David, {yeush ketoohomauau Jehovah papaume ukkuttoowongash} Cush {up-Benjamite}.
7.1 Woi Jehovah num-Manitt8m, nen kupbaubuhtánumoush, wadchaneh wutch wame neg kodwoskhukqueoneg, kah pohquahwusseh.
7.2 Ishkont sóhkwushônau nukketeahogkonuh, onatuh qunônou sohqshadtunk, matta woh toh adt wodchanutteumukish.
7.3 Woi Jehovah num-Manitt8m, yeu usséon, matcheseongan88uk nunnutcheganit.
7.4 Onkquodtaúogis matcheseonk wonohk[â]sit (nux, nuppohquohwhunop noh tahn8che ayeuohkáusit.)
7.5 Matwau wunnômattuhkauonch nukketeahogkonuh, kah tohqunonch, nux, taskuhkodch nukketeaonk ohkekontu, kah ayeuw[á]hitch nukquehtiánumitteaonk puppissiyeuut. Selah.
7.6 Waapish, woi Jehovah, musquantaman waabin kuhhog, newutche ukkogkeeuwaongan8 nummatwomog: kah t8nhkanumwansheh en ne wussittumm8onganit, ne an8w[á]up.
7.7 Nemehkuh mukkinneonkane missinninnuog pish k8weenohkongquog, newutche nag wutch qunnunkquappúe qushkish.
7.8 Jehovah pish wussumau missinninnuh; wussummeh, woi Jehovah, neaunag n8nomwausseonk, kah neaunag nussampweusseonk nen ut nuhhogkaut.
7.9 Woi matcheetowog ummatcheetowongan8 wohkukqu[t]hsitch, qut menehkeh sampwesecheg: newutche wunnomwáe God qutchehtau metahhash, kah mutt8nussoh.
7.10 Nuttongk8ogquss8 God: noh wadchanont sampwuttahonutcheh.
7.11 God wussumau wunnomwausseaenuh: God musquanumau matcheetowoh asekesukokish.
7.12 Matta quinnuppekompauuk, kéhtadtau wuttogkodteg, ónchippinnau wutohtompe kah ukquoshwunuh.
7.13 Kah wonk ukquóshwunnumau tôh woh ánuppinnit: kah wussantequohwoh ukk[ô]unkquodtash noshteanutcheh.
7.14 Kusseh, wutonkquomome paudtaun matcheseonk, wompequaou woskehuwáonk, kah pann8wayeuonk neechau.
7.15 Wônteaúh, kah ukkuthámun, onk petshau wônogqut ne kezteunk.
7.16 OOwoskhuwáonk pish quinnuppem8 en nehenwonche uppuhkukqut, kah wutcheke usseonk pish pogkishin nehenwonche uppuhkukqut.
7.17 Nuttabuttantamau Jehovah neaunag 8[n]omwausséonk: kah nuttinn8hhomom tabuttantamóonk, 8wesuonganit Jehovah noh quanunkquappit.
8.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut} Gittith: {Ketoohhomaonk} David.
8.1 Woi Jehovah num-Manitt8m, uttoh nukkukque wunnegen k8wes[u]onk wame muttaohket! kupponam kussohsumóonk ongkouwe kesukqut.
8.2 Wutch wutt8n8wóut mukkiesog, kah n8nukeg kuhkuhquttum menuhkesuonk, newutche kummatwomog, onk woh kummanunnisseh matwau onk an8tont.
8.3 Natwontamon kukkesukkumash kuppuhkukqu[á]nutchée anakausuonganash, nahnepaúshadt, kah anogqsog kukkeihtimopanneg.
8.4 Howan wosketomp woh mehquânumadt? kah wosketomp wunnaumonuh woh nadtuahheadt?
8.5 Newutche kukkezheop ut agwésu Angelsog: onk kutcheetuhquabin nashpe sohsumóonk kah quttiánittuonk.
8.6 Kittinnunnumain nánaánumun kenutchegane anakausuongash, kupponam wame teanteaquassinash agwe wusseetit.
8.7 Wame sheepsog kah oxenog, nux, kah puppinashimwog ut ohte[a]konit.
8.8 Puppinushaog mamahchekesukqut, kah namóhsog ketahhannit, kah nishnoh pomushom8 mayash ketahhannit.
8.9 Woi Jehovah num-Manitt8moh uttoh en muttae wunnegen k8wesuonk wame muttaohket.
9.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt [a]t} Muth-Labben: {Ketoohhomaonk} David.
9.1 Kuttabuttantamoush, woi Jehovah, nashpe mámusse nuttahhut: nunnáhtutteam wame kummonchanatamwu anakausuwongash.
9.2 N8weekontam káh kumm[u]skouanatam8woush nuttinn8homom tabuttantam8wongash k8wesuonganit, woi ken quanunkquappean.
9.3 Nummatwomog quaskehettit, nag pish penushaog, kah paguanúog ut anaquabean.
9.4 Newutche kuta[n]umwontamah nussampwusseonk, kah noo[t]s[i]nn8wonganit, kutapip 8sittam8ongane appuonganit, sampwe wussittumunat.
9.5 Kuttaushkomomp penuwohteaog, kuppáguanomp matcheetoweg, kutjiskhomup 8wesuongan8 micheme.
9.6 Woi ken matwau, pagwan8onganash wohkukquôshinneash yauyatcheh: kah kuppapâgodtoh otanash, mehquanumaongan8 nashpu nuppók.
9.7 Qut Jehovah pish michemeyeu8, quaquashwe[e]htomup wutappuonk wutch wussittum8wonk.
9.8 Kah pish sampwe wussittum muttaohke, pish wussumau missinninnúh ut sampwiyeuut.
9.9 Jehovah pajeh spúhh8wáonkánu8 mukk8kinutcheg, pajeh sp[ú]hh8wónganu8 wuttammepunáumuk.
9.10 Kah nag wahteunkig k8wesuonk k8namptunkquog: newutche ken Jehovah matta kenukkonóog neg natinneahhukquéaneg.
9.11 Ket8hhomok Jehovahut, noh ápit Sion: pahketeau8k kenugke missinninnutu wutusseongan8.
9.12 Nat8tomuhteadt nushehteáonk, 8wâanumoh nahog: matta wunánatámou ummauongan8 ohhohpánutcheh.
9.13 Monanumeh, woi Jehovah, natauwompadtash n8tamehpunáonk nashpe nag sekeneunkqueaneg, ken tahshinnea[n] wutch nupp8wongane squontamut.
9.14 Woh nahtitteam wame kuttabuttantamonteaongash 8squontamut wuttaunésoh Sion: n8wekontam k8wadchanuaonganit.
9.15 Penuwóhteaog quttauwéog ut wônahteahéganit ne kesteauhetteup: wonâshahettit appéhonuh, ut upputhugkouoh ut nehenwonche wusseetuóut.
9.16 N8wahêoun Goduh nashpe 8sittam8ongash nish aseche, matchetou puttuhhuk ut nehenwonche wunnutchegane usseonganit Higgaion. Selah.
9.17 Matchetoog pish no[h]kónog chepiohkomukqut, kah wame wutóhtimonneash wananumoncheg Goduh.
9.18 Newutche matta nagwutteáeu wunánuma[ú]ou matchekuoh wutanno[ó]suonk matcheku, matta pish 8wánteauun micheme.
9.19 Omohkish, woi Jehovah, ahque sohkoiitch missinnin, penuwohteaog wussumunaj ut anaquabean.
9.20 Wâbesuah, woi Jehovah: onk woh wutohtimóneash, nehenwonche wahteauog webe wosketompaog. Selah.
10.1 Tohwutch neepaiyean n8adtit, woi Jehovah? tohwutch puttogquéan ne adt wuttammepunni?
10.2 Matcheetou pitchu[à]numwudt kodwoskéhheau matchékuoh: tohqunukquehettich uppuhchúteaongan8 ne unnantamohettit.
10.3 Newutche matcheetou muskóau toh ânahtág wuttah ne nnih: kah wunnanumau i[á]hchewontamwoh uttiyeuh Jehovah óhquanumonche.
10.4 Matcheetou pitchuánumweenongqussit, matta natinneahwóou Goduh, wame wuttinanatam8wonganit matta Godunn8.
10.5 Wutusseongash nagwutteáeu unkqunneonkquodtash: kussittam8wonganash wohqut ahtáash wunn8nomputtamunash: kah wame ummatwomoh ummámeshanimuh.
10.6 N8wau ut wuttahhut, matta pish nuttóntsappu; newutche matta woh toh nuttit wuttammehpunóh.
10.7 Wutt8nit numwohteau matchenánutteáonk, k[á]h as8kekodtea[o]muwonk kah p[ù]hchuteáonk: agwu weenann[ú]uh na wosk[e]huwáonk kah tohn8cheyeu8uk.
10.8 Appu ónkaumpamúkquodtit otanáemesittu, assampamukquodtit, wuttit nushon m[at]ta woskhuánutche: wuskesukquash kemompamáuh matchekuoh.
10.9 Askuhwheteau matta na[û]ou onatuh qunônou, ne seepsuk: askuhwhau matchekuoh noh wuttin tohqunóneat: tohqunau matchekuoh pas8ont wuthashabut.
10.10 Ohtáeu & hohpaheau wuhhogk[u]h, matchekuoh woh penushau nashpe ummenuhkeseumoh.
10.11 N8wau ut wuttahhut, God 8wánanatumun: putt[a]ghom wuskesuk, matta woh nunnukqut naum8.
10.12 Omohkish, woi Jehovah, woi God tohshinush kenutcheg: ahque wananum hohhohpacheg.
10.13 Tohwutch matcheetou mamànowánumónt Goduh? n8wau ut wuttahhut matta k8nompagunnumiéin.
10.14 Kenaumunáp, newutche kenaumun wosk[e]huwaonk, kah wutjishanumowonk, onk nashpe kenutcheg woh wuttinheun: matcheku kuppaubuht[á]numuk wuhhogkuh, ken aninnumauadt nag mat wad8sh8gig.
10.15 Pokshadtash wôhpit matcheetou kah woskehuaénin, natinnehash ummatcheseonganash n[ô] pajeh monteag kummi[s]kom8unat.
10.16 Jehovah keihtas8tam88 micheme kah micheme: penuwohteaog paguanóog wutch wutohtuwóut.
10.17 Jehovah ken8tam hohpou ukkodtantamóonk: kukquoshaeihtam wuttahhou, kutáyum kuhtaúog wutch n8tamunat.
10.18 Wussumónat mat wad8sh8gig, kah woskhetcheg, onk wosketomp yeu muttaohket matta wonk woh woskehuwóou.
11.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ketohhomaonk} David.
11.1 Nuppaubuhtanum ut Jehovah, ut [t]oh woh unnók nukketeuhogkou [p]t8wej onatuh psuksesit en k8wadchum8wóut?
11.2 Newutche kusseh, matcheetowog anchepunuhtaog: quashinumwog úkkôunkquodtou, ut wutahtuman8óut: woh kemu pumwôog sampw[ú]tteah[ó]nutche.
11.3 Quenohtáe agweóhteagish matchehteaumuk, toh woh wutusseneau sampweusseaenúog?
11.4 Jehovah appu wunnetupanatamwe templeut, Jehovah wutappuonk kesukqut: wuskesukquash ná8om8oash, wanadteaskesukquash qutcheheau wunnaumonáoh wosketompaog.
11.5 Jehovah qutchéheau sampweussaénuh, qut ukketeahogkóunoh sekeneauau matchetowoh, kah [n]eh womantamunutcheh chenauausuonk.
11.6 Matcheetowoh pish wussokanummaoh ahpehhanoh, n8htau kah brimstone nashquttin: yeu wutchippiyeum8 wuttattam8ongkan8óut.
11.7 Newutche sampweusseae Jehovah womantam sampweusseonk, wuttinnussuonk moneaúau sampwusseaeneuh.
12.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut} Sheminith: {ketoohhomaonk} David.
12.1 Aninnumaiinnean Jehovah, newutche wanne manittowompaenúun8h: newutche paubuhtanumwaenuog oggushéoog kenugku wunnaumonaohut wosketompaog.
12.2 Tahn8che keket8hkaâog, nish noh weetatteamongan88 nashpe wunanak8wáe wussissitt8n8woash, kah neesi[nn]ú8 wuttahh8woash keket8kaóg.
12.3 Jehovah pish tummessum wunának8wáe mussissitt8nash, kah meenan noh n8wadt mish8waonk.
12.4 N8wâhettit neenannúu[n]nonash pish nutomskausuwohtómun, nussissitt8nonash nehenwonche, howan w[ȧ]santimámeog?
12.5 Newutche matchekuoh woskeheaog kah n8nunnúkeg ummishonnom8óngan8, yeuyeu nutomohkem (n8wau Jehovah) nuppon nanauwinnuat wutche noh mamashanimont.
12.6 Ukkutt8wongash Jehovah pahke kutt8wongash onatuh silver sabassumuk kutohk[o]esabassohsuonganit nesausuk[t]ahshit pahketeaumuk.
12.7 Woh k8wadchanóog, woi Jehovah, kenánaihéaog yeu wutch pometuonganit micheme.
12.8 Matcheetoog popomsháog nish noh ut, uhque matchetowog ut kenugke wunnaumonuh wosketompaog nananuwahettit.
13.0 {Nohtompuhpequ[a]dt ukketoohomaonk} David,
13.1 Tohutt8che pish k8wannumeh (woi Jehovah) nagwutteaeu? tohutt8che pish kupputtogkuhhum kuskesuk wutche neen.
13.2 Tohutt8che woh nukkinn8n nukketeahogkou; neuanatamunish ut nuttahhut asekesukokish: toh utt8che pish nummatwomog mishshehheaog anue onk neen.
13.3 Nawontash kah n8tah, woi Jehovah num-Monitt8m, wussompuwahteoush nuskesukquash; iskont nukkouem nupp8e koueonk.
13.4 Iskont nummatwom n8wau, nutomska[û]óp, kah yeug wadtamméhukquéaneg woh muskouanatamwog ontsappeon.
13.5 Qut nuppaubuhtantam kummonaneteaonk, nuttah muskouanatam8wontam k8wadchan8waonk.
13.6 Nukket8hhomau Jehovah, newutche numm8cheke aninnumunk.
14.0 {Nohtompohpequodt ketohhomaonk} David.
14.1 Mattamog n8wau ut wuttahhut, wanne God[u]n8, aninwog, niskanakausuongash wuttussenáoash, wanne howan wunnesu.
14.2 Jehovah womómpu wutche kesukqut monneáuau wosketomp wunnaumonuh, kodnaum uttoh wuttin wohtamunneau, kah natinnewhon God.
14.3 Wàme amaeog, moeu niskeneonkqussuog matta howan wunnesu, matta pasuk.
14.4 Wame matanakausuog, wanne wahteau8og? m8whôog nummissinninnumoh, mechumuk petukqunneg kah matta wehquetumáauóog Goduh
14.5 Naut m8cheke wabesu[m]og, néwutche God ut uppometuonganit wunnomwausseaénu appu.
14.6 Kutákodchehteomw8 ukken8n8waonk matcheku, newutche Jehovah wutushpuhh8waonguh.
14.7 Woi 8wadchanuongan8 Israel waj sohhom88uk wutch Syon: Jehovah sohh8wunont wutch missinnainneat ummissinninnumoh, Jakob pish muskauanatam, kah Israel pish wekontam.
15.0 {Ketoohhomaonk} David.
15.1 Jehovah, hówan woh apit keekit? howan woh wadohket k8neetupanatamwe wadchumut?
15.2 Noh sompwshadt, kah anakausit Sampweusseonk, kah n8wadt wanamuhkutéyuonk ut wuttahhut.
15.3 Noh matta n8numimonk ut weenañóut: asa mat matchenehheunk weetatteamunguh kah matta wunnamptamaoou kehkontuonk weetatteamunguh.
15.4 Wuskesukquash jishánumau matcheetowoh: qut quttianumau wabesuonóncheg Jehovah: quashómuadt matta qús[h]k8áu tohk[ô]nogque wannéhteunk.
15.5 Noh matta nogohkouhuog wutteaguas wutch anuwu aninnumauwó[n]ah, matta onk quatusseg wutch paumm8waonk ayeuuhkonittue noh matta tamhóuog, howan ásit yeush, matta pish ontsappu.
16.0 {Um-Michtam} David.
16.1 Wadchaneh, woi God: newutche kuppaubahtanumush.
16.2 Nuttah kuttinnomp Jehovah, ken num-Manitt8m: n8neetowonk matta k8nehhukk8un.
16.3 Qut waneetupanatogig yeuut ohkeit, kah wanekitcheg, yeug wame nuttappenea[uo]og.
16.4 Pish monatash wutôhquanum8ongan88ash natinneohwáhettit onkatoge manitt8h: 8tattamóe wsquehheonkane sephamaonk matta nussephamaôh, asa mat neemunnum8h 8wesuongan8h ut nussisset8nut.
16.5 Jehovah wutchippiyeum nutahtaúonk, kah n8tattamwáitch: kenanaáihteóh nuttittanohtôadtúonk.
16.6 Nukhuhkinónghash ut wunnegen ohkéit, nux wunnegen nutahtauonk.
16.7 Nuttabuttantamau Jehovah wutch nukkinn8nuk8onk, onk nutt8unissog nukkuhk8tomunkquog nukkonaeu.
16.8 Nagwutteaeu nuppon Jehovah anaquabeh: newutche appu nuttinnohkôunit, matta pish nutontsappu.
16.9 Newutche nuttah weekontam, kah nussohsumóonk weekontam8m8: kah n8weyaus pish anwôsin8m8 ut an8ôsinneat.
16.10 Newutche matta kenukkonôh nukketeahogkou ut cheppiohkomukqut, asa mat kuttinnanumoh k8neetupanatamwaénin náish aninnowonk.
16.11 Pish k8wahteauwahe may en keteaonganit: anaquabean wâmut weekontam[ó]onk, kuttinohkôonit weekontamóonk micheme kah micheme.
17.0 {Peantamowonk} David.
17.1 Nootash sampweusseonk, woi Jehovah, kuhkeitash nummauonk, n8tash nuppeantamowonk, mo waj sohham8un8g eiantogkieue mussissit8nut.
17.2 K8sum̃uonk 8m8utch wutch anaquabean: kuskesukquash naj wunnomwausseonk.
17.3 Kukqutchteop nuttah, kenátaaheup nukkonaeu: kukqutchheup, kah pish monteag kummiskom8, nutahchuwéussen, nutt8n mat pish matcheyeu.
17.4 Papaume wutanakausuongash wosketompaog nashpe kukkutt8wongash, ut kussisset8nut nunnaanôweh wutch mayut pagúanaucheg.
17.5 Kenunnush nuppomushaongash kummayut, onk mat woh nusseetash t8nequssinun8h.
17.6 K8wehquetummaunup, newutche ken8tah, woi God, equóhtuhquaeihtah, kah n8tash nukkutt8wonganash.
17.7 Nait[u]tt8sh monchanatamwe kukkitteamonte[á]nutteaonk, woi ken pohquóhwuss8waen nashpe kuttinohkôu, nag paubuhtanumukqueaneg, wutch nag au8hkon[ó]ncheg.
17.8 Unn8wadchaneh neane m8eskesuk: puttógwheh wutonkôuhtomut, kenuppawhúnash.
17.9 Nag wutch matchetowog woskhukqueaneg: kodnushhukkowoneg nummatwomog, wéenuhkaitcheg.
17.10 Nupp8kóm8wog nehenwonche 8weesu: wutt8n8 pittuánumweyeú[u]8.
17.11 Yeuyeu nukquiñupuhkóngqunonog nuppomshaonganonut: wuskesuk88ash ussukkompadtaoash ohkekontu.
17.12 Onatuh qunônou paskonóntog neh kodtohqunoncheh: kah onatuh wushkoshim8m qunónou keemohteadt ut onkâompamukquodtut.
17.13 Omkish woi Jehovah wuttameh n[]noh, penuhteash, pohquohwhin nukketeahogkou wutch matchetowog, neg kuttogkodtegannog.
17.14 Wutch wosketompaog kenutcheganog woi Jehovah, wutch wosketompaog yeu muttaohket, nag wuttahtauongan8 yeuut keteaonganit: kah kenumwóhtinash wunnogkusséont kutadtahtouongash nag numwápuohwunneechánowoh, chaubohkish um̃[?]úmachiyeumoash wunnukkodtumaooh uppeissesimo[?]oh.
17.15 Qut neen, pish nunnaum kuskesuk ut wunnomwausseonganit: pish numm8chekohtóh, t8keon, nussean neánussean.
18.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk muttinneu Jehovah} David, {kenoonau Jehovah yeush ketoohomae kuttoo[m]ongash, nekesukok Jehovah wame pohquohwhunont, wutch wunnutcheganooont matwomoh, kah wutch w[u]nnutcheganit Saul, kah noowau}.
18.1 K8womonsh woi Jehovah nummenuhkesuonk.
18.2 Jehovah nukqussukquánum, kah n8wonkônous, nuppohquohwussuaenum, num-Manitt8m, nukqussukquanum noh paubuhtanumog nutonk8ohqoss8, kah askon wadchanukqueh, kah nukqunohque wonkônous.
18.3 N8weequetumau Jehovah tapenuk tabuttantamauónat: nemehkuh woh nuppohquohwhunit wutch nummatwomut.
18.4 Nupp8wonk wutonkquomomhuaongah n8wéinuhkongqunash: wuttomogka[n]8m8 matta peantam8gig n8wabuwunukquog.
18.5 Wutonkquomomhúaongash chepiohkomuk nukquinupuhkongqunash: wutahpehunah nupp8onk nukoshkóme tohqunukquog.
18.6 Onkupinnaon n8weehquetumau Jehovah, nummaúonitteau num-Manitt8m, n8tamup n8wadtauatongqussuonk wutch wuttempleumut, nummauonk peyaum8 anaquabit, en wohtaúogut.
18.7 Neit ohke nukkeem8 kah quéquan: onk agwu ohtagish wadchuash ontahtaash, kah nukkem8ash newutche musquantamup.
18.8 Sohweem8 pukit wutch wutchonit, kah n8tau wutch wutt8nut unnunau, mohkohsaash ne nashpe chikohtaash.
18.9 Quanábuhkam kesuk, kah n8keu, kah pohkenái ut agwu wusseetit.
18.10 Kah nayeumugk cherub, kah pt8wu: nux, pt8wu wutch wuñuppawhuno[h] waban.
18.11 Pohkinteau wutassampamugquodt8m: week wueenuhkunk, pohkinnuppog, kuhpógke matohqs póhkahqut.
18.12 Kodshaumwushont ut anaquabit, kuppogki matokqs pamém8, mussegan kah n8tae mohkohsaash.
18.13 Kah Jehovah padtaquóhhunnéhtea[n] ut kesukqut, kah nôahpit wuttauatonkquísu, mussegon kah n8tae mohkohsaash.
18.14 Nux, pummu ukkôunkquodtah, kah wusseauhkonuh nahoh, kah pepummu ukkutshánum, kah wutomskauoh.
18.15 Neit passéhtannash nippekontu nógquadtash, kah muttaohke quenohtagish puhkônumunash, aushkòáan, woi Jehovah, kutchân nashaum8ug.
18.16 An8team8 wutch wohqudt, nunneemunuk: nukkuhpunuk wutch nippekontu missi.
18.17 Nuppohquohwhunuk wutch menuhkesu nummatwom, kah wutch nag sekenáitcheg: newutche nag [á]nue menuhkesuog onk neen.
18.18 Nukkinhomunkquog onkapunnáon: qut Jehovah nuttannumunkou.
18.19 Onk nussohh8wunuk en mummishke ayeuonganit: nuppohquohwhunuk, newutche n8weeteánumuk.
18.20 Jehovah nutunkquatunk neaunag n8nomwausseonk: neane pohkág nunnutcheganash nuttinunkquatunkqun.
18.21 Newutche nussampwushám ummayash Jehovah, kah matta nummatcheseáeu nutámaéhtâóh wutch num-Manitt8mut.
18.22 Newutche wame 8sittam8ongash ohtaash anaquabeh: kah matta nuppogketam8h ukkuhk8waongash.
18.23 Neen wonk nussampwes ut anaquabit: kah n8wadchan nuhhog wutch nehenwonche nummatcheseongash.
18.24 Yowutche Jehovah nutunkquatunk neane n8nomwausseonk, neane pohkág nunnutcheganash ut anaquabit.
18.25 Monaneteáhettit, kummonânumóog: sampwésit, kah ken kussampwes.
18.26 Pahkezhettit, kah ken kuppahkes: kah chenouaushettit nánuk kuchénoaus.
18.27 Newutche k8wadchan kuttamunge onkapunácheg missinninnuog, qut kuppenuhteam pahtuánummonugqussitcheg.
18.28 Newutche ken kenashqussum n8weequanánteg: Jehovah num-Manitt8m wequanantam nuppohkená8m.
18.29 Newutche nashpe ken nuppanupwusham, chppan8og, kah nashpe num-Manitt8m nukqueishontam pummeneutunk.
18.30 Qut Jehovah ummay pannuppu wunnegen: wuttinn8waonk God pahketeáuun: wuttonkk8woquoss8unn8wôh neg wame pabuhtanumoncheg.
18.31 Newutche howan Manitt8it webe Jehovah, kah howan quasukquânuit webe num-Manitt8m.
18.32 God nupputtukquábunuk menuhkesuonk, kah uppahketeoun nummay.
18.33 Nusseetash ogquéhteau ahtúhqusseetit, kah nuppónuk nukkussôhkôóoumut.
18.34 Kuhk8tomauau nunnutcheganoh ayeuhkonat: nemehkuh nashpe nuhpin pôhqunau mooshagquohtomp.
18.35 Kah wonk kittinnumaiip k8wadchanuáe ogqunneg kah kuttinnohkou nutashinuk, kah kummanunnissuonk nummishúkqun.
18.36 Kummissigskéhteau nuttóntahnehtuonganash ut agwu neen, onkummat nutt8nukqussin8h.
18.37 N8nômahtúhkôomp nummatwóog, kah nummátamóog, onk matta wonk nukqushk8h nô pajeh nuppaguanónat.
18.38 Nutchadchéuhtahwhóog onk ummatta tapenumóog ompken, penusháog ut nusseetit.
18.39 Newutche kupputtukquôbussup kummenuhkesuonk ayeuwuttinneat: kenáuwôsikkómpaihéaog yeug neepaiitunkqueaneg.
18.40 Wonk kittinninnumah wussittippukánoóash nummatwomog: onk woh nuppaguanóog sekeneáitcheg.
18.41 Mauwog, matta howan uppohquohwhunoh: nux, Jehovah[]ut, qut matta wunnamp8hamaúoh nahog.
18.42 Neit nussukquttahwhôog onatuh puppissai toht8anontog: nussohwhôkonunk onatuh pusseog mayut.
18.43 Kuppohquohwussup ummusquánitteaonganóont missinninnúog, kah kutayeuweh 8puhkúhqunneaóont penuwohteaog: missinninnúog matta wahhéaogig, pish n8wówussumukquog.
18.44 Quéna n8taehettit, pish nosweetunkquog, penuohteáog pish n8wonkkumukquog.
18.45 Penuwohteaog pish mahchéog, pish wabesuog ut assompamukquodtit.
18.46 Jehovah pomantam, kah 8nantaj nukqussukquánum: kah wadchán8wáe num-Manitt8m mishehhenaj.
18.47 N noh God an8tauanshikqueh, kah naôhsikómpaaiheunk missinninnúh ut agwu neen.
18.48 Nuppohquohwhunuk wutch nummatwâut: nux, kutahshineh waabe yeug neepaiittunkqueaneg; kuppohquohwussup wutch musquantamuoenúut.
18.49 Newutche kuttabuttantamoush, woi Jehovah, kenugku penuwohteáog, kah nukket8homom tabuttantam8wonganash ut k8wesuwonganit.
18.50 Missiyeuash uppohquohwussuáonkanash wuttinumaon ukketass8tomómoh: kah ummonánumoh saséqunoncheh, Davidoh, kah wuskannemunneoh micheme.
19.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt: Ukketoohhomaonk} David.
19.1 Kesukquash wunnáhtuhkóneau wussohsumóonk God, kah mamachekesuk kuhk8tomuhteaum8 wunnetchegane anakausuonk.
19.2 Hóhsekôeu kesukodash keket8hkon: kah hóhsekôeu nukonash náhteteauog wahteauonk.
19.3 Wanne unnónt8wáonkanunn8 asa mat pen8wont8waonkanunn8; adt mo n8tamómuk ukkutt8wongan8.
19.4 Uppemunneohtón8 pannu[p]shaum8 wame ohket, kah ukkutt8wongan88ash aongkoue muttaok: na upponamun wetu wutch nepâuzoh.
19.5 N noh onatuh weseentamwaen sohhog wutch weetu: kah weekontam onatuh menuhkesuwen, nanôahteadt.
19.6 Ummoncheonk[]au weekqshik kesuk, kah uppogkudtuhkomóonk na weekqshik: kah wanne teag asómpamukquodtino8 woh mo kôssopitán8g.
19.7 Wuttinnaumatuonk Jehovah pannuppu wunnetuoh, quanuppinónt keteahogkôunoh, 8wauwáonk Jehovah wunnamuhkuteyeú8, waantamwehheunt as8tuoh.
19.8 Ukkúhkwa8onganash Jehovah sampao[ù]ash, weekontamwahteunk metah: wutan8hteam8wonk Jehovah pohkoi, wôshwunnum8m8ug muskesukquash.
19.9 Qusháonk Jehovah pohkoi, machemohtag: 8sittum8ongash Jehovah wunnamuhkutêyeu8ash, kah wame sampweyeu8ash moáeu.
19.10 M8cheke kodtantamunash onk ne gold, nux, onk ne m8cheke wanegik gold: onk ánue weekon onk ne hony, kah honycombe.
19.11 Kah wonk amômáog kittinninnúmoh: kah usséog nishog, missi kutongquatunkanun.
19.12 Howan 8wahteoúnash uppéhchummaauongash? pahkhe wutch kéme matcheseongash.
19.13 Wonk assón kittinneum wutch mat qushe matcheseongash, ahque piahtimehhettich: neit woh nussumpwes, kah numm8ses wutch mishe matcheseonk.
19.14 Nukkutt8wonganash wutch nutt8nut, káh nunnatwontam8wongash ut nuttahhut, tapeneaúmunach ut anaquabean, woi Jehovah, nukqussukquanum, kah nuppohquohwussuaénin.
20.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt: Ukket[oo]khomaonk} David.
20.1 NOOtunkquash Jehovah wuttammepunnáan: 8wesuonk um-Manitt8moh Jakob wadchanukqush.
20.2 An8nonch aninnummoadtuonguh wutch peantamwakomukqut: kah menuhkhukqush wutch Sion.
20.3 Mehquantaj wame kummag8onkanash: tapeneaj chikohtáeu sephauseongash. Selah.
20.4 Uninnumungqush neane kodtantog kuttah: kah wame n naj kukkinn8s8waongash.
20.5 N8wekontamumun k8adchan8onganit, kah 8wesuonganit num-Manitt8mun nupponamunnan nummuttáagunun: Jehovah ussitch wame kuppeantam8wonganash.
20.6 Yeuyeu n8wahteóun, Jehovah wadchanau sasequnutche, wunn8taoh wutch 8netupanatamwe kesukqui8mut nashpe k8wadchán8wáe kuttinohkóunne menuhkesuonk.
20.7 Nawhutch pabahtánittamwog chariotsash, nawhutch horsesoh: qut nummequontamumun 8wesuonk Jehovah num-Manitt8m.
20.8 N8keahheóog kah penusháog: qut nutomohkémun kah nussampokompaúun.
20.9 Wadchanean Jehovah, ketass8t n8tunkqutteuh weekquetumáogkut.
21.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt, ukketoohhomaonk} David.
21.1 Ketass8t muskouantam ut kummenuhkesuonganit, woi Jehovah: kah k8wadchan8wonganit, woi Jehovah: kah k8wadchan8wonganit ut toh nukkukqun ummuskouanatam8wonk?
21.2 Kuttinnumauop neane kodtantamunit wuttahhoh, kah matta kukkogkaanumaoun nohhan wehquetumunkqueanish wussisset8nit. Selah.
21.3 Newutche aspapeantamungk8up kuttinnumau wunnaiyeue k8naneteaonk, kupponumau pahke gold chetuhquab uppuhkuhqut.
21.4 K8wehquetumunk keteaonk,, kah kittinnumauau sepepomantamowonk micheme kah micheme.
21.5 Wussohsumowonk missi ut k8wadchanitteaonganit, quttianittuonk kah wohquanittuonk kupponamau.
21.6 Newutche kutayimau m8cheke wunanumaonk micheme: kuttinsuonk ummuskouanatamheuh m8cheke.
21.7 Newutche ketass8t pabahtanumau Jehovah, kah kesukqut apit monanumont, matta pish ontsappeoh.
21.8 Kenutcheg pish namehheau wame kummatwomoh: kuttinohkou pish namehheau yeug sekeneanukqueaneg.
21.9 Pish kutayeu8g onatuh kesomsquttag musquanumadt naghog: Jehovah pish ummishashqunneuh musquantog, kah pish mahchekussuog nashpe n8teau.
21.10 Wutontsetuongan8 pish kuppagquodtoh wutch ohket, kah 8skannemunnoh wutch kenugke wosketompaog wunnaumonaout.
21.11 Newutche kukkodmatchenehukquog: natwontamwog missi matchenehhuwaonk, ne mat tapenumunhetteg ussen.
21.12 Yowutche pish anummekompoog: quoshonkqunnumauadt nagoh ut wushkesukkouwout
21.13 Mishehhenunaj Jehovah, nehenwonche kumenuhkesuonkanit: nemehkuh nukket8hhomomun, kah n8wawussittumun kummenuhkesuonk.
22.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Ajeleth Shaharukketoohhomaonk} David.
22.1 Nummanitt8m num-Manitt8m, tohwutch ahquanumean tohwutch nau8ssuhkáuwean wutch kuttannumiyeuonk: wutch nummaue kutt8wonganash.
22.2 Woi num-Manitt8m kesukodtae nanompanwam, qut matta ken8tiyeuh, kah nukkonaeu, kah matta nutchequnappu.
22.3 Qut k8neetupanatam, woi ken wadohtean wutabuttantam̃8ongan8out Israel
22.4 N8shunnonog kuppabahtanumukquog: kuppabahtanumukquog, onk kuppohquohhunnopanneg.
22.5 Kummauunnitteonkapanneg, onk kuppohquohwhunopanneg, kuppabahtanumukquog, kah matta akodchuog.
22.6 Qut neen ask8k kah mat n8wosketompóou; nukkekomukquog wosketompaog, kah nummishananumukquog missinninnuog.
22.7 Wame neg náaitcheg nutâhanetunkquog, mamuskéog, nunnukukquoshôog n8waog.
22.8 Pabahtánumop Jehovah, woh uppohquohwhunnuh: pohquohwhunonch, tapeneaúont.
22.9 Qut len neemunnéap wutch ôontomuk kutáyimaiup ánoósuonk n8nont ut wussogkodtunganit nokas.
22.10 Kuppadchippuhhouwónup wutch ôontomuk, ken num-Manitt8m wutch nokas wunnogkussit.
22.11 Ahque nô8sukah, newutche wuttammepunnáonk paswohteau: newutche wanne howan nuttannumungkou.
22.12 Monáog bulsog n8weenuhkongquog menuhkesuog Bashane bulsog n8weenuhkongquog
22.13 Nuttôunnehtongquog onatuh qunnônou m8hm8skupwit, kah neeneehteadt.
22.14 Nussókem onatuh nippeh, kah wame nuskonash n8hn8htahshineash: nuttah onatuh wasôbôhteau ut nôeu nunnogkussit.
22.15 Nummenuhkesuonk nunnohteau ónatuh kodchuhkwishquadt, kah neenan pissogquem8 nutó[m]peuhkô[n]it, onk kuppás8weh uppuppissaiyeumut nupp8wonk.
22.16 Newutche anumwog n8weenuhkunk: matchetowog ummukkinneongan8 n8weenuhkongquog, kanittequómwog nunautcheash kah nusseetash.
22.17 Woh nutapogkétam wame nuskonash: nukkehkinneungquog, kah nummosompámukquog.
22.18 Chadchapenumoadtuog nuthogk8unash, kah tanahtóadtuog nuppetashqushaonk.
22.19 Qut ahque nô8sukah woi Jehovah, woi nummenuhkesuonk teanuk aninnumah!
22.20 Pohquahwhas nukketeahogkou wutch togkodteganit: nunnegonn8womoneg wutch ummenuhkesuonganit anum.
22.21 Pohquohwusseh wutch qunonou wutt8nut: newutche ken8taup wutch wutaskonat nequtyeuun.
22.22 Nukkuhk8tomau neematog k8wesuonk: ut noeu mukkinneonganit kuttabuttantamoush.
22.23 Kenaa[n] quoshogish Jehovah, tabuttantam8k: wame kenaau wuskannemu[n]neoh Jakob sohsum8on8k kah qush8k wame kenaau 8skannemunneoh Israel.
22.24 Newutche matta wutchadchepantam8un asa wutjishontam8un wuttammepunaonk wuttammepunahettit: asa matta puttoghom8 wuskesuk noh whutch, qut mau[n]nitteaonk wu[u]n8taoh.
22.25 Nuttabuttantam8onk pish papaume ken ut mishemukkinneonganit, pish nuttussen nukquoshaumuwaongash anaquabhettit nag qushoncheg.
22.26 Manunnissuog pish meetsuog kah tabep8og: nag tabuttantamauaog Jehovah, nag natinnewhoncheg, kuttahh8oash micheme pomantam8ash.
22.27 Wame aongkoue muttaôhket pish mehquoantamwog, kah quinnuppeôg en Jehovah[]ut: kah wame unnauadtuongash wuttahtimoneat pish wowussummuwaog ut anaquabean.
22.28 Newutche ketass8tamowônk wuttaihe Jehovah: kah nagum nanaunnuwaenin kenugke wutahtimoneash.
22.29 Wame wónogqutcheg ohket pish meetsuog, kah waussumóog: wame aoncheg puppissiyeuut pish nauwaeog ut anaquabit, kah matta woh howan pomantamwaheoou, nehenwonche ukketeahogkouunuh.
22.30 Wuskannemunwog 8wowussumouh, ne pish ogquontamun ut Jéhovah newutche pometeunk.
22.31 Nag pish peyauog, kah pish wahteauwahuwaog wussampweusseonk missinninnuh nag woh nekitcheg, yeuoh yeu mahche ussit.
23.0 {Ukketohhhomáonk} David.
23.1 Jehovah nussohkomm8nuk8waeneum, wanne teag woh nukquenaahik8.
23.2 Nuseepsumwahik ashkoskuhkontu nutass8wunuk ahtou pagodtut.
23.3 Wonk omohkinau nukketeahogkounoh nutuss8wunuk wunnomwausseongane mayut newutche 8wesu[ó]nk.
23.4 Nux, pumusháon wutonkauhtómut 8náunkôáe nupp8onk, matta woh nukquehtam8 woskehittúonk: newutche k8weetomeh, kuppogkomunk, kah kutanwôhhou n8nenehukquog.
23.5 K8nech8hkah ut anaquabeh, anaquabhettit nummatwomog: kussisséqunum nuppuhkuh nashpe pummee, n8tattámwáitch pomponeetupóhshau.
23.6 Wunnamuhkut 8náyeuonk kah monaneteaonk pish nutásukkonkqúnash tohsohkepomantam: kah pish nutta[i]h weekit Jehovah micheme.
24.0 {Ukketohhomaonk} David.
24.1 Ohke wuttaihe Jehovah, kah neadtahshimméchimik: muttaok kah neg na wa[d]ohkitcheg.
24.2 Newutche ukquenuhtauunah kehtahhannit, kah umménuhkehtin woskeche sepuut.
24.3 Howan kóhkuhquidt 8wadchúmut Jehovah? kah howan neepau ut 8netupanatamwe ayeuonganit?
24.4 N$noh po[h]pohkenutchont, kah pahketeahont, noh matta tohshinunk ukketeahogkonuh tahn8che, matta as8kekodteaumowu chadchekeyeuog.
24.5 Noh pish attumunum 8nanetuonk wutch Jehovah, & wunnomwausseonk wutch 8wadchanuáe Manitt8mut.
24.6 Yeu pometeongan8 nag natinneawhoncheg, nátinneahogig kuskesuk, woi Jakob. Selah.
24.7 Tahshinum8k kuppuhkuk88ash, woi kenaau squontamog: tahshinnutteagk micheme squontamog, kah sohsumóe ketass8t pish petutteau.
24.8 Howan sohsumóe ketass8t? Jehovah menuhkesu kah mishimmenuhkesu, Jehovah menuhkesu ayeúwuttuonganit.
24.9 Tohshinum8k kuppuhkuk88ash, woi kenaau squontamog: kah tohsheg michemohtáe squontamog, kah sohsumóe ketass8t, pish petutteau.
24.10 Howan sohsumóe ketass8t? Jehovah wutayeuwehteomuh, n noh sohsumóe ketass8t. Selah.
25.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
25.1 Kutahshinnumaush, woi Jehovah, nukketeahogkou.
25.2 Woi num-Manitt8m, kuppabuhtanumoush, ahque akodchitti, nummatwomog ahque wunnantamm8wôshéttich.
25.3 Nux, ahque akodjhettich nag anoónukqueáneg: nag akodjhettich tahn8che matchesecheg.
25.4 Kah nahtusseh kummayash, woi Jehovah, kuhk8tomah kuttáongash,
25.5 Sagkompaguneh en k8nomwaonganit, kah kuhk8tomah: newutche ken n8wadchánitteáe Manit, ken kutânóonsh qunni kesuk.
25.6 Mehquoantash, woi Jehovah, k8womoausuwáe kitteamonteaneteaongash: kah womoausuwáe k8nesuongash, newutche nôadt unniyeupash.
25.7 Ahque mehquontash nummatcheseonganash waskénuean, asa nuppanneseonganash: neaunag kummonaneteaonganash ne nummequanumeh, newutche k8neseonk, woi Jehovah.
25.8 Wunneetou, kah sampwésu Jehovah: yowutche kuhk8tomauau matcheseaenùh en mayut.
25.9 Samp8wunnau má[n]unnissuoh en wussittum8wonganit: kah kuhk8tomauau mánunnissuoh en ummayut.
25.10 Wame ummayash Jehovah monaneteaonganú8ash kah wunnomwaonganú8ash: nah nanaihteánutche 8n8waonk kah 8wauwaongash.
25.11 Newutche k8wesuonk, woi Jehovah, ahquoantamah nummatcheseonk, newutche missi.
25.12 Howan noh quoshont Jehovah? woh ukkuhk8tomauoh én mayut uttiyeu pepénog.
25.13 Ukketeahogkôunoh pish ayeuoh wunáyeuonganit: kah 8skannemuneoh pish wutahtaunin ohke.
25.14 Jehovah ukkemeseongash 8wahteauwun[á]oash nag quoshoncheg: kah pish wunnahtinoh wunn8waonk.
25.15 Nuskesukquash nagwutteáeu unnogque Jehovahut: newutche pish kôdtinnum nusseetash wutch hashabpit.
25.16 Qunnupish en nuhhogkáeiyeu, & monanumeh: newutche nonsiyeu & n8tamehpunám.
25.17 OOtaméhpunaongash nuttah mogkiyeuash: woi sohh8wunneh wutch nánakompanaonganit.
25.18 Móninneash nutonkapunaonk, kah nutonkquomom8wonk: onk ahquoantamah wame nummatcheseonganash.
25.19 Natwánum nummatwômog newutch m8naog: kah nag nutjishanumukquog nashpe mishe jishánittuonk.
25.20 Woin nanâih nukketeahogkou, kah pohquahwusseh, ahque akodchitti newutche kuppabatanumoush.
25.21 Pannuppu wunneetowonk, kah sampweseo[n]k wadchanhettich: newutche kuttannóonsh.
25.22 Pohquahwhus Israel, woi God, wutche wame 8tamehpunnaongan88ash.
26.0 {Ukketoohhomaonk} David.
26.1 Wussumeh, woi Jehovah, newutche nuppompomusham ut nuppannuppe wunneetowonganit: kah nuppabuhtanum Jehovah, newutche matta woh nutt8nequssin8h.
26.2 Nat8tomah, woi Jehovah, kah qutcheheh, qutcheh nutt8unnussog, kah nuttah.
26.3 Newutche k8womoausuonk anaquabe, kah nuppompomushap k8nomwayeuonganit.
26.4 Matta n8weetapemo tahn8cheyeuwutcheg, asa matta pish nuppetukauóog eiantukeiyeuog.
26.5 Nussekenam ummukkinneongan8 matchesecheg: kah matta n8weetappem8 matcheetowog.
26.6 Nukkutshitto nunnutchegash en pahketeahónat: nemehkuh nukquinnuppuhkom kut-Altar8m, woi Jehovah.
26.7 Onk woh n8wahshadtóh nashpe wuttanatongqussue tabuttantamóonk, onk woh nussinneash wame kummonchanatamwe anakausuongash.
26.8 Jehovah n8womantam ayinneat keekit: kah ayeuonk uttoh ohtag kukquttianumutteaonk.
26.9 Ahque mukkin nukketeahogkou kenugku matcheseaenúut, asa nukkuteaonk kenugku shehteaenúut.
26.10 Wunnutchegan88ash woskêhuwóm8ash, kah wuttinnohkôunn8 numwohteau matcheseonkquatunkash.
26.11 Qut neen nuppompomusham nuppannuppu wunneetuwonganit, pohquohwhunch kah monanumeh.
26.12 Nusset ohteau m8saiyeuut, mukkinneonganit nuttabuttantamau Jehovah.
27.0 {Ukketoohhomaonk} David.
27.1 Jehovah n8wequá8m, kah n8wadchanitteaonk, howan quóshog?
27.2 Matchetowog nummatwomog kah ayeuuhkausitcheg nohkuhkoihettit en meechinat n8weyaus, togkussittassunwóg kah mishnkoúushsinwog.
27.3 Tohkônogque ayeuhteaog waéenuhki[e]hettit, nuttah matta wabesu: tohkônogque ayeuwuttuonk waabehtúnkquea[n], neit pish n8t8anatam.
27.4 Pasuk nukkodtanatamau Jehovah, ne nunnatinnehamun: onk woh nuttai weekit Jehovah tosohkepomantam, naumunat 8nesuonk Jehovah, kah nuppeantamunat ut wut[-]templeumut.
27.5 Newutche wuttammepunnáon, pish nutáudtashuk ut weekit, ut asampâmukquodtut uppeantamwakomukqut, pish nutadtashúk, pish nukquenashhuk qussukquanit.
27.6 Onk yeuyeu nuppuhkuk tahshém8 ánue nummatwomog qunnuppekoihettit: newutche nuttininnumau ut weekit weekontamóe sephausuongash, nukket8hhomo[m], nux nuttinn8homom tabuttantam8wongash Jehovahut.
27.7 N8tah Jehovah mauunnitteauunon nashpe n8wadtauatongqussuonk: onk monánumeh, kah namp8hamah.
27.8 N8waan natinneham8k nuskesuk, nuttah kuttinuk kuskesuk, woi Jehovah, nunnadtinneóhham.
27.9 Ahque puttogwhush kuskesuk ut nóadtit wutche nen ahque kuttinninneum musquanittamwe pogkes: kuttannumaiip, a[h]que nukkósseh, asa ohqu[ȧ]numeh, woi n8wadchanitteae Manit.
27.10 N8sh kah nokas ahquánuméhettit: neit Jehovah nunneemunuk.
27.11 Kuhk8tomash kummay, woi Jehovah: kah uss8wusseh m8siyeuut may, newutche nummatwomog.
27.12 Ahque aninnaumau nuhhog ut wuttenantam8ongan8óut nummatwomog: newutche pann8wáe wauwacheg n8waábetunkquog, kah neg nashontogig woskehuwaonk.
27.13 Woh nussauunumup, matta wunnamptam8wóus, woh nunnaumunat 8neséonk Jehovah kenugku neg pamontogig.
27.14 Annoôs Jehovah, wutt8ántash, onk pish menuhkitteau kuttah: annoôs nussim Jehovah.
28.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
28.1 Kummauunnitteaush, woi Jehovah, nukqussukquanum, ahque cheequnappehtah, iskont chequnapehtiyean, woh nutogqunneunkqus neg womussitcheg en passohtheganit.
28.2 N8tash n8wadtauatonkqussue peantamoongash, mauunnitteaunnon, spunnumon nunnutchegash ennogqueu wunneétupanatamwu kut-orackleumut.
28.3 Ahque s8wusseh matcheetowehtu, kah k8wutche anakausitcheg matcheseonk nnag manunne ken8nahettit weetatteamungan8oh, qut woskehuwaonk wuttahh8wout.
28.4 Aninnumau naghog neaunag wutanakausuongan8oash, kah neaunag wutussenitteaongan8oash: aninnumau naghog neaunag wunnutcheganne anakausuongan8oash aninnumau naghog wutonkatongan8oash.
28.5 Newutche wanne tohhentupantamoog wutanakausuong[á]nash God, asa wunnutchegane kesteauongash, pish uppaguanuh kah matta pish 8wekuhkonuh.
28.6 Tabuttantamauunach Jehovah, newutche n8tam n8wadtau[a]tonkqussuonkane peantamoonk.
28.7 Jehovah nummenuhkesuonk, kah nuttogqunneg nuttah uppabuhtanumopuh, kah nuttánumungkup: newutche nuttah misheweekontam, kah nashpe nukke8hhamaonk nuttabuttantamau:
28.8 Jehovah ummenuhkesuwonganouh: & sasequnonche8 wadchanuwae menuhkesuonk.
28.9 Woi wadcha[n] kummissinninnumog, kah wunnantash kutahtoonk: sohkom8us wonk kah tahshin micheme.
29.0 {Ukket8homaonk} David.
29.1 Aninnumok Jehovah, (woi magass8tamogish) aninnumok Jehovah sohsumoonk kah menuhkesuonk.
29.2 Aninnumok Jehovah ne wussohsumoonk neaunag 8wesuonk: woussum8k Jehovah ut wussohsum8ongane wunneetupanatamwé weekit.
29.3 OOwadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah ohteau woskeche nippekontu: wussohsumoe God padaquohha[n]u8: Jehovah woskeche mishinnippekontu.
29.4 OOwadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah menuhkoi, 8wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah numwahteau wohquanittuonk.
29.5 OOwadtauatongqussuonk Jehovah pokshanau chikkuppemusse, nux Jehovah pokshadtou utchikkuppemussee ut Lebanon.
29.6 Onk wutayimunash quequeshaut onatuh cowashinuemesit: Lebanon, kah Syrion onatuh wushkoshimwemesu nequtyeuun.
29.7 Wadtauatonkqussuonk Jehovah, chadchápenum n8n8náeu n8htau.
29.8 OOwadtauatongqussuonk Jehovah ayeúau wunnechonaóont ahtuhquog: kah 8wôshwunoh ut touohkomuk, kah ut weekit nish noh pasuk unn8wau wussohsumowonk.
29.9 OOwadtauatongqussuonk Jehovah ayeúau wunnechonaóont ahtuhquog: kah 8wôshwunoh ut touohkomuk, kah ut weekit nish noh pasuk unn8wau wussohsumowonk.
29.10 Jehovah appu tomogkonehtu: nux, Jehovah michemappu ketass8t.
29.11 Jehovah aninnumauau menuhkesuonk ummissinninneumoh: Jehovah 8nanum[à]u ummissinninneumoh nashpe wunohteaonk.
30.0 {Ketoohhoma<e>nk, kah unno[o]hhomaonk} David, {anumaont week Goduh.}
30.1 Kutashinush, woi Jehovah, newutche kutashinip: kah matta kuttinánumop nummatwomog nutahánetunkqunnaóut.
30.2 Woi Jehovah num-Manitt8m, kummauunnitteánup, kah kenetskeheup.
30.3 Woi Jehovah, kutashin nukketeahogkou wutch weenohkeet: kuppompomantamwáheh, woh mat nuttónat weenohket.
30.4 Ket8homók Jehovah (woi kenaau 8neetupanatam8moh) kah tabuttantam8k, mehquantamóg 8neetupanatam8onk.
30.5 Newutche ummusquantam8onk tiohqui: kitteamonteanumugquéog ne keteaonk: woh kummau pasuk nukon, qut nompoáeu pish k8weekontam.
30.6 Kah wânáéon, nussip, matta pish nummicheme ontsappu.
30.7 Jehovah newutche kitteamonteanumeup, kummenuhkehteóh n8wadchúm, kupputtagkuhhumup kuskesuk neit n8tamehpunap.
30.8 Kummauunnitteánup, woi Jehovah: kah nuppeantamauop Jehovah.
30.9 Toh kittinanúhhumont wutche n8sqhéonk posekinimuk: sun woh puppissai k8waeenomuk? sun woh kuhk8tomuhtean k8nomwausseonk.
30.10 N8tah Jehovah, kah monánumeh, Jehovah aninnumah.
30.11 Kukquinnuppinnum[á]h nummauonk en pummukkônat: kutamaunumaiip nummauongane hogk8onk, kah kupputtukquóbsip m[s]koúanatam8ónk.
30.12 Onk woh nussohsumóonk k8waeenomuk, kah woh matta nutchequnappu, woi Jehovah num-Manitt8m kuttabuttantamoush micheme.
31.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt: Ukketoohhomaonk} David.
31.1 Ken, woi Jehovah, kuppabuhtanumóush, ahque akodchitti: pohquahwusseh en k8nomwausseonganit.
31.2 Ehquóhtuhquaehtuh, teanuk pohquohwusseh: ken menuhkaj nukqussukquanum, wutch nutushpuhh8wae-komuk n8wadchanukqunat.
31.3 Newutche ken nukqussukquanum, kah n8wonkónous: newajeh, newutche k8wesuonk sagkompáneh, kah sampwusháseh.
31.4 Kodtinneh na wutch hashabput uttoh ponamihetticheh kemeu, newutche ken nummenuhkesuonk.
31.5 Ut kenutcheganit kutahtôhshinun nunnashauonk: kuppohquáwussip, woi Jehovah, wunnomwáe God.
31.6 Nussekeneauóog n nag wadt8wóntogig tahn8che pann8wáyeuonk: qut nuppábahtanum Jehovah.
31.7 N8weekontam kah nummuskouantam ut kummonaneteaonganit: newutche kenatwontamup n8tamehpunáonk: k8waheomp nukketeahogkou wadtamehpunáon.
31.8 Kah matta kukkuppuhh[ú]h en wunnutcheganit matwau: kupponum nussetash papahchiyeuut.
31.9 Monanumeh, woi Jehovah, newutche n8tamehpunam: nuskesuk mohtupaémo nashpe neuantam8wonk: nux, nukketeahogkou, kah nunnogkus.
31.10 Newutche nukketeáonk sánum88 wutch neuanatam8wonk, kah nukkodtum8mash nashpe mishánum8onk: nummenuhkesuonk sánum8m8 newutche nummatcheseongash, kah nuskonash mohtupaémoash.
31.11 Nummamântunkuppanneg wame nummatwomog: qut nâhnâunne neetatteamunganog: kah netompaog nukqushukkuppanneg: nahetticheh ut poquadchik n8sémoteunkquog.
31.12 N8wanánumukquog onatuh nánupuk wanánumit, nutogquñeukqus sukwiwshquadt.
31.13 Newutche n8tamau monaog nukkekômukquog, wabesuonk quaquinnuppe ohteau: kân8nittehettit moáe ayeuuhkóne neen, nukkodnushúkqunnaóont.
31.14 Qut kuppabahtanumunup, woi Jehovah, nussip, ken num-Manitt8m.
31.15 Nutaquompayeumash kenutcheganit: pohquahwusseh wutch wunnutcheganóut nummatwomog, kah nag wutch woskhukqueaneg.
31.16 Kuskesuk wôssumwahteauush kittinnumoh, wadcháneh newutch kummonaneteaonk.
31.17 Ahque akodchitti, woi Jehovah, newutche kuppeantamonsh, matcheetowog akodjhettich: kah neetoshuáhettich ut weenohkeet.
31.18 Pann8waeu mussissitt8nash neetashum8utch: uttiyeush matcheyeum8ugish, p[o]htuánumweyeum8ugish mama[n]aantamwu yeum8ugish wunnomwaussenutcheh.
31.19 Woi uttoh nukkukqun k8neet8onk nish wadchanumauadcheh neg quashukk8unneg, neananakausuwéhtauasit neg pabahtanumugqueaneg, ut anaquabhettit wosketompaog[]wunnaumonaoh.
31.20 Nag kutadtashôog wutch uppéhtuánum8ongan8 wosketompaog, asampamukquodtit ut anaquabean: nag kemu k8wadchanôog ut asampamukquodtut wutch meenanúe penuanittuonk.
31.21 Wun[á]numunaj Jehovah, newutche [n]ahtinuk monchanatamwu 8womoausuonk, ut menuhke otánit.
31.22 Newutche nussip wadtamanatamon, nuttumuttahwhut wutch anaquabean: qut ken8tamup n8wadtauatongqussúe kenanampassumunowonk, máunnitteáuunon.
31.23 Woi womónok Jehovah, wame kenaau 8neetupanatam8moh, newutche Jehovah wadchanau pabahchuussenutcheh: kah mishongquttauoh pohtuanumwesenutcheh.
31.24 Wutt8anatam8k, onk menuhketeaou kuttahhou, wame kenaau ánoânogish Jehovah.
32.0 {Ukketoohhomaonk} David, {Maschil}.
32.1 Wunnanumau noh ummatcheseonk ahquoantamanut, kah ummatcheseonk padtagkuhwhôsik.
32.2 OOnanumau missinnin, Jehovah matta ogquanumunk ummatcheseonk: kah wuttah ut wanne as8kekodteaum8onk.
32.3 Matta kodt8on, nuskonash nukkônekônú8ash, newutche nummauonk quinnikesuk.
32.4 Newutche kesukodtáeu kah nukkonáeu kenutcheg nuttuhk[é]k8[k]ongqun, nutogkuskesuonk óhs8wem8 en neepune kunkanit. Selah.
32.5 Kussamp8wontamauunup nummatcheseonk, kah matta nupputtoguhhum8h nummatcheseonk: nussip, nussamp8am nummatcheseongash Jehovahut, neit kutahquoantamaiip nishkeneungque nummatcheseonk. Selah.
32.6 Newútche yeu, nish noh wunneetupanatamwenin pish kuppeantamunk, uttoh woh adt8che namehhikquean: wunnamuhkut mishittomogkog, matta pish uppas8sukauouh nnah.
32.7 Ken nutassampamukquodt8m, pish k8wadchâneh wutch wuttamehpunonat: pish kukquinnupohtah pohquawunnitue ket8homaonash. Selah.
32.8 Kukkuhk8tomoush, kah kenatinush may ut toh woh aôan: nuskesuk pish kussampshanuk.
32.9 Ahque ohqueneunkussek horsesut, asa muleuut, matta waahtam8g: uttiyeu mós wutt8nut kashpussik nashpe bridle-bit, ishkont kuppas8sukkongquog.
32.10 M8cheke pish onkapunn8og matcheetowog, qut n noh pabahtanumont Jéhovah, monaneteaonk pish weenuhkunk.
32.11 Weekontam8k ut Jehovahut, muskouantam8k kenaau sampweseogish: kah weekontamoé mishont8wag, wame sampwutteahheogish.
33.1 Muskouanatam8k ut Jehovah, woi sampweusseogish: tabuttantamowonk 8nekonkqunau neg sampwesitcheg.
33.2 Wa[u]ssum8k Jehovah nashpe harp, k8t8hom8k nashpe psaltery, kah puhpequonegh piogquomposik pemunneahtonash.
33.3 Ket8ham8k wuske ket8homaonk: wunnepuhpequagk mishont8wom8ut.
33.4 Newutche wuttinnowaonk Jehovah sampwi kah wame wutanakausuongásh wunnamuhkut-eyeu8ash.
33.5 Womantam sampweusseonk, kah wussittam8onk: ohke numwohtau 8net8onk Jehovah.
33.6 Nashpe wuttinn8aonk God kesteauunash kesukquash: kah nashpe wunnashauonk wutch wutt8nut wame neadtahsheu nag.
33.7 Mohmôunum nuppeh ketahhannet, onatuh nomungquag, ponam monóiyeuash maumachiyeu komukqut.
33.8 Wame ohke qushonch Jehovahuh: wame neg wadohkitcheg muttaohket qushahettich
33.9 Newutche kutt8p, onk nnihyeup: wussinneuh onk menuhkahtop.
33.10 Jehovah ukken8nittuongan8osh penuohteaog mo teagwunneteauunash: wuttinanatam8onganoash missinninnuog wutayimunas[h] monteagwunninn8ut.
33.11 Ukken8nittuonk Jehovah michemohteau, wuttinanatam8wongash ut wuttahhut en wame pometeonganash.
33.12 Wunnanumau wutahtimôin wáManitt8mut Jehovah noh: kah missinninnuh, neh pepenóoncheh God nehenwonche 8tohtoonganinnuh.
33.13 Jehovah w8mompu wutch kesukqut, naau wame wunnaumonaoh wosketompaog.
33.14 Wutch nawadohkit, natauwompamau wame wadohkinutche ohket.
33.15 Tatuppehteau nag wuttahh8oash: natwontam wame wutanakausuwongan8ash.
33.16 Matta ketass8t wadchanau nashpe m8chequshae wutayeuwehteomoh: manuhkesit, ummishe menuhkesuonk matta pohquohwhunugk8.
33.17 Horse tahn8cheyeu8 wutch wadchanittuonk: kah nashpe mishemenuhkesuonk matta pohquohwhunugk8.
33.18 Kusseh wuskesuk Jehovah náau neh qushhukqutcheh: neg anoôsitcheg ut ummonanitteaonganit.
33.19 Pohquawhus ukketeahogkounouh wutche nuppunat, kah uppomantamwaheuh wutch mohshagqunneoneat.
33.20 Nukketeahogkou anoonau Jéhovah: noh nutannóhsueneumun, kah nutohqunneganun.
33.21 Newutche nuttahhun weekontam8onoh, newutche nuppabahtantamumun 8neetupanatamwe wesuonk.
33.22 Kummonaneteaonk, woi Jehovah, nuhkuhkongqutteuh, nean anoonog.
34.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David, {osuwunuk wutusseongash anaquabit} Abimelek: {noh monchaoohkauont, kah moncheu.}
34.1 Nuttabuttanamau Jehovah nagwutteaeu: tabuttantamauwaonk pish ohteau nutt8nut yeoyatcheh.
34.2 Nukketeahogkou muskouantam Jehovahut: hohpóog pish n8tamwog, kah weekontamwog:
34.3 Woi misheheh Jehovah weeche neen, kah môeu tahshinummuttuh 8wesuonk.
34.4 Nunnanamptassumomp Jehovah, kah n8tunkup: kah nuppohuohwhunukup wutch wame n8wabesuonganit.
34.5 Wummóneauouh kah wequaiyeúm8og: kah wuskesuk88ash matta akodchumun8ash.
34.6 Yeuoh kuttummunge wosketomp mau8p, kah Jehovah wunn8taòpuh, onk uppohquohwhunuh wutch wame wuttammepunnaonganit.
34.7 Wut-angelsumoh God weenuhkauwaog nag nah quoshóncheg: kah uppohquohwhuneh nah.
34.8 Woi qutchehtam8k kah naum8k Jehovah wunneetou, wunnanumau wosketomp noh pabahtanumont.
34.9 Woi qusheuk Jehovah kenaau 8netupanatam8moh: newutche neg quoshoncheg matta teag quenahukk8og.
34.10 Wushkóshumwu qunnón8wog quenáhukquog kah paskanantamwog: qut neg natinnewhoncheg Jehovahnoh, mat quenahukk8og ne teag wanegik.
34.11 Peyonk peissesog n8tiegk, kukkuhk8tomauonumw8 qushaonk Jehovah.
34.12 Howan nnoh kodtantog pomantamowonk, kah womantam sepepomantamun, woh wunnaumunat wanegik;
34.13 Nanaaitaash keenan wutch matcheyeuonganit, kah kussissitt8nash matta éyeumun8utch as8kekodteam8wonk.
34.14 Amaehtash matchetowonk, kah wunnésish: natinnehash wunnohteaonk, kah asuhkash.
34.15 Wuskesukquash Jehovah wunnomwaénutu: kah wéhtauogash wôshweemoash en ummauongan8óut.
34.16 Wuskesuk Jehovah ayeuuhkonau matchesenutcheh, wuttummehtahwhónat wutch mehquánumaongan8 ohke.
34.17 Wunnomwaen mauunnitteauoh, kah God wunn8taoh, kah uppohquohwhunoh wutche wame wuttammepunnaongash.
34.18 Jehovah uppas8sukauoh nahog pokshunk wuttahhouwoash, kah 8wadchanoh nahog pokshunkish wunnashauongan8.
34.19 Monat wutonkapunaongash wunnomwausseaénin: qut Jehovah uppohquohwhunoh nish wutch wame.
34.20 Wunnanaehteau wame wuskonash: matta pasuk pokshaunn8ut.
34.21 Matcheseonk pish nushau matcheet8oh: kah nag sekeneauoncheg wunnomwausseaenu pish nonsayeu8og.
34.22 Jehovah pohquohwhunau ukketeahogkôunn8oh wuttinnumoh: kah nag pabahtanumoncheg, matta pish pasuk nonsayeueu.
35.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David
35.1 Ke[n]8tamwansheh woi Jehovah, wutch nag mekausitcheg, ayeúkus nnag ayeukónukque[ó]neg.
35.2 Neemunush ohqunneg kah musonk8, kah neepaush aninnumah.
35.3 Kodtunush wonk quonnontuk, kah kuppúhhamau ummayou nag kod woskhukquéaneg: us nukketeahogkou nen k8wadchanitteaonk.
35.4 Chepshahettich nnag, kah akodchhettich kodnushhukqueaneg: qushkehettich, kah sohquéhenaj natwontogig n8woskhuk8ongan8.
35.5 Ogqunneungqussehettit wossadteamunit t8unnontog waban: kah wut-angelsumoh God wunnaumatehtáhwhonch.
35.6 Ummayou pohkenaj kah t8nequaj: kah wut-angelsumoh God wunnaumahtáhwhonch.
35.7 Newutche wanne mon teag wutch nupponahshabpunkquog ut passahthéganit, ne passahteamóhettit wutch nukketeahogkôunnoh, wanne mon teag wutch.
35.8 Paguanúonk nuhkuhkongqutch asq wâhteoóukup: kah neh ponashabpunkqueumpuh puttuhhukqutch, ne nunneáonk unnenneaj.
35.9 Kah nukketeahogkou pish weekontam Jehovahut: pish nummuskouanatam ut 8wadchan8waonganit.
35.10 Wame nuskonash pish n8waog, Jehovah howan anunkquean, pohquohwhunont matchekuoh noh wutch n8nunonche, nux matcheku, kah quenahukqut nàh wutch woskheont.
35.11 Pann8wae woacheg n8wabetunkquog: nuttinaunchem8wónukqunau ne mo wahteauo.
35.12 Nutunkquatunkquog matcheseonk wutch wunneseonk, woskeheonát nukketeahogkou.
35.13 Qut neen, mahchenáhettit, nohtonke nuthogk8onk: nutáhohpah nukketeahogkou mátta meetseon, & nuppeantamowonk qushkem8 en nupp8chenauónut.
35.14 Nutógqueenne neetompaut asa neematuh, naòshikquábip, onatuh maémont okasoh.
35.15 Qut onkapunnaon weekontamwog, kah miyaeog: nux matchetowog miyaeog nutayeuhkonukqunaout, kah matta n8wahteauouun: nunnenehkshanukquog, kah matta ahqheog.
35.16 Weeche eiantukeiyeuog kah mômôntuhuénuog mahshadtupp8hettit nummaumosketunkquog.
35.17 Jehovah tohutt8che kummoneauóog? kenáhamash nukketeahogkou wutch 8woskhuaonganuóut, pasuk88 nuñaumon wutch qunnón8ut.
35.18 Kuttabattantamoush ut mis[h]e mukkinneonganit: k8wowussumush kenugku monaog missinninnúog.
35.19 Ahque nummatwomog muskouanatamm8wóushettich pann8waeu, asuh ahque kehkehtequohtohuttehettich tahn8che sekeneaiitcheg.
35.20 Newutche matta n8wa8wog wunnohteaonk: qut natwontamwog as8kekodteam8e ahhunagish nah wutch manunaiinutche ut wuttohtawout.
35.21 Nux mishitt8naéog ayeuukone neen, n8waog, Ho, ho, naumunan nashpe nuskesukqunónat.
35.22 Yeu kenaumun, woi Jehovah ahque chequnapash, woi Jehovah, ahque na8sukah.
35.23 Mamonchish, kah t8hkish en k8sittumwanshuonkanit, kah en nuppissaumatuonganit num-Manitt8m kah nut-Jehovah.
35.24 OOsummeh, woi Jehovah, num-Manitt8m, neaunag k8nomwausseonk, kah ahque muskouantamwonshettich.
35.25 Ahque n8wahettich wuttahh8wout, ho ne nukkodnehteauunnan, ahque n8wahettich, nummisseasquinnean,
35.26 Akodchuhettich, kah moeu sohquehhenaj muskouantamohettit ut n8woskhukqunaont: hogquehhettich akodchuonk kah mishshonanittuonk mashehtunkqueoneg.
35.27 Mishontoe wekontamohettich, muskouantamohettich tapeneagig nussampweusseonk, nux n8wahettich nagwutteaeu mishehhunaj Jehovah noh tapeneog 8nenehheaonk wuttinnumoh.
35.28 Kah neenan pish yeum8 k8nomwausseonk kahk8wowussumunn8wonk neteagu.
36.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk} David {wuttinneumoh} Jehovah
36.1 Ummatcheseonk matcheetou n8wau anomut nuttah ut, qushaonk God wanne ohtano anaquabit.
36.2 Newutche waeenomou wuhhogkuh ut nehenwonche wuskesukqut nô pajeh ummatcheseonk namehteaumuk woh jishanumukquodtu.
36.3 Ukkutt8wongash ut wutt8nut, matcheetoash kah as8kekodteaum8ash: nukkodtum waontamun kah 8nesen.
36.4 Natwontam woskehuwaonk ut wuttappinneat, ponau wuhhogkuh matta wanegenunn8g may, matta jishantam8 matcheseonk.
36.5 Kummonanteaonk, woi Jehovah, kesukqut ohtau, kah k8nomwausseonk matokqsit.
36.6 Kussampweusseonk ogqunneunkquodt mogkodchuut: k8sittum8wongash m8nôhshinneash: woi Jehovah k8wadchan wosketomp kah puppinashim.
36.7 Toh nukkukque mishoadtu k8womoausuonk, woi God, yowutche wunneechanaoh wosketompaog pabahtantamwog kenuppawhunog wutonkauhtom8wôut.
36.8 M8cheke wamep8og nashpe 8nogk8onk kek, kah k8tattamhéoog kussepue weekontam8wongash.
36.9 Newutche tohkekommue pomantam8wonk kutahtauun: k8weequaioumut woh n8che naumunnean wequai.
36.10 Woi nagwutteanumau k8womoauseónk neg wahukk8aneg: kah k8nomwausseonk neg sampwutteahhoncheg.
36.11 Ahque pittuanumwemuseet ayeuuhkonsitch: kah ahque wunnutcheg matcheetou ontsinukquttei.
36.12 Anakausitcheg matcheseonk ne wuttit penushonau: kepuhkonog, kah matta pish tapenumoog neepaun.
37.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
37.1 Ahque musquanum kuhhog newutche matchesecheg, onk ahque iskáaus anakausitcheg matcheseonk.
37.2 Newutche pish teanuk: tummehtahwhoog onatuh moskehtuut, kah pish upp8pásuog onatuh oshkoshqut.
37.3 Pabuhtanum Jehovah kah wunnesish, neit pish k8tohkin yeu ohke, kah wunnamuhkut pish kussohkomm8nt.
37.4 Wonk tapeneau kuhhog en Jehovahut, kah pish kittinninnumunk kukkodtantam8wongash ut kuttahut.
37.5 Ahtuhsh kummay Jehovah, kah pabahtanum, kah pish kittinuhkqun.
37.6 Onk pish wussohwhuttauun k8nomwausseonk neane wequai, kah k8sittum8onk onatuh puhshaquodt.
37.7 Anwohsinous Jehovah, manunne annous ahque musquanum kuhhog newutche noh wónaiit ut ummayut, newutche wosketomp noh kesteunk matanatammóongash.
37.8 Netahshe musquantash, ahqueteaush chenauausuonk, ahque musquanam kuhhog ne teag wutch matchesenat.
37.9 Newutche matchesecheg pish tummehtahwhoog: qut yeug anounoncheg Goduh pish wutahtauunneau ohke.
37.10 Newutche teanuk kah pish mat matcheetowenuunn8, nux, menuhke pish kenatwontam wutayeuonk, kah wanne ohtano.
37.11 Qut manunnissuog pish wutahtauuneau ohke, kah pish tapeneaumwog monát wunnohteaonk.
37.12 Matchetou kodwoskéheau sampweusenutcheh, kah ummomoskéetauóuh.
37.13 Jehovah wutáhanehtauoh newutche wunnaumaoh usskesukodtum peyaúm8uk.
37.14 Matchetou sohwhunnum wuttogkodteg, kah anchuppinohtau, noh wuttin penohkonát matchekuoh kah quenahukqunutche kah nushonat sampweussecheg.
37.15 Wuttogkodtegano pish aum8 nehenwonche wuttahh8wóut, wutahtompeyeuoh pish pokshauoh.
37.16 O[h]guhsadchasuadt sampweusseaenin, anúhkâaumonaoh matchetowoh 8weenaieetuongan88ash.
37.17 Newutche wôhpittenash matchetou pish poksheau; qut Jehovah tahshinau wunnomwausseaenu.
37.18 Jehovah wahteau ukkesukkodtumash sampwesenutche kah ne ahtaahettit pish michemeyeu8.
37.19 Matta pish akodchuog ut matcheetinat kah mashogque kesukodtut pish wamep8og.
37.20 Qut matchetou pish onkuppunnau: kah ummatwomoh Jehovah pish onatuh Lambse wanogqut, nag pish mohsepaeog, pish pukutau[8]og.
37.21 Matcheetou nogohkou qut matta wonk wunnompenum8un: qut wunnomwausseaenin, monaneteau, kah ummagu[n].
37.22 Newutche neh wánanumoncheh pish wutohtauneau ohke: qut nag matchenanumoncheh pish tummehtahwhoog
37.23 Wutontanehtuongash wunneetou ummenuhkehteunash God kah tapeneam ummay.
37.24 Tokonogque uppenushon matta pish papukquane kepsha8; newutche Jehovah wuttahshinoh nashpe wunnutcheg.
37.25 N8skenneu8p, yeuyeu nummattauntam, qut asq nuppaje n[aáu]n wunnomwaussu ahquanumon, asa 8skannemunneoh weenshau petukqunnunk.
37.26 Micheme mona[n]eteau, kah nogohkaeihhuun: kah 8skannemuneoh 8nanumoneuh.
37.27 Amaéhtash matcheseonk, kah wunnesish; neit micheme wutohkish.
37.28 Newutche Jehovah womantam wussittum8wonk, kah matta ahquanumáou wunneetupanatamwoh: nag micheme wadchan8og, qut 8skannemunnuoh matcheetowog pish tummehtahwhôog.
37.29 Sampweusseaenuog pish 8tohkinneau ne ohke, kah ne pish 8tohkinneau micheme.
37.30 Wutt8n sampweusseaenin missohham waantam8wonk, kah weenan weogquttam8m8 wussittum8wonk.
37.31 Wuttinnaumatuonk um-Manitt8moh ohteau wuttahut, wanne pasuk wuttóntanehtuonk t8nequshininn8.
37.32 Matchetou askuhwau wunnomwausseaenu, kah ukkodtinneánuh.
37.33 Jehovah matta pish wunnukkonuh ut wunnutcheganit kah wussumahettit, mat8sumau.
37.34 Anous Jehovah, kah muttumash ummay, kah pish kutashinuk kutahtaunat ohke: matchetowog tummehtahwhut pish kenaumun.
37.35 Nunnaumup matcheetowog missi uppiohquttumóongan8, uppenaekinneat onatuh askuhquâmut nehenwonche neepadtag.
37.36 Qut amaem8, kah kusseh matta ohtano: nux nunnatinneawhop qut matta nunnamheuh.
37.37 Tuppanum pannuppu wunneetou, kah náou sampwesit: newutche adwòhkukquosik noh wosketomp wunnohteaonganu8.
37.38 Qut matchesecheg pish moeu paguanôog; 8wohkukquosinnunnaoont matchetowog, pish tummehtahwhoog.
37.39 Qut wadchanaongan8 wunnomwausseaenuog, 8m88 Jehovahut: & nag ummenuhkesuongan8oh wuttammepunahettit.
37.40 Kah Jehovah pish wuttannunnumaoh, kah pish uppohquohwhunuh; pish uppohquohwhunoh wutch matcheetowut kah wadchanoh, newutche uppabahtanumukquoh.
38.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David {mehquontamwahuon}.
38.1 WOi Jehovah ahque auskomeh musquantaman: asa ahque sasamukouheh kossoppag kummusquantam8onk.
38.2 Newutche kóunkquodtash patukshauash nuhhogket: kah kenutcheh m8cheke nukkinnequohkunk:
38.3 Wanne pasquanninn8 n8weyaus newutche kummusquantam8onk: kah wanne anwósinninn8ash nuskonash newutche nummatcheseonk.
38.4 Newutche nummatcheseonganash wunnuhkukkonkqunash nuppuhkuk: onatuh tuhkequod weanin, naish wussaume tahkekhukqunash.
38.5 Nuttanhukkash matchemungquot, kah anittash newutche nutas8tuonk.
38.6 N8tamanatam, m8cheke n8wonkohkom: pumuhshaon n[u]mmau qunnekesukod.
38.7 Newutche nusseganohtogqut numwohteau neechepunaonk, wanne menuhkano n8weyaus
38.8 N8chumwes kah nutchechishqusham, nummauup newutche n8tamehpunam nuttahhut.
38.9 Lord wame nukkodtantammoonk ohteau anaquabean, kah nutauwakont8waonk mutta assampamukquodtinn8 wutch kuhhogkaoo[u].
38.10 Nuttah tetequshin, nummenuhkesuonk sanumm8m8: kah nunnaum8wongan ut muskesukqut wonk amaemoi,
38.11 Womonukqueaneg, kah neetompaog nukqushhukkongquog wutch nukkehkechesuonk, kah anunkomogig nuppechohkongquog.
38.12 Kah neg wonk kadtinneanukqueaneg, nupponamungquog apehhunnah, kah kod[-]woskehhukqueanég nummamatchenukquog, kah natwontamwog as8kekodteaum8wonk quinnikesuk.
38.13 Qut neen, onatuh kókobsont,matta n8táoog: kah nutogqunneungqussip mokaket8muk, mo waushwunnum8g wutt8n,
38.14 Nemehkuh nutogqunneungqussip mo nan8tam8k, kah wanne auskomuwaongash wut8nut.
38.15 Newutche ken Jehovah kuttannóonsh pish ken8tah woi Jehovah num-Manitt8m.
38.16 Newutche nussip n8tah, iskont nuttoontahkanukquog: nusseet t8nukqushik mishehheaog wuhhogkauh nutayeukonukqunnaout.
38.17 Newutche nahen nukk8kqunnukshom, káh neuantam8onk nagwutteaeu ohteau anaquabeh.
38.18 Newutche nupahketeaun nummatcheseonk: nunneuantam wutche nummatcheseonk.
38.19 Qut nummatwomog wunnetantauneau, kah menuhkesuog kah [n]ag tahn8che sekeneunkqueóneg monaog.
38.20 Kah nag wonk onkquatausitcheg matchet wutche wunnegen nutayeuuhkonukquog, newutche nutahsuhkom ne wanegig.
38.21 Ahque ohquanumeh woi Jehovah; woi num-Manitt8m, ahque na8sukah.
38.22 Kenuppe aninnumah woi Jehovah, n8wadchanitteaonk.
39.0 {Nohtumpuhpequodt ut Jeduthun: ukketoohomaonk} David.
39.1 Nussip nutahqueteounash nummayash onk woh matta nummatchesu ut neenanut: nunnanaueihteoh nutt8n nashpe bridle matcheetowog anaquabeh.
39.2 Mo nukkaket8p chequnappean: nutchequnapip wutch wunnegenut, kah nunnuantam8onk woggkouem8p.
39.3 Nuttah kussoppiyop anomut nuhhogkat, natwontamon n8tau chikohtop: neit nukkeket8komp neenanuut.
39.4 Jehovah ayimah wahteaun n8wohkukquosin8wonk; kah quttuhhumun nukkesukkodtumash teagua; onk woh n8wahteoun toh anukuhquohtei.
39.5 Kusseh kuttinnukkuhqutteah nukkesukkodtumash menutcheg neanuhkuhque kiskag kah nussepepomantamoonk wanne teag ut anaquabean, wunnamuhkut nish noh wosketomp ut menuhkesit, pannuppu tahn8cheyeu8. Selah.
39.6 Wunnamuhkut nish noh wosketomp pomushau tahn8che onatuh onkauohtaut: wunnamuhkut nag wuttamanatamwog tahn8che: numwonkquottou weenauweetuonganash, kah matta wahheo8 howane pish mohmounumunit.
39.7 Kah yeuyeu Jehovah, teaguas nutannoantam? kuttannoonsh.
39.8 Pohquáhwusseh wutche wame nummatcheseonganash, ahque ayimah wutuspunamoaongan8 as8kutcheg.
39.9 Mat nukkaket8p, mat n8waoshwunnumop nutt8n, newutche kutussenap.
39.10 Amaunumah kuttogkom8waonk: nummohchikonaip nashpe wuttógkomuaonk kenutcheg.
39.11 Auskomue sasamatahwadcheh wosketomp newutche ummatcheseonk, kutayimun 8neetuonk mahchem8 onatuh moth: wunnamuhkut nish noh wosketomp tahn8cheyeu8. Selah.
39.12 N8tash nuppeantam8wonk woi Jehovah, kah kuhkeitash nummauonk, ahque chequnapsh ut nussuppequnut, newutche nuppenowohteau ut anaquabean, kah nuppenowohteau neane wame n8shunnonog.
39.13 Woi Ahque onk woh nummenuhkes, asquam ne mamonchean, kah matta wonk nutappein.
40.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk} David.
40.1 Nummanunne annoónup wutch Jehovah, kah nukkeihketunk, kah n8tam nummauonk.
40.2 Kah nukkodtinuk wutch uhqueneungquotte pohshahtheganit, wutch pisseagquane man8nskut, kah ponam nusseetash qussukquanit, kah menehketeau nuppomushaonganash.
40.3 Onk ponam wusku ket8homaonk nutt8nut, wáussumonat num-Manitt8mun, monaog pish wunnaumunneau, kah pish wabesuog, kah pish pabahtanum8og Jehovah.
40.4 OOnanumau noh wosketomp ayig uppabuhtanumaonk Jehovah noh, kah matta tohhentupanumonk pihtuanum8oh, asa yeuhoh quashkenutcheh en pannuwayeuonganehtu.
40.5 Monatash, woi Jehovah, num-Manitt8m, kummonchanatamwe anakausuongásh nish kesteauanish; kah kittinanummewonganinnonash, matta woh kuttápohkeetamonteanâsh: tohneit pahketeawon, kah ken8tamon monataash onk woh na adtashogkeetamuk.
40.6 Sephausuonk kah magoonk, matta kukkodtantam8unash, nutteauogash kuppohquanumup: chikohtae mag8ongash, kah matcheseongane sephausuongash matta kussein nash aninnumaiegk.
40.7 Neit nussip, kusseh nuppeyaum, k8sukkuhwhonganit tannussukkuhwhosu papaume nen.
40.8 N8wekontam ussen kuttinanatám8wonk, woi num-Manitt8m, nux kuttinnaumatuonk anomut nuttahut.
40.9 Nukkuhk8tomwehteam sampweusseonk ut mishemukkinneonganit, kusseh matta nussissetonash chequnohtanoash, woi Jehovah k8wahteoun.
40.10 Matta nutadtahtoou k8nomwausseonk anomut nuttahhut, nuppahketeounap kussampweusseonk kah k8wadchanuwaonk: matta nuputtagg[u]hhum8 k8womoausuonk kah k8nomwayeuonk wutche mishemukkinneonganit.
40.11 Ahque kogkôunumah kukkitteamonteanitteae monaneteaonk, woi God; kukkitteamonteanitteaonk, kah k8nomwayeuonk nagwutteaeu wadchanehettich.
40.12 Newutche woh mo tâpogkeetamounash matchetowonganash n8weinuhkongqunash nummatcheseongash [n]ukkogkonunuk newaj wanne nuttapenumm8 ishpuhquain: monatash onk neadtahshik nummeesunk ut nuppuhkuhqut, newaje nuttah sauwunuk.
40.13 Wussikketea[n]ininaj, woi Jehovah, pohquohwusseh, woi Jéhovah, kenuppu aninnumáh.
40.14 Nag akodchhettich, káh moaeu chepshahettich kodnushoncheg nukketeahogkounoh, nag a[sô]8hkaunaj kah akodchhenaj matcheanumukqueaneg,
40.15 Nonsayeuwehhettich, newutche wutonkatongan8 akodchuonk, anukqueaneg ho ho:
40.16 Wame nattinneahukqueaneg, wekontam8onukqush, muskouanatamonukqush newutche ken: neg womontogig k8wadchan8waonk, nagwutteaeu n8wahettich, Jehôvah mishshehenaj.
40.17 Qut nummatchek kah nukquenanhuk, onch Jehovah nummehquanumuk, ken nuttannosuenu, kah nuppohq[u]awussuénu ahque pitchinw[ô]ish woi num-Manitt8m.
41.0 {Nohtompuhpequod ukketoohomaonk} David.
41.1 Wunnanumau n noh tatabpanumont mátchekuoh: Jehovah pish uppohquohwhunoh wuttammepunanit.
41.2 Jehovah pish 8wadchauôh, pish uppomantamwaheuh, kah pish wunnanumau yeuut ohket: kah matta pish kupponoh wuttinanatam8onganout ummatwomoh.
41.3 Jehovah ummenuhkehheuh ut ummahchekonaeyeu appinneat; k8nashinnumau wame wuttappinneat mahchinait.
41.4 Nussip Jehovah monanumeh neetskeh nukketeahogkou, newutche kummatchenehhesh.
41.5 Nummatwomog nummatchenukquog, aquompak woh nupuk, kah 8wesuonk nupp8m8?
41.6 Kah natauwahit, tahn8che keket8kau: wuttahhoh mukkinnumont matcheseonk, sohhog, wuttinnaunchemwin.
41.7 Wame sekeneaitcheg nukkehkemwâ[ô]nukquog, ayeuuhkonittue natwontamwog n8woskhukk8ongan8.
41.8 N8waog, matcheepunaonk menuhkodtau wuhhogket: kah yeuyeu seepsik, matta pish wonk omohku.
41.9 Nux nehenwonche neetomp sompwanumog n noh sompwanumog, n noh meechup nupputtukqunnunk, nuttogskunk.
41.10 Qut ken Jehovah monanumeh, kah omohkineh, onk woh nutonkquttau.
41.11 Yeu nashpe n8wahteoun k8sekitteahe, newutche nummatwom, matta nutahanetunk8.
41.12 Qut neen, kutahshineh nussámpwutteahaonganit kah kupponeh anaquabean micheme.
41.13 Waussumunaj Jehováh um-Manitt8m Israel, wutche micheme yea[n] micheme[.] Amen kah Amen.
42.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt Maschil wutch wunnaumonuh} Korah.
42.1 Onatuh sâakussit aiump ut sepuussit: netatupe nukketeahogkou wuttinsanunumun wutche ken, woi God.
42.2 Nukketeahogkou kuhket8n Goduh, pomantamwae Goduh uttoh ahquompe woh peyaon kah woh nunnait ut anaquabit God?
42.3 Nussuppegwunash nummeechinapash kesukodaeu kah nukonaeu, nagwutteaeu nag anukquean uttiyeuwoh kum-Manitt8m.
42.4 Yeush mehquontamon, nussewoh nukketeahogkou ut nuhhogket: newutche n8weechauomp monacheg: n8weechauopanneg en wekit God, wadtáuatonkqussue n8weekontamoonkanun, kah n8wawussumaonganun weeche monacheg nananimohhettit peántamwakesuk.
42.5 Tohwutch penuhteaan woi nukketeahogkou, kah tohwutch wuttamanataman ut nuhhogkat, annóôsish en Godut, newutche pish n8wowussum, newutche nuttannunumunk wuttinnissuonk.
42.6 Woi num-Manitt8m nukketeahogkou penuhkon ut nuhhogkat newutche k8wáanumush wutch ohkit Jordan, kah Hermonites, kah wutch wadchu Missar.
42.7 Mahskehtugk weéquetum monoi mashant8wom8ug sokanon, wame kuttugk8mog kah kuttontukquog nupaumukongquog.
42.8 Qut Jehovah an8nau 8womoausuonk kesukodaeu, kah nukkonaeu ukket8homaonk n8weetomup, kah nuppeantamauaonk pomantamoe num-Manitt8m.
42.9 Nuttinh God, nukqussukquanum, tohwutch wananumean? tohwutch wutohposeh, newutche 8woskhuwaongan8 nummatwomog.
42.10 Togkodteg nuskonut ukkekomuwaongan8 nummatwomog, ashettit askesukokish, uttiyeuoh kum-Manitt8m.
42.11 Tohwutch penuhteaán woi nukketeahogkou, kah tohwutch wutamanumea[n] ut nuhhogkat? anoas God; newutche onch n8wowussum, noh uppomantamowonk nuttinnissuonk, kah num-Manitt8m.
43.1 Wussumeh, woi God, keket8hkansheh en matcheetowog wutahtuóut: woi pohquohwusseh wutch as8kekodteamocheg, kah mat sampweussegig.
43.2 Newutche um-Manitt8moh nummenuhkesuonk, tohwhutch pogkésean? tohwhutch wutohpôseh newutch 8woskhúaongan8 nummatwomog?
43.3 Woi ann8s k8wequai8m kah k8nomwayeuonk, nag sagkompagunéhhettich: nag pas8wéhettich k8neetupanatamwe wadchúut kah keekit.
43.4 Neit pish nuttóm wut-altarit God en Godut mussi n8weekontamóonk: nux: ut harput k8waeenomoush, woi Manit, num-Manitt8moh.
43.5 Tohwhutch penuhteáan woi nukketeahogkou, kah tohwutch wuttamanuméan ut nuhhogkut, anôas God, newutche onk onch n8w[a]wussum, noh uppomantamóonk nuttinnissuonk kah num-Manitt8m.
44.0 {Nohtompehpequodt wutch wunnaumonuh} Korah.
44.1 NOOtamúmunnónup nashpe nuttaúogunnónut, woi God, n8shunnónog nuttugqunnanónup, chagua anakausuonk kukkesteaoun nag ukesukkodtum8wóut n8adtit.
44.2 Kukquons8kauópanneg penuohteaog nashpe kenutcheganit, kah kuppasuopaneg: kutonkapunnanomp missinninnuog, kah kuppogkenópanneg.
44.3 Newutche matta 8tahtauóunneau ne ohke nashpe nehenwonche wuttogkodteg, kah nehenwonche wóhpittén8 wadchanukuppanneg, qut kuttinohkou kah kuppit, kah wussohsumoonk kuttinnussúonk newutche ken kukkitteamonteanumópanneg nnag.
44.4 Ken nukketass8timom woi God: an8hteám8 pohquohwussuaongash wutche Jakob.
44.5 Nashpe ken nukkepuhteamun nummatwomunonog: nashpe k8wesuonk nutahtaskuhkôunnonog ayeuhkonukqueagig.
44.6 Newutche matta nuppabahtanumoh nutahtomp, asa nuttogkodteg matta pish nuppohquohwhunugk8h.
44.7 Qut k8wadchannimun wutch nummatwomunonut: kah kutakodchehheoog neg sekeneunkqueagig.
44.8 En Godut m8cheke n8weekontamumun nehteagu: kah n8woeenodtumumun k8weesuonk micheme. Selah.
44.9 Qut kuppogkesumun, kah kutakodchehimun, kah matta k8weeche sohhamm8tam8 nukkesauwameonganun.
44.10 Kukqushk8kayimun wutch matwout: kah nag sekeneunkqueogig mukk8kinnuwaog wutch wuhhogkauh
44.11 Kuttinnumauoog nuhhogkanonuh onatuh shepsog m8hwhut, kah kussiswahimun ut penuwohteatu.
44.12 Kummag kummissinninnumog wutch monteag, onk matta k8chenaetu wuttinnoadtuongan8.
44.13 Kutayimaiimun nukkekomukk8wonganun neetatteamunganonut, nummamanauwanummitteaonganun kah nutahanehtonteaonganun neg weenuhkongqueogig.
44.14 N8woweenwhomukk8onganun kutayimaiimun kenugke penuwohteaog: nununukkuhquohtunkqunanonut missinninnuog.
44.15 Nukquenauanumoonk nagwutteohteau anaquabeh kah nuskesukqu[u]e akodchuonk nunnuhkukko[n]gqun.
44.16 Newutche 8wadtauatonkqussuonk nnoh kekomukqueog kah noh blasphemont: newutche matwau kah an8toaenin.
44.17 Wame yeush nunnuhkukkongqunnanonash: onk onch matta k8wannanumunn8mun: asa matta nuppann8waussumun wutch k8n8waonk.
44.18 Nuttahhun matta qushkeu; asa nutôntanehtuonganunnonash matta panneomun8ash ut kummayut.
44.19 Tokonogque m8cheke kuppokshassunau wutohtuout Dragonsog: kah kupputtagkuhhimun wutonkaohtom nupp8onk.
44.20 Wananatamôgis 8wesuonk num-Manitt8mun; asa spu[nnn]umauogit nutcheganunnonash pénowe Manitt8og.
44.21 Sunnummatta woh God wunnatinneahham8un? newutche wahyeau keme unnantam8onk nuttahhut.
44.22 Nux wutche ken nunnashshitteàmun quinnikesuk: nutogquanumu[ttt]eamun onatuh sheep nohshit.
44.23 T8hkish tohwutch kouean woi Jehovah, omkish ahque pogkesinan micheme.
44.24 Tohwutch puttoghuman kuskesuk onk wanantaman nuttonkapunnaongan, kah n8woskhetteyaonganan.
44.25 Newutche nukketeahogkôunnun n[ô]áyeu en puppissiyeúut nunnogkussen menuhkohteau ohkekontu.
44.26 Omohkish aninnumaiinnean, onk pohquohwussinnan wutch kummonaneteaonk.
45.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Shoshannim wutch wunnaumonuh} Korah, {Maschil: womoausuoohomaonk}
45.1 Nuttahhut mohchekomeetau wanegik: nussinneash nutayimmoongash papaume ketass8t: neenân ummequnuh kenupsukqwhosu.
45.2 Kumm8cheke wompes onk wunneechan8oh wosketompáog, wunneetupanatam8wonk sokanumun kussisset8nut: newajeh God wananumukquean micheme.
45.3 Wushpinnaush kuttogkomoneg ut kehquâut woi másugkénan, weeche kussohsumowonk kah k8wohquânum8onk.
45.4 Kah k8wohquanum8wonganit, wunnaiyeue náiyeumukqush, newutche wunnomwayeuonk, manunnissuonk kah wunnomwausséonk: kah kuttinnohkou kukkuhk8tomunk uhquinneunkquokish.
45.5 Kukkouhquodtash kenaiyéuash ut wuttahh8wout Ketass8t ummatwomoh: ne nashpe penushahettit missinninnuog ut agwe ken.
45.6 Kutappuonk, woi God, michemohteau kah micheme, kukketass8tamoe togkodteg sampwe togkodteg.
45.7 K8womontam sampweusseonk, kah kussekeneam matcheseonk: ne wajeh God kum-Manitt8m sussequanukquean nashpe weekontamoe pummee m8cheke onk neg weechaiyeumukqueaneg.
45.8 Wame kuthogk8ongash assumungquodtash myrre, aloes, kah cassia: wutch Ivory weetuomash, uttoh waj muskouanatamhinumuk.
45.9 Ketass8tamwog wuttaun8oh wee[c]haiyeumaog wutt8wuttumwossissoh: kuttinnohkôunit sonksq wunnepaun golde hogk8unash wutch Ophir.
45.10 N8tah (nuttaunes) kah natwontash kah kukkeitash: wannanum wonk nehenwonche kummissinninnumog, kah k8sh week.
45.11 Neit ketass8t m8cheke kodtantam k8neetuonk newutche noh kum-Manitt8m kah noh wowussum.
45.12 Kah wuttaunoh Tyre na pish wutappen paudtaun mag8onk: weenaeetuog kenugke missinninnuut pish k8wonkkumukquog.
45.13 Wuttaunoh ketass8t pannuppe sohsum anomut, wuthogk8ongash assequosu Gold.
45.14 Pish pas8au ketass8tamwut, wuthogk8unit ayinneas ahómogquesuuk, nunksquaog, weechayeumonche asukkonkqutcheh pish kuppaudtonteanunk.
45.15 Pish weekontamwe kah muskouantamwe pasou8og: pish petutteaog ketass8t weekit.
45.16 K8shuw8g keneechánuwôog pish wunnómpekompanean yeug woh kussontimóhkouog wame ohkeit.
45.17 Nutayum k8wesuonk mehquantamunat ut wame pometuonganit: newajeh pish missinninnuog k8waeenomukquog micheme kah micheme.
46.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt wutch wunnaumonuh} Korah {ketoohomaonk ut Alamoth}
46.1 Jehovah n8tusphuaonganun, kah nummenuhkesuonganun: kenupaninnohsu wuttammepunaùmuk.
46.2 Newajeh matta wabeseog tokonogque óntohtag ohke, kah tokonogque wadchuash óntahtag en nôeu ketahhannit.
46.3 Ketahhannuppog mishontowag, kah tukk888gk, wadchuash quequog muttaontuk8k. Selah.
46.4 Na seip n ne kussitchuan weekontamwahtunk wut8tan God: wunneetupanatamwohke week nôappit.
46.5 God nôeu appu, matta pish ontappu, God pish wuttannunnummaoh nompôaeu.
46.6 Penuwohteaog musquantamwog, as8tám8ongash ontahtaash, mishontowau, ohke mohtupaémo.
46.7 Wut-Jehovahnum8oh ayeutoáog k8wetomukqun: ummanitt8moh Jakob kuttusphuaonganun. Selah.
46.8 Peyunk naum8k wutanakausuonganash Jehovah, uttoh in paguanuongash wutayimun ut[]ohkeit.
46.9 Sohkom ayeuhteaongash aongkouokhomuk: pohqunau ohtompeh; pohquetahham qunnunktug, chikohsum chariotsash ut n8taut.
46.10 Chequnappek, kah wahteau8k neen Manit, pish nummishhet ut penuwohteátu: pish nummishhet ohket.
46.11 Wut-Iehovahnum8oh ayeuteaog k8weetomukqun, um-Manitt8moh Jakob kuttusphuáonganun. Selah.
47.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ketoohhomaonk wutch wunnaumonuh} Korah.
47.1 Woi puhpunkanitcháh8k wame missinninnuog, mishont8wag en Godut, nashpe sohkuhsue mishont8waonk.
47.2 Newutche Jehovah quanunkquapit [û]hqunneongqussu: nnoh kehchu ketass8t wame muttaohket.
47.3 Pish sohkauau missinninnuh kenaan ut agwu; kah wutohtimóneash agwu kusseetinnónut.
47.4 Pish kuppépenamwanshhikqun kutohkein: 8neetuonk Jakob neh womononcheh. Selah.
47.5 Manittou spéi nashpe mishontowaonk: Jehovah nashpe kutt8wóm8 monopuhpeg.
47.6 N8homunk waeenomaongash God, n8hhomunk waeenomaongash: n8hhomunk waeenomaongash kukketass8tomomun n8homunk waussumaongash.
47.7 Newutche God keitass8tim88 wame muttaohket, n8hhomunk waantamwu waeenomaongash.
47.8 God nánauneau pénuwohteoh: God appu wunneetupanatamwu wutappuonganit.
47.9 Nanaunoncheg missinninnuh moeog, ummissinninnumoh um-Manitt8moh Abraham: newutche muttaohke ogqunnegash wutchayeu8oash Godut: nnoh m8cheke mishehheuh.
48.0 {Annoohhomae keto[h]homaonk wutch wunaumonuh} Korah.
48.1 Missugken Jehovah, kah mishewa[e]enomau wutt8tanit kum-Manitt8mun, wunneetupanatamwu wadchumut.
48.2 Wunnohteau, 8weekontam8wonk wame muttaok ne wadchu Sion, nanummuttinneaou, wut8tan mishe ketass8t.
48.3 God wahheau weekuwout wuttusphuaongan8.
48.4 Newutche kusseh ketass8tamwog moieog, môeu paumushaog.
48.5 Wunnamuneau, nemehkuh ummonchanatamunneau, 8tamanatamunneau, 8semutteamunneau.
48.6 Na ut wabesuonk tohqunukquog, kah onkquammam8onk, onatuh mittamwossis [n]eechadt.
48.7 Kuppokshadtoh Tarshishe kuht8nogquosh wutchepwosh.
48.8 Neane n8tamog, ne kittinne naumunnan ut wut8tanit um-Manitt8m8 ayeuteaog; ut wut8tanat kum-Manitt8mun, God pish ummenuhkehteun micheme. Selah.
48.9 Nummequantamunnan k8womoausue kitteamonteanitteaonk, woi Manit, ut nôeu kuppeantamwakomukqut.
48.10 Néaunag k8wesuonk, woi Manit, ne nih k8waeenamitteaonk, wehque aongkouohkomuk, kittinnohkounit numwohtau wunnomwausseonk.
48.11 Muskouantaj wadchu Sion, wuttauneunk Judah weekontamwehettich newutche k8sittumm8wongash.
48.12 Papomshak Sion, quinnupwshak, ogkeetam8k wonkan8sinash.
48.13 Kuhkinneam8k naneutungash, natwontam8k weetuomash: onk woh kummishamâônash pometuonk p[a]om8uk.
48.14 Newutche yeuoh God kum-Manitt8mun micheme kah micheme: n noh kussamp8wunuk en nuppunnat.
49.0 {Nohtumpuhpequodt ukketoohomaonkanoo wutch wunnaumonuh} Korah.
49.1 Yeu n8tam8k wame missinninnuog kuhkeihtam8k wame wadohkeogish: muttaohket.
49.2 Wosketompaog, kah nanánuacheg weenaieetuwog kah matchekuog moeu.
49.3 Nutt8n missohham waantam8wonk: kah nuttahhe natwontam8wongash papaume waantamowonk.
49.4 Kukkodn8tam kukkinneasuonk: n8wóhshinum nunnupw8aongash ut harpeut.
49.5 Tohwutch wo[h] wabesee matchesemuk, nagquonne matcheseonk quinnuppekongquean?
49.6 Nag pabahtóntogig 8weenaieetuongan8, kah maskauacheg ut m8natut ummaumacheiyeum8ash.
49.7 Matta woh howan ta[h]wh8ou weematt8oh: kah matta woh ummanouhhumauouh nahoh Goduh.
49.8 Newutche man8whaonk ukketeahogkon8oh mishóadtu, kah chequnappu micheme.
