49.9 Onk woh micheme pomantam, kah matta woh naum8 anneu weenohke.
49.10 Newutche náau waantamwoh nupp8oh kah wonk mattamogquoh, kah puppinashimwe wosketomp awohkompanau, kah pish nukkodtumauwaog 8weenaeetuongan8 onkatogeh.
49.11 Kemeu wuttinanatam8ongan8, week88ash pish micheme ohtaash, kah 8tahtuongan88ash pannuppu wame pometeonganash: hettamwog wutohkéeuoash neahennit.
49.12 Qut quhtianumit wosketomp, matta 8weekohteáun: ohqunneungqussu puppinashimwut noh awakompunneat.
49.13 Yeu wutusseongan8 wutass8tuongan8: onch wunneechán8oh wuttapeneaumunun ne an8wahettit. Selah.
49.14 Onatuh sheepsoh seepsinwog weenohket, nupp8wonk pish umm8hwho, kah sampwesitcheg pish umm8hwho, kah sampwesitcheg pish wunnanaunouh nahhog nompoaeu: kah 8neetuonkan8 pish mohtupaemo ut weenohket ne wadohkehettit.
49.15 Qut Manit pish pohquohwhunau nukketeahogkounoh, wutch ummenuhkesuonganit weenohkee, newutche pish nutattumunuk. Selah.
49.16 Ahque wabesish, howan weenauweekit: wussohsumowonk weekuwout nano mishehteaumuk.
49.17 Newutchu nuppuk, matta pish teag 8tauoouun[:] wussohum8wonk matta pish ássuhkongkóu.
49.18 Tohkonogque pamontog, wunnanumau ukketeahogkounoh: kah wosketompaog k8woweenomuk 8nenehheádt kuhhog nehenwonche.
49.19 Noh pish au pometuongan8 8shuoh: nag matta pish naum8og wequai.
49.20 Wosketomp quttiantog, qut matta[]waantog ogqunneunkqussu wutawakompunnae puppinashim.
50.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
50.1 Masugkenuk Manit Jehovah wussinneah, weequetum muttaok waj pashpishont, onk yea pajeh wayont.
50.2 Wutch Sion pannuppu wunneetuonk, God wohsumup.
50.3 Kum-Manitt8mun pish peyau, pish mat chequnnappu: n8htau pish nashqunneau ut anaquabit, onk pish mishehtashin wewenu.
50.4 Wutch wohqut wee[h]quetum kesukquásh, kah ohke, onk woh wussumau ummissinninnumoh.
50.5 Mukinumah n8neetupanatam8mog: yeug ayimaiutcheg wunn8waonk nashpe sephausuonk.
50.6 Kah kesukquash pish nahtitteau 8nomwausseonk: newutche nagum nehenwonche wussittum. Selah.
50.7 N8tiek, woi nummissinninnumog kah kukkinn8numw8 woi Israel, kah kutayeukonittue wauwóonsh, nen Manit kum-Manitt8m.
50.8 Matta kutaushkômun8h newutche kussephausuongash, asa chikohtae kummag8onganash, nagwutteohtaash anaquabeh.
50.9 Matta pish neemunoh nomposhim wutch keekitm asa nompshimwe goats wutch kutchipaneutunkanit.
50.10 Newutche nish noh puppinashim touohkomukqut nuttaihe: puppinshimwog nequt mutanunkanogkussuog wadchuukontu.
50.11 N8waeh wame papinshásog ut wadchukontu: kah tauohkomukwe puppinashim nuttaiheog.
50.12 Kodtupwean matta kuttinninn8un, newutche muttaohk nuttaihe kah neadtahshimmechumik.
50.13 Sun woh nummeech k8washinne weyaus, asuh sun woh n8tattam 8sqheonk goats?
50.14 Aninnumok God tabuttantam8wonk kah ôadtuhkou kukquoshaumaongash God nôappit.
50.15 Kah wehquetumah ne késukok wuttammepunnaa[n] pish kuppohquohwhunush, onk pish kussohsumm8woneh.
50.16 Qut God unnau matchetowoh, tohwutch ussean n8tamwahuwon nukkuhk8waongash; asa noh kittin neemunnumunat n8[n]8waonk ut kutt8nut?
50.17 Sekeneamán kuhk8tomuhteaonk, kah unnohteaan nuttinn8waongash kuppusquanit.
50.18 Náutcheh komm8towaenin, neit k8weetowom kah k8weetom mamussuenuog.
50.19 Kummamatcheyim ut kutt8nut: kah keenan ayim as8kekodteam8ongash.
50.20 Appean kummamatchein keemat: kukkehkom wunnaumonuh nehenwonche kokas.
50.21 Yeush kuttoussenash, kah matta toh nussu, kuttenantamup nuttinussin neanussean qut kutaushkomush, kah n8nehtauunash ut anaquabeân,
50.22 Yeuyeu yeu natwontam8k wananumogish God, ishkont kenehneeksháunumw8, kah matta howân kuppohquohhunukk8mw8.
50.23 Howan maguk tabuttantamowonk, nussohsum8wonuk: kah noh sampwe wánohtunk wutanakausuongash, nunnohtin 8wadchanuwaonk God.
51.0 {No[h]tompuhpequodt ukketohhomaonk} David. {Nathan Manittoowomp paaonont mahch[e] petukauont} Bathshebah.
51.1 Kitteamonteanumah, woi God, neaunag k8womoausue kitteamonteanitteaonk: neaunag mattanukish kukkittamunge m[o]naneteaonk jishkhash nummatcheseongash.
51.2 Pannuppu kutchessumeh wutch nummatcheseongash: kah pahke wutch nummatcheseongash.
51.3 Newutche nussamp8am nummatcheseongash, kah nummatcheseonk nagwutteohteau anaquabeh.
51.4 Ken, ken webe kummatche[n]ehesh, kah yeu nutussen matcheseonk ut anaquabean: onk woh kussampotont ket8hkôan, kuppahkesittont wussittuman.
51.5 Kusseh nukkuhkenaihetteap ut matcheetupanatamowonganit: wompoquait nokas, ut matchéseonganit.
51.6 [missing!]
51.7 Pahkhe nashpe hisop, onk pish nuppahkes: kutchessumeh, onk pish nutánue wompeseum k8n.
51.8 N8tamwaheh weekontam8onk kah muskouanatam8onk, nish nuskonash pohquatóhha[m]ahpash kuskesuk wutch nummatcheseongashh, onk jiskhash wame nummatcheseongash.
51.9 Puttogwhush kuskesuk wutch nummatcheseongash, onk jiskhash wame nummatcheseongash.
51.10 Kesteah pahkemetah, woi God: kah nagwutteáe sampwôhteae nashauonk wuskéheh.
51.11 Ahque pohkeseh wutch anaquabean, kah ahque amaunumah k8neetupanatamwe nashauonk.
51.12 Nompahtah wonk weekontamm8wu k8wadchanuwaonk kah kenannouwe nashauanit kogkánenitch.
51.13 Neit pish nukkuhk8tomau pánesecheg kummayash kah matcheseaenuog pish kukquinnuppekompauwehtunkquog.
51.14 Pohquohwusseh wutch shuhkonat, woi God, ken God wadchanuae num-Manitt8m: kah neenan pish mishontowá8homau kussampweusseonk.
51.15 Woi Lord wóshinish nussissitt8nash, kah nutt8n pish nahtitteau k8woweénomitteaonk.
51.16 Newutche matta kukkodtantamo sephausuonk, onk woh kittinnummaunun: matta k8wekontamo chikohtae mag8ongash.
51.17 Sephamauaongash God ne pohquesu nashâuonk, pohqui kah tannogki metah, woi matta kutchadchepantam8h.
51.18 Wunnesish weekontaman ut Sion: ayish qussukquaninnutongash ut Jerusalem.
51.19 Neit pish k8seketahhuk sampweusseae sephausuongashh, chikohsumwe mag8ongash kah mumusseu chikohsum8ongash: neit pish kussephamungquog oxinoh ut kut-Altarumut.
52.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt Maschil ukketoohomaonk} David, Doeg {Edomite anont} Sauloh, {wuttinuh,} David {peyau weekit} Ahimelech.
52.1 Tohwutch waénómut kuhhog woskehuwônat, woi masugkenan? 8net8onk God nagwutteohteau.
52.2 Keenan natinneham woskehuwaongah, onatuh kenag chahquog, as8kekodteamwanakausin.
52.3 Kumm8cheke womantam matchit onk ne wanegik: kah pann8wayeuonk onk ne sampwayeuonk. {Selah.}
52.4 K8womantam wame shehteae kutt8wongash, woi as8kekodteamwe meenan.
52.5 God pish ken wonk kenushhuk micheme pish kutamaúnuk kah pish kukkodtunuk wutch k8tahtuonganit: kah pish ken8sw8muhhuk wutch pomantamwae ohket. {Selah.}
52.6 Kah sampweusseaénin pish wunnaumun, kah wabesu, kah wutahanehtauoh.
52.7 Kusseh, yeuoh wosketomp matta unnant[à]m8 God nummenuhkesuonk; qut pabahtantamm8nat mishe 8weenaieetuonk, menehkheau wuhhogkuh ut ummatcheseonganit.
52.8 Qut nutogqunneunkqus askuhquamut olive mahtug, ut weekit God: nuppabahtantam ummonaneteaonk God micheme kah micheme.
52.9 Kummicheme waeenomush, newutche kummahche ussen; kah nuttannôantam k8wesuonk newutche wunnegen ut anaquabhettit k8neetupanatam8mog.
53.0 {Nohtompuhpequdt ut Mahalath Maschil ukketoohhomaonk} David.
53.1 Mattamog n8wau ut wuttahhut, wanne Godunn8, anunwog, kah mahche usseog niskeneungquok matcheseonk: nag wanne pasuk wun[n]esu.
53.2 God womámpu wutch kesukqut en wosketompaog wunnaumonaoh, kodnâau howaneh wahwatánumutcheh, kah natinneawhont Goduh.
53.3 Nag nishnoh pasuk qushkeog, nag wàme pannuppu niskeneunkqussuog, wanne howan 8nesu, wanne mo pasuk.
53.4 Anakausitcheg matcheseonk wanne ahteauog wahteauonk? mohwhaog nummissinninnumoh meechwog petukqunneg: wanne wehquetumauoog Goduh.
53.5 Naut mishe wabesuog toh woh mat adt wabesúmuk: newutche God seóhham wushkonash nnoh ayeuhkonukquéan, nag kutakodcheheaog, newutche God wutjishânumoh nahog.
53.6 Woi wadchanaongan8 Israel, wutch sohhamm88utch Sion! God quáhchuwunont wutch missinnáinneat ummissinninnumoh, Jakob weekontam kah Israel pish muskouanatam.
54.0 {Nohtumpuhpequodt ut Neginoth Maschil ukketoohomaonk} David. {Ziphimsog paahettit kah ônahettit} Sauloh: {sun matta} David {puttogqueu w[e]eche nenawun}
54.1 Wadchaneh nashpe k8wesuonk, woi God, kah wussumeh naashpe kummenuhkesuonk.
54.2 N8tash nuppeantam8wonk woi God: kukkeitash nuttinn8waongash nutt8nut.
54.3 Newutche penuwohteaog neepaeihtunkquog, kah woskehuacheg nukkodnushúkquog: matta pónau8og Goduh anaquabhettit. Selah.
54.4 Kusseh, God nuttannohsuenu: God weetomau nag kogkanoncheg nukketeahogk[ô]unoh.
54.5 Pish matunkquatauau nummatwomoh: tummehah naghoh wutch k8nomwayeuonk.
54.6 Nanouwe kussephamoush n8woweenodtum k8wesuonk woi Jehovah, newutche wunnegen.
54.7 Newutche nuppohquohwhunuk wutche wame wuttammehpunnaonganit: kah nuskesukqut n8che naum uttoh en kodtantog wutch nummatwômog.
55.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Neginoth Maschil ukketoohhomâonk} David.
55.1 NOOtash nuppeantam8wonk woi God: kah ahque puttogwehtah wutch n8weehquttumm8wonganit.
55.2 Kukkeitah, kah n8tah, nummau nuppeantam8wonganit kah n8wadtauatongqus.
55.3 Newutche 8wadtauatongqussuonk matwau, newutche 8woskhuwaonk matcheetou: newutche nuttinnuhkongquog matcheseonk, kah musquantamwe nussekeneungquog.
55.4 Nuttahhut m8cheke nutonkquomom, kah mishe wabesuonk newutche nupp8wonk nunnuhkukkongquog.
55.5 Wabesuonk kah nukshaonk nunnuhkukkongquog, kah quoshque wabeseuonk nukkepuhkonuk.
55.6 Kah nussip, woi onunnuppohwhunonti wuskuhwhunonáut, onk woh nutt8wem, onk woh nutanwohsin.
55.7 Kusseh, onk woh nôadtit nuppomuhsham, woh nutap touohkomuk. Selah.
55.8 Woh nukkenuppisham wutch nuppohquohhamunat wutch mehshétash, kah nashqut.
55.9 Paguóhteash, woi God, chachabuwóm8utch weenannúwóash, newutche nunnaum mishe musquanetúonk kah penuánittuonk ut otanat.
55.10 Asekesukokish, kah nukonáeu papomshaog qussikquanun[n]eutunkanit; woskehuwaonk wonk, kah uhquanum8onk noeu.
55.11 Matcheetowonk nôeu ohtau, as8kekodteam8onk kah puhchuteaonk matta ámaémun8 wutch wuttaumaukqut.
55.12 Newutche matta matwau nukkekómuk8h, neit woh numm[ã]nunnes: asa matta nnoh sekeneaiop mishshéheop wuhhogkuh áyeuuhkonittue neen, neit woh nutattashômp nuhhog.
55.13 Qut ken wosketomp kuttatuppeyeu8mun, ken sampwoshássean, kah neetomp.
55.14 N8ne weetuódtimun, moeu nuppompomushaumun weekit God.
55.15 Nupp8onk tohqunonch nahog: kah keteáeu áhettich chepiohkomukqut: newutche matcheseonk ne wodohkéhettit, kah kenugku nagkoh.
55.16 Qut nen n8weehquetumau God: kah Jehovah pish n8wadchánuk.
55.17 Wanúnk8ukish: kah mohtompogkish kah puhshaquadcheh nuppeantam, kah nummishantowae mau: onk pish n8tam n8wadtauatonkqussuonk.
55.18 Wunohteae pohquohwhunau nukketeahogkounoh wutch ayeuwuttinneat ayeuqueúhpanneg: newutche monaog n8weechuhumukup.
55.19 God pish n8tam kah pish wutônkapinnanoh: nagum macheemapit, Selah: newutche wanne aûseweog newajeh matta qusháhetteg Goduh.
55.20 Quohshunnummaau wunnutcheash neh wânuhkônukqutche: pohqunum 8n8waonk.
55.21 Ukkutt8wongash wutt8nut m8siyeuash m8cheke onk ne butter; qut ayeuteaonk wuttahh8wout: ukkutt8ongash anue n8hkiyeuash onk ne pummee; qut nish kodtunnumwe togkodtegash.
55.22 Unnuhkou k8weanun Jehovah, kah pish kukkogkónuk: matta pish unnanumau8 wunnomwaenu ontsapsh.
55.23 Qut ken woi Jehovah pish kuttinohkonog onkapunnae psahtheganit: sheteaenuog kah as8kekodteamoenuog matta pish pomantamoog pohshe ne woh sohtepomantamwehhetteup: qut neen kuppabahtanumush.
56.0 {Nohtompuhpequadt ut Jonath-Elim-Rechokem, Michtam} David, {Philistiansog tohqunahettit ut Gath}
56.1 Monanumeh woi God, newutche wosketomp nukkod-misheashquónuk: ayeuwéhteadt nishnoh kesukod, n8woskhik.
56.2 Nummatwômog nukkod-missashquónukquog asekesukokish, newutche nag monaog ayeuhkôsutcheg, woi ken nô appéan.
56.3 Wabeseon kuppabahtanumush.
56.4 Ut Godut n8woweenodtumau wuttinn8waonk: nuppabatanum God, matta n8wabissuónoh weyaus toh kodnéhit.
56.5 Asekesukokish wôónkitteau8og nuttinn8waongash: wame wuttinanatam8ongan88ash nutayeuuhkonukqunassh wutche machuk.
56.6 Moeog, puttogwhâog w[u]hhogkâug, askuhhumwog nuttontannehtuongash, askwehettit wutch nukketeahogkou.
56.7 Sun woh pohquohhumwog nashpu ummatcheseongan88ash? kummusquantamunat penuhteash missinninnuog woi God.
56.8 Kutogkeetam n8wauwónuongash, ponsh nussuppéguenash k8wishquadt: sun matta ohtanoash k8sukkuhwhonganit?
56.9 Maunnitteaunnon, neit nummatwomog qushkeog: yeu n8wahteou[n], newutche God n8weech8humuk.
56.10 Godut n8woweenodtu[m] wuttinn8waonk: ut Jehovah n8wowussittum wuttinn8waonk.
56.11 God nuppabahtanum matta n8wabesu wosketomp toh woh ânhukqueh.
56.12 Kukquoshámuaongash nutapehtunkqunash woi God, k8woweenomsh.
56.13 Newutche kuppohquohwhun nukketeahogkou, wutch nuppunat: sun matta kuppohquohwhuttau nusseetash wutch penushó[n]at? woh nuppompomusham anaquabit God 8wequaiyeum8out pomantogig.
57.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt Al tasehith michtan} David, {waseem[o]teaont} Sauloh {ut hassunnegkut}
57.1 Monanumeh woi God, monanumeh, newutche nukketeahogkou kuppabahtanumuk: nux wutonkaohtomut kenuppahwhunnog n8tspuhh8aonganinneunk; onk neit yeush onkapunnaongash pamwushaum8uk.
57.2 Nummauunnitteau God nôhappit: Godut noh aseau[u]shhikque wame teanteaquassinish.
57.3 Pish an8team8 wutch kesukqut, kah n8wadchanuk wutch ukkekómuwaonk, noh kodmusseasquonukqueh. Selah. God pish an8nau um̃onaneteaonk kah 8nomwáonk.
57.4 Nukketeahogkou weetomau qunnón8oh, kah n8weetappemoog chogaswutcheg: wosketompaog wunnaumonaoh, weputtú8ah k[ô]unkquodtú8ash, kah qunnuhtugk88ash, kah weenannu8 keni[]togkodteg.
57.5 Mishshehununaj woi God ut ongkoue kesukquehtu: kussohsumoonk ongkoue ohtaj wame ohkit.
57.6 Quoshwunnáog wutashhabp8uh, wutch nutôntanehtuongash, nukketeahogkou nauwáeu: wônteaop ut ne áyoi, uppetshóneau nagumau ut nôeu. Selah.
57.7 Nuttah menuhkohteau woi God, nuttah menuhkohteau, nukket8homom kah nuttabuttantum.
57.8 T8kish nussohsum8onk t8hkeg psaltery kah harp: nen nompoéeu nutt8hkem
57.9 Kuttabuttantamoush woi God, ut kenugke missinninnuut: kukket8homoush ut kenugke wutohtimmóneat.
57.10 Newutche kummonaneteaonk missi, ut kesukqut, kah k8nomwáonk ut matokqsit.
57.11 Ken misháhenunaj ut ongkoue kesukqut woi God, kussohsumoonk ongkoue ohtaj wame ohkit.
58.0 {Nohtumpuhpequodt Altaschith michtam} David.
58.1 SUN wunnamukut kussimw8 wuñomwayeuonk woi mukkinnéonk? sun k8newussittumumw8, kenaau wosketompaog wunnaumonaoh?
58.2 Nux, kuttahhouóut kututussemw8 matcheseonk: kukquokquadhûmumw8, kenutcheganu 8wo[skh]uaongan88ash ut ohkeit.
58.3 Matchetówog penuwohteoóog wutch wompequainneat, wô[o]nuog quenanneekhettit, pann8wayeuog.
58.4 Wutonkquosketúeuonk[X] ogqueneungquodt wutonkquosketúeuonk ask8k: ogqunneunkqussuog mo nan8tam8k Addar, kobhog wehtáuog.
58.5 Nnoh matta n8tauonk wuttaúatongquss[ú]oh padchummúau, tohkonogque waantamwu padchummúadt.
58.6 Pohquetáhash weepittúash woi God, wutt8n8wóut pohquetahash ukkehtomputteau wskoshshumwe qunn[ó]n8og woi Jehovah.
58.7 Sobpáshettich onatuh nuppe pamutchúwog nagwutteaeu: sonteq[h]ohh8adt ukkôunkquodt, ogqunneunkquodtich tohmetohho[ó]m8ug.
58.8 Onatuh askéquttum mahtupáit: onatuh poékheunt mittumwossis, woh mo nauô8og nepauzoh.
58.9 Ohk8k asq aumattam8kup n8sippasqunaonk, pish wunneemunuh nahog onatuh pémsquoh, aspomantamwéhhettit, káh musquantog.
58.10 Sampweusseaen pish weekontam nag ann8taonk: pish kutchishitteau wussetash 8squehheongan8 matcheetowog.
58.11 Nemehkuh pish wosketomp n8wau, wunnamuhkut na wutonkquatunk wunnomwausseaen: wunnamuhkt nnoh God wussittuk ut ohkeit.
59.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt Altaschith Michtam} David, {Saul anooteamwut, kah wutaskuhwouh, ut weetuomut wunushonaont.}
59.1 Pohquohwusseh wutch nummatwomut, woi num-Manitt8m, wadchaneh nag wutch waabehtunkquéaneg.
59.2 Pohquawusseh wutch ánakausitcheg matcheseonk, kah wadchaneh wutch nushehteaenuog
59.3 Newutche kusseh, nag askuhw[a]og nukketeahogkôunoh, mas[u]gkénugig wuttôéog nuhhog, mátta wutch nuppanneseonk asa nummatcheseonk woi Jehovah.
59.4 Nag quogquéoge nanashwehtamwog, wanne wutch nummatcheseonk: t8kish aninnumah, kah naish.
59.5 Newutche, woi Jehovah, ummanitt8m8wóh ayeuhteáog um-Manitt8mwoh Israel, t8kish natauwaheoneat wame penuohteaog: ahque monanum matchetowog matcheseaenúog. Selah.
59.6 Nag qushkeog wunnonk8áe, nisketonkqussuog onatuh anum, kah quñupshaog otan.
59.7 Kusseh, kóhkonneauwáog ut wutt8n8wout, togkodteganash wussisset8n8wout: newutche (n8waog) howan n8tunk?
59.8 Qut ken woi Jehovah, kutahanehtauôog nnag: wame penuwohteaog kuttôontuhkonôog.
59.9 Newutche ummenuhkesuonk, kuttannôonsh, newutche God nuttusph8waonk[.]
59.10 Nummonaneteae Manitt8m nukqushoi monánumuk: God pish nunnohtinuk nukkodtantamoonk en nummatwomut.
59.11 Ahque paguas nagok, ishkont nummissinninnumog wunántamwog, kummenuhkesuonk suswohwonch nahog, n8kôhteash naghok, woi Jehovah nutogqunnéganun.
59.12 Newutche ummatcheseongan8 ut wutt8n8wóut, kah ukkutt8wongash ut wussisset8n8wout, tohqunach ut pittuánum8onganit, kah newutche matchenaneteáonk kah pann8waonk ne an8wahettit.
59.13 Machukis naghok kummusquantamunat, machukis, matta woh wuttinniéneau: kah wahteauhettich God nánaunnau Jakoboh, en aongkouohkomuk. Selah.
59.14 Kah wunnonk88k qushkehettich, kah nehnehteáhettich onatuh anumwut, & qunnupwsháhettich otan.
59.15 Nanwódtinneahhamwohettich meetsuonk, kah m8hm8skouáhettich asquam wamep8hetteg.
59.16 Qut nuttinn8homom kummenuhkesuonk, nux nummishont8wa8homom kummonaneteaonk nompoáeu: newutche ken nutusphouaonk, kah n8wonkônous wuttammepunnáon.
59.17 Kukket8homoush woi nummenuhkesuonk, newutche God nutusphowaonk, nummonaneteae Manitt8m.
60.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Shushan Eduth michtam} David, {kuhkootommuhkou ayeukonont Aram Naharaim kah Aram Zobab: Joab quashket, paguanau Edomitsoh oonaohteaouut salt, nabo neesit muttannonganogkussuoh.}
60.1 Woi God kuppogkesumun kussisw[à]uhkôsumun: kummusquanumimunnonup, woi qushkish wonk en nuhhogkanonut.
60.2 Kukquéquanehteam ohke, kussokshadtaun: neetskehtaash nishnoh ut pohqui, newutche nunnukshau.
60.3 Kenohtin kummissinninnumog siôgokish: k8tattamhimun quoshkussippâm8we wine.
60.4 Kuttinnumauoog nag quashhukqueaneg muttâag: onk woh pôpômush[á]numun newutche wunnomwaonk. Selah.
60.5 Noh wômônat woh pohquohwhunau: kuttinnôhkou pohquohwussitch, kah n8tah.
60.6 God unn8wop ut 8neetupanatam8onganit, n8wekontam: nuppaushinnu8 Sechem, nukquohquodhumun 8n8wohkói Succoth.
60.7 Gillead nuttaihe, kah Manasse nuttaihe, onk Ephraim ummenuhkesuonk nuppuhkuk: Judah ayeuont naumatuongoh.
60.8 Moab nukkutshitunk ohkuhquoh: nuttánuwohkou nummohkis ut Edom: Philistia weekontash ken newutche neen.
60.9 Howan woh pas8wit menuhki 8tanit? howan ás8wussit Edom?
60.10 Sunnummatta ken woi God, sohwhôkôseógkup? kah ken woi God, matta k8chaiyeúmunnónup ut nutayeuwohkonnanoweenut.
60.11 Aninnumaiinnean wutch wuttammepunnaonganit: newutche wutannoôsuonk wosketomp tohn8cheyeu8.
60.12 God aninnumungqueog pish nukquehtâèmun: newutche nnoh pish tashkuhkonau nummatwomunônoh.
61.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Neginoth ukketoohhomaonk} David.
61.1 NOOtah nummauonk woi God: kukkeihtash nuppeantamowonk.
61.2 Wutche aongkouohkomuk kummauunnitteoush, nuttah k8shkoshunk: uss8wusseh qussukquanit, ne anuwohquss8mukqueh.
61.3 Newutche ken nutonk8wohquass8, kah menuhki wonkonous wutche matwâut.
61.4 Pish nuttay keekit micheme: nuppabahtanum wutonkaúhtomuh kenuppawhunnog. Selah.
61.5 Newutche ken God ken8tam nukquoshômuaongash: kuttinninnumah wutahtaongan8 neg quóhtukeg k8wesuonk.
61.6 Ken kusepepomantamwah ketass8t: kah ukkodtumm8mash neane monatash pometeongash.
61.7 Pish appu anaquabit God micheme: woi nanashwunush monaneteaonk kah wunnomwaonk ne woh wodchanukquit.
61.8 Nemehkuh nuttinn8homom k8weesuonk micheme: onk woh asekesukokish nutussen nukquoshómuaongash.
62.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Jeduthun ukketoohhomaonk} David.
62.1 Webe nukketeahogkou annoôneau Goduh: noh wutch n8wadchanitteaonk.
62.2 Noh webe nukqussukquanum, kah n8wadchanitteaonk: noh nutusphouaonk, matta pish numm8cheke ontsappu.
62.3 Toh utt8che kenatwontamw8 woskehuwaonk wutch wosketomp? pish wame kenushitteamw8: onatuh qussukquaneneutunk kodn8kompskem8uk: kah onatuh kuhqushqueneutunk.
62.4 Webe weétuotuog penuhkonat wutche quttiánumaonganit, tapeneaumwog pann8wayeuongash: wunnaneteam8 wutt8n8: qut anomut matchenaneteaog.
62.5 Nukketeahogkou webe anôous God, newutche nutannoôsuonk wutchayeumó wuhhogkat.
62.6 Nagum webe nukqussukquanum, kah n8wadchanitteaonk, nagum nutusph8waonk, matta pish nutontsappu.
62.7 Ut Godut n8wadchanitteaonk kah nussohsum8wonk, ukqussukquanum nummenuhkeseuonk, nutusphuaónk ut Godut.
62.8 Pabahtanum8k nagwutteaeu kenaau missi[n]ninnuog: sokanum8k ketahhouwoash ut anaquabit, God kuttusphouaonganun. Selah.
62.9 Wu[ñ]amuhkut matche[k]eog tahn8chéyeuog, kah wutt8wosketompaog pann8wayeuog: quogquodwhut naghok, wamu môeu, ánue nunkinwog onk ne tahn8cheyeu8uk.
62.10 Ahque pabahtantam8k ut mukk8kinnuaonganit, ahque tahn8cheyeú8k kumm8towonganit: monak weenai[é]etuonk, ahque kuttahh8woog appehettich.
62.11 God wussinnu pasukqut, neesit nunn8tamun yeu, menuhkesuonk wutchaiyeum8 Godut.
62.12 Kah wonk ken Jehovah wutchayeum8 monaneteaonk: newutche kuttinongquodtauon nishnoh wosketomp neane anakausit.
63.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David {ait touohkomukqut Judah.}
63.1 WOi God ken num-Manitt8m, nompoaeu kenatinneawhush: nukketeahogkou kúhket8n kuhhog, n8weyaus kukkodtaânumuk, nunohtae kah kuhket8n8e ohke toh mo adt nuppên8g.
63.2 Naumunat kummenuhkesuonk kah kussohsumóonk neane mahche nau[u]nop ut kekit.
63.3 Newutche k8womoausuonk m8cheke wunnegen onk ne pomantamoonk: nusissitt8nash pish k8wâwu[ss]umuk.
63.4 Yeu kittinne waussumunun ash pomantam: nuttahshinum nunnutcheganash ut k8wesuonganit.
63.5 Nukketeahogkou pish tâpep8h onatuh nashpe wein kah weesuuk: kah nutt8n pish k8wâwussumuk nashpe weekontamwe nussissitt8nash.
63.6 Nehquanumunnon ut nutappinneat kah natwanumunnon nishnoh utt8che nukonáeu.
63.7 Newutche ken kutáninnumaiip: newajeh kenuppawhunog wutonkaohtom8 n8wekontam.
63.8 Nukketeahogkou kummenuhkodti neóhhuk: kuttinnohkou nukkogkôónuk.
63.9 Qut yeug natinneawhoncheg nukketeahogkôunoh nahunnushônat, pish auog wutchómuhqut.
63.10 Pish nushôog nashpe togkodtega[n]it: pish ummôwhôoh wonkqussissog.
63.11 Qut ketass8t pish wekontam ut Godut, pish wame waeénomaog chadchekeyeuánit nashpe wuhhogkuh, qut pann8wahettit wutt8n8ash pish kuppohhôsuash.
64.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk} David
64.1 NOOtash n8wàdtauatonkqussúonk woi God, ut nuppeantam8wonganit, wadcha[u]sh nukketeaonk wutch qushonat matwau.
64.2 Adtasheh wutch kéme ukken8nittuongan8wout matcheet8wog: n8waabetunkqu[n]naóont anakausitcheg matcheseonk[.]
64.3 Nah kehtattóog weenannu onatuh togkodteg, p8tonkunáog wutahtompeuh quosh[ô]hqunnumwog weesogkeyeuwongash.
64.4 Onk woh pumwáog kéme panuppu wunneet8oh: teanuk uppumwóuh matta wabesuog.
64.5 Nag wutt8máog wuhhogkauh wutche machik; ken8netuog wutch wunashónat kému appehanog n8waog, howan woh nógqueog?
64.6 Nag natinnehamwog matcheseongash usseog pannuppe natinneteaonk: nag wame né anomut ohtag, kah wuttahhou m8nói.
64.7 Qut god pish uppumwoh kôuhquodt, teanuk pish wutchadchetahwoh.
64.8 Nemehkuh pish nehenwonche weenannu uppenushátauneau ut wuhhogkaout: neg wame nauoncheg pish wussem8og.
64.9 Kah wame wosketompaog wabesuog, kah pish wahteauwahuwaog wutanakausuonk God: newutche pish waantamwe natwontamwog wutusseongash.
64.10 Sampweussecheg pish weekontam8unaog Jehovahoh, kah pish uppabahtanumouh: kah wame s[á]mpwutteahoncheg pish waeenoáog.
65.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt: Ukketoohhomaonk} David.
65.1 Waeenomuwaonk kutannóonukqun woi God, ut Sion: kah quoshauaonk pish kittinhittean.
65.2 Woi ken n8taman peantamoonk, wame weyaus pish kuppeyaónukqun.
65.3 Matcheseongash nutaumskunkqunash: qut nummatcheseonganash pish kutjiskhomunash.
65.4 Wunnanumau noh pepenauadt, kah noh pas8adt, onk woh k8weetomuk ut keekit: pish n8wamepumun k8neetuonk ut keekit k8neetupanatamwe Temple.
65.5 Nashpe uhqunneunkquokish sampweusseonganit, kenamp8ho[m]aiimun, woi God n8wadchanitteaonganun: uspuhh8waonk pajeh wame aongkouohkomukquash: kah neg aitcheg nôadtit kehtahhanit.
65.6 Nahspe ummenuhkesuonk manuhkehteunk wadchuash, puttukquo[b]ussit menuhkesuonk.
65.7 Chequnehteau wadtauatunkqussuonk keitoh: 8wadtauatonkqussuongan8 tukk8og, kah 8wogkâeongan8 missinninnuog.
65.8 Kah nag wadohkitcheg onkouohkomuk, wabesuontamwog kuhkinneasuongash: mohtompanaeu, sohhamunah, kah wunnonkwaeu k8weekontamwahuwám.
65.9 Kenatauohtóh ohke, kah kutogquechittauun: k8nogquehtaun nashpe wussepeum God ne numwohtau nippe: kukquoshaeihtau[ó/o]og weatchimiñeash, mahche yeuin quaquashweihtaman.
65.10 M8cheke kutogquechitoh wonitchuhhongash, kutasetahteanum ohke, ken8keteauun nashpe sókanon, k8nantamun ne noh adt sonkuk.
65.11 Kutchetuhquabenoh kodtumm8 nashpe k8neetuonk, kummayut padtippashin wunnogk8onk.
65.12 Padipashin maskehtuash ut touohkomuk: kah wadchuemesash weekontam8m8ash waéenu.
65.13 Wunnádtupp8ongan88ash wunohkukkomunnáoash monacheg floksog, kah 8naohkôaouash pashanahteau weatchiminneash, mishe weekontamwog, kah ket8hhomôog.
66.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ketoohmaonk}
66.1 WEeketongqusseg ut Godut, wame muttaók.
66.2 An8hamunk quttianatam8onk 8wesuonk: sohsumwahtau8k tabuttantamauaonk.
66.3 Unn8k God, toh kittinne uhqueneunkqus ut kutánakausuonganit? newutche missi kummenuhkesuonk, kummatwomog woskeche kuttit k8namptunkquog.
66.4 Wame muttaok pish k8wowussumuk, kah pish kukket8homungquog, pish unn8homoog k8wesuonganit. Selah.
66.5 Peyunk naum8k wutanakausuongash God, noh ohqunneongquotash wuttinheaongásh wosketompaog wunnaumonaoh.
66.6 Kehtoh ayim nu[n]obohteai: pomushopanneg tomogkonit wusseet8wout; na nuttit weekontam8unnanónúp.
66.7 Noh nanawunnum nashpe ummenuhkesuonk micheme, wuskesukquash naum88ásh wutohtimoneash: ohquontogig nananuaonk ahque misheheahettich wuhhogkauh. Selah.
66.8 Woi wunnanumok num-Manitt8mun kenaau missinninnuog, ayimau wuttauatongqussue tabuttantamoonk n8tamounnat.
66.9 N noh kókônunont nukketeahogkóunnun8noh ut pomantam8onganit: kah katta unnantam8 ontohtaj nussetinonash.
66.10 Newutche ken woi God, kukqutchhimunnonup: kukqutchhimunnonup onatuh silver quajteomuk.
66.11 Kuppas8umunnonup hashabput, kupponumaiimun nuppisquaninnonut ohquommom8wonk.
66.12 Kutayeu wosketompaog wunnayeumukqunnaoont nuppuhkukqun, nuppannupwushaumun n8htau, kah nuppanupwushaumun nuppekontu qut ken kuppas88mun weenaeetuohkomukqut.
66.13 Nuttom keekit weeche chikohtae mag8ongash kuttâadtuhkaush kukquoshaumunn8wongash.
66.14 Nish nussissit8nash an8wohpash, kah nutt8n an8wohpash wadtamehpunaon.
66.15 Kittinninnumaush chikohsue mag8ongash wees, kah ramse weekemungquok: kittinnumaush oxinog kah goatsog. Selah.
66.16 Nonche n8tam8k wame kenaau quoshogish God, kah nussamp8am uttoh asehtauomp nukketeahogkounoh.
66.17 Nummauunnitteau nashpe nutt8nut kah mishsheheop nashpe neenan.
66.18 Womontamon matcheseongash ut nuttahhut, matta God woh nunn8tunk8h.
66.19 Qut wunnamuhkut nunn8tunk God: kuhkeihtam n8wadtauatongqussue peantam8onk.
66.20 OOnanumunach God: matta quashkenumaeg en nuppeantam8onganit, asa ummonaneteaonk wutch nuhhogkat.
67.0 {Nohtumpuhpequodt ut Neginoth ukketoohomaonk.}
67.1 GOD monanuminnean, kah wunnanuminnean: wuskesuk wôsumungquttuh. Selah.
67.2 Onk woh wahteoun kummay ut muttaohkit, kah k8wadchanum8onk kenugku wame wutohtimóneash.
67.3 Missinninnuog waeenomugqush woi God, wame missinninnuog waeenomugqush.
67.4 Woi wutohtimoneunk weekontamohettich, weekontam8homahettich, newutche pish k8sum missinninnuog sampwe: kah pish kenanaa[n]num wutahtimoneash ut muttaohkit. Selah.
67.5 Missinninnuog waeenomugqush woi God: wame missinninnuog waeenomugqush.
67.6 Neit pish ohke mishummeechummu: kah God kum-Manitt8mun pish k8nanumugqun.
67.7 God pish k8nanumugqun, kah wame aongkouohkomuk pish ukqushóoh.
68.0 {Nohtumpuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk} David.
68.1 Neepauitch God, ummatwomoh seahwhonch: kah wonk neg sekeneaoncheg wussemohettich wutch anaquabit.
68.2 Onatuh pukit pt8hog, neinne nen8hkau naghog: onatuh wax mohtupohtag ut n8taut, nein paguanehettich matcheetowog ut anaquabit God.
68.3 Qut wunnomwaenuog weekontamwehettich: weekontamohettich ut anaquabit God, nux, m8cheke weekontamohettich.
68.4 Ket8hamok God an8hamunk waeenom8ongash ut 8wesuonganit: mishehheuk n noh na8mukqut kesuk, nashpu 8wesuonk JAH: kah weekontam8k ut anaquabit.
68.5 Mowadt8sheg na 8shoh, sekousquaog 8sumugkouoh, God 8neetupanatamwu ayeuonganit.
68.6 God ponamauau nonsiyeu8oh weechinnumonát sohh8wunau wehweepapissumutcheh m8wóhshogquohtogquosh, qut ohquoantogig nananuwaonk wutohtuog nunnobohtéaouut.
68.7 Woi God sohh8wunnat negonohkouadt kummissinninnumog: panupwuhaan touohkom[u]k. Selah.
68.8 Ohke quequanup, kesukquash punnemoash ut anaquabit God, Sinai, ut anaquabit God um-Manitt8moh Israel.
68.9 Ken woi God kuttann8n mishe sokanon, uttoh adt menehketeauop kutohke sauunum8m8ug.
68.10 Kummukineonk 8tohkinneaop: ken woi God kukquoshaeihtau mátcheeku, wutche k8neetuonganit.
68.11 Jehováh unn8wau kutt8wonk: monaog wunn8tamwahuwoneau.
68.12 Kehtass8tamwog wutayeuwehteom8woh kenuppe wussem8og: káh mittumwussis n8titteadt, chadchapenum máchehteaumuk.
68.13 Mukk8kône n8wetsum8moneau ahkukquog, qut pish kutogqunneunkqussimw8 wunnuppawhunnit wsk8wanon aqut Silver, kah ummequnoh wesôag gold.
68.14 Wamemanuhkesu soswohwhont kehtass8timwoh na ut wompiyeup onatuh k8unit ut Salmon.
68.15 OOwadchum God, onatuh wadchu Bashan, kussohkoi wadchu onatuh wadchu Bashan.
68.16 Tohwutch quesháog kenaau kussohkoaeu wadchuog? yeu wadchu God kontantog 8tohkinneat, nux Jehovah ummicheme wutohkin.
68.17 Wuttatuppequanumukquaash God neesneechagut muttannunganu8ash,m8cheke mattanunganogkussuoh Angelsog: God 8weamukshanoh ut Sinai: wunneetupanatamwe weekit.
68.18 Kuttuspeup en ongkouwu, kummisinohteam missinnohkonunk, kutattumunumup ummag8onganooash wosketompaog, nux, wutch ahquoanitogig nananuwaonk, onk woh Lord god weechayeumoh.
68.19 OOnanumunach God asekesukokish k8n8washhikqun, Manit n8wadchanitteaonganun. Selah.
68.20 N noh wâmanitt8meog, n noh wadchanuwae Manit, kah God Manit wutchayeum8 pohquohhamoongash wutche nuppowonganit.
68.21 Qut pish God chadchetahhom uppuhkukk8 ummatwomoh: kah quánonuhquoánt n noh aiont ummatcheseonganit.
68.22 God n8wau pish nukqushkeaheoog wutch Bashan, nuppas8woog wutch monaiyeuut kehtahannit.
68.23 Kusseet woh mussishin 8sheaongan8out kumma[t]womog, kah wenann8 kuttiog [nunan].
68.24 Naumwog kutauonganash, woi God, wutauonganash num-Manitt8m, nukketass8tim8m ut wunneetupanatamwe weetuomut.
68.25 Ket8homwaenuog negonshauog, puhpequaenuog wutasukauouh, kenugku nag penompaog puhpequahtog timbrelsash.
68.26 Wunnanum8k God ut mukkinneaonganit, Manit wutch tohkekomuwu Israel.
68.27 Na wuttappen peississit Benjamin, weeche wunnananuaeneum8uh, wussontimosumoh Judah, kah kôn8s8acheg, wussontimomoh Zabulon, kah wussontimomoh Naphthali.
68.28 Kum-Manitt8m ken8tamup kummenuhkesuonk: menuhketeaush, woi God[,] ne aséansheagup.
68.29 Newutche kuttempleum ut Jerusalem ketass8timwog pish kuppaudtunkquog mag8ongash.
68.30 Auskom quáqunnontugqutcheg, monacheg bullsog, kah kalfse missinninnuog, nonchemaghettit silver: siswah missinninnuog, weekontogig mattompog.
68.31 Sontimoog wutch sohhomwog wutch Egypt, Ethiopia teanuk pish summagunnumwog wunnutcheganooash en Godut.
68.32 Ket8homok God kenaau as8tam8ongash muttaohket, woi ket8ham8k waeenom8ongash Jehovah. Selah.
68.33 Noh na8mukqut ongkoue ohohtag kesuk, na negonneyeu8gkup, kusseh mishont8wau, kah ne mishe mishont8waonk.
68.34 Samp8ak ummenuhkesuonk God, 8netuonk waabappehtauau Israel, kah ummenuhkesuonk matohkqsut.
68.35 Woi God, kutohqunneongqus wutch k8netupanatamwe appuonganit; um-Manitt8moh Israel noh anumaont ummissiñinnumoh menuhkesuonk kah tapenum8onk, wunnanumunach God.
69.0 {Notompuhpequodt ut Shoshannim ukketoohomaonk} David.
69.1 Wadchaneh, woi God: newutche nippeash petutteaum8ash nukketeahogkounut.
69.2 Nupwohkehch8am mónói pissohquanuhtu, matta woh neep[a]u[ôú]muk, nuppeam m8nompagwut uttoh adt nukkokqsin.
69.3 Nusauanum wutch nummauonk, nukquttunk nunnohteau, nuskesukquash sauunum8m8ash, ánoónog num-Manitt8m.
69.4 Nag sekeneaitcheg tahn8che, monaog onk ne nummeesuonk ahtahshik: nag kodnushikqueoneg, nummatwomog tahn8che, menuhkesuog: neit nunnompinnumun wonk ne matta neemanummoup.
69.5 Woi God k8wahteoh nummattammagweseonk; kah nummatcheseongash matta kutassompatamm8.
69.6 Nag anóonukquéaneg woi Lord Jehovah ayeutaunit, ahque akodchhettich newutche neen: nag natineóhukquéaneg ahque quequenaúanumwehettich newutche neen, woi um-Manitt8moh Israel.
69.7 Newaj, newutche ken, nukkekómukquog, akodchuonk puttaghum nuskesuk.
69.8 Nuppenowohteau ut neematut, kah nu[ppp]enowohteau ut nokas wunneechanit.
69.9 Newutche nuszelum ut keékit numm8hhuk: kah ukkekomuwaongan8 neg kekomukquéaneg n8chepunaùmukqunnau.
69.10 Mauon, kah áhhohpadt nukketeahogkou nashpe mat meetseonk, ne nukkekomitteáonk.
69.11 Numman8tiónakin hogk8unam hogk8: kah nuttehinohkunukqunneau.
69.12 Nag apitcheg anómsquoant nummamatchenukquog: kah nashp8hum8og nuhhog kogkeissippamwaenuog.
69.13 Qut neen kuppeantamoush woi Jehovah tapeneamanish: woi God ut monakish kummonaneteaongash n8tah, ut wunnamuhkuteyeúe k8wadchánuwáonk.
69.14 Pohquohwusseh wutch wunnumwiyeuut, kah ahque kuttauweti: pohquohwusseh wutch nag sekeneaitcheg, kah wutch n8nompagwut.
69.15 Ahque anéuhkauitch tomogkon, kah ahque m8nôi misseaashquoasit, kah páhsahtheg ahque kupwamwitch ut wutt8nut.
69.16 N8tah woi God, newutche k8womoausúonk wunnegen, qushkish en nuhhogkat neane monak kukkitteamonteaneteáeu monaneteaongash.
69.17 Kah ahque puttogwhush kuskesuk wutch kuttinninneumut, newutche n8tamehpunam, teanuk n8tah.
69.18 Pasosukau nukketeahogkou, kah pohquáwhus: pohquawusseh newutche nummatwomog.
69.19 K8wahteoun nukkekómitteaonk, kah nutakodchúonk kah nummishauanumitteaonk, wame nummatwomog anaquábean.
69.20 Kekómitteaonk wutch pokshau nuttah kah nuhhogkat numwohteau onkquanum8onk: kah nutôanóus howan woh nahtunkinneiit, qut wanne howan, kah mánetimmew[á]cheg, qut wane howan namheuh.
69.21 Kah nutassamukquog weswe noh nittin meechinneat: kah kúhkutt8non n8tattamhukquog sée wine.
69.22 Wuttablum8 ahpehhanneu8utch anaquabhettit: kah n[e]woh wanégikup ahpehhanne[á]8uach.
69.23 Pogkénumwóhettich, ut wushkesukkouwout onk woh monaumóog: kah nagwutteaeu nunnuksho[n]sh wusségonnohtogk88ash.
69.24 Sókanuttau kutjishánumaonk, kummuttae musuantamoonk tohqunukquéhettich
69.25 Wutáyeuongan8 wanne howaunun8utch: wanne howaununn8utch wek.
69.26 Newutche sasamakoúhwadt, 8waskheouh: kah weattimáhettit, umm8skheouh neh chadchetahwodcheh.
69.27 Ponamau sasamakuhhuwáonk wutch ummatcheseongan8: kah ahque petutteahettich kussampweseonganit.
69.28 Nag jishkuhwunach 8sukkuhwhongan8 pamântogig: kah ahque wetsukwhoshettich sampweusseaenuwud.
69.29 Qut nummatchek kah nunneuantam: k8wadchanuwaonk, woi God, qunnunkquappehikquttei.
69.30 K8woweenodtum 8weesuonk God ket8homaonganit: kah nummishsheh nashpe waeenomaonk.
69.31 Kah yeu en wussikkutteahukqut Jehovah, onk noh ox asa bullok noh wadaskonit kah wôhkassit.
69.32 Manunnissuog yeu pish wunnaumunneau, kah pish weekontamwog kah pish kuttahhou pomantamomou kenaau natinneawhog God.
69.33 Newutche Jehovah n8tauau matchekuoh, kah matta jishánumoou kobshagkinausinutcheh.
69.34 Kesuk kah ohke waussumahettich neh, keitoh kah nishnoh teag naut momonchemoug.
69.35 Newutche God pohquohwuttau Sion, kah pish 8tanahteau ut Judah, onk nag woh 8tohkinneau, kah woh wutahtaunau.
69.36 Kah wunneech[a]n8oh wuttinnúm8oh, pish wutohtaunneau nahohtôeu 8shuoh: kah wamontogig 8wesuonk na pish 8tohkinneau.
70.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt, ukketoohhomaonk} David. {koowaantamwahukqunnan}.
70.1 Teanuk pohquohwusseh woi God, teanuk aninnumah woi Jehovah.
70.2 Nag akodjhettich, kah quequenauanumwéhettich natinneawhoncheg nukketeahogkóunoh: qushkehettich, kah akodjhettich neg kodwoskéhukqueaneg.
70.3 Nah qushkéhettich, ne wutonkqu[a]tunkan8 wutakodchuongan8 an8wacheg, Ho, ho.
70.4 Yeug wame natinneóhukqueaneg nag weekontamm8ónukqush, kah muskouanatamm8onukqush: kah neg womontogig k8wadchanuaonk nagwutteaeu n8wahettich God mishshehhenach.
70.5 Qut neen nummatcheek kah nukquenáhuk, kenupshash en nuhhogkat woi God; ken nutannósuéneum, kah nuppohquohwussueneum, woi Jehovah ahque sepohteash.
71.1 Kuppabahtanumush woi Jehovah, ahque quequenauanumitti.
71.2 Pohquawusseh ut k8nomwauseonganit, kah pohquohhumwáhe: kuhkeihtah kah wadchaneh.
71.3 Ken menuhkaj nutáyeuonk, uttoh woh adt nagwutteáe wuñaiyee: kutann8teamup k8wadchaneat; newutche ken nukqussukquanum kah n8wonkónous.
71.4 Pohquawusseh woi num-Manitt8m wutch wunnutcheganout matcheetowog: wutch wunnutcheganout mat wunnomwausseaen, kah nushehteaen.
71.5 Newutche ken nutannoósuonk woi Lord God: ken kuppabahtanumush, wutch n8skenúunneat.
71.6 Kutashineup wutch ôontomukqut, ken was8wéan nokas wunnogkussit, nagwutteaeu k8waeenomush.
71.7 Neen onatuh monchanatam8onk wutch m8nacheg: qut ken menuhki nutusphouwaonk.
71.8 Nutt8nuit numwohtaj k8waweenomutteaonk, kah kukquehtianumitteaonk qunnikesuk.
71.9 Ahque pohkeseh ut nukkehchiyeuunneat, ahque ohquanumeh nummenuhkesuonk mahchem88uk.
71.10 Newutche nummatwomog num̃atchenukquog kah nag askwhononcheg nukketeahogkôunuh ken8nittuog.
71.11 N8waog, God wutahquanumoh: wunómohtuhkau kah tohqun, newutche matta howan uppohquohwhunoh
71.12 Woi God ahque nô8sukah, woi num-Manitt8m, teauk ani[u]numah.
71.13 Quequenauanumwehettich, kah mohtuppaehettich matwahettit wutch nukketeahogkôunoh: kekontuonk kah mishananittuonk hogquehettich, kah woskehetcheg.
71.14 Qut nagwutteaeu nuttannous, & wonk nano k8woweenomsh yauyatche.
71.15 Nutt8n pish natitteau k8nomwausseonk, kah k8wadchanuwaonk qunnikesuk, newutche matta n8wahteau8h toh adtahshik.
71.16 Nuttom ummenuhkesuonganit Manit Jehovah: n8wahteauwahuam k8nomwausseonk ken webe.
71.17 Woi God kukkuhk8tomah wutch n8skenuunneat: kah toh yeu pajeh n8wahteauwáhuwam kummonchanatamwanakausuongas[k].
71.18 Kah yeuyeu kohchiyeueh kah wompoquoi, woi God, ahque ohquanumeh nô pajeh wahteauwahuwaon yeu ut pometuonganit kummenuhkesuonk, kah kuttapenum8onk neg wame paoncheg.
71.19 Kah k8nomwausseonk, woi God, qunnuhquohteau noh mashanakausit: woi God, howan anunkquean?
71.20 Ken nátissean mishsheu kah onkquommommu wuttanmepunaonk*, wonk pish kukketeaheh, kah pish wonk kukkódtinne wutch m8n[a]iyeuut ohke.
71.21 Pish kummishteoh nummissugkenuonk, kah pish k8weekontamwahhe wéenu.
71.22 Kah k8woweenomsh nashpe psaltery, n8waweenodtum k8nomwaonk: woi num-Manitt8m, kukket8homoush nashpe harp, woi ken wunneetupanatamwaen ut Israel.
71.23 Nussisset8nash pish mishe weekontam8m8ash, ket8homaunon, kah nukketeahogkou pohquohwhunop.
71.24 Kah neenan pish keket8kau k8nomwausseonk qunikesuk: newutche nag quequenauánumôog, nag akodchuag kodwoskehetcheg.
72.0 {Ketoohomaonk wutche} Solomon.
72.1 Aninnumau ketass8t k8sittum8ongash, woi God, kah k8nomwausseonk ketass8t wunnaumonuh.
72.2 Noh pish wussumau kummissinninnumoh en wunnomwausseonganit, kah kummatchekumog, wussittum8onganit.
72.3 Wadchuash pish paudtoog wunnohteaonk en missinninnutu, kah wadchuwemesash nashpe wunnomwausseonk.
72.4 Pish wussumau matchekuoh ut missinninnutu, pish wadchanau wunnechan8oh quenahukqutcheg, kah pish sokqshanau woskehuwaenuh.
72.5 Nag pish kukqushhukquog nishokke nuppauzsauk kah nanepaushadto8k, pannuppu wame pometuonganit.
72.6 Pish enunn8keu onatuh sokanunk ut sashquonkanit: onatuh sokanon agwachippadtunk ohke.
72.7 Aspomantog wunomwausseog pish wunayeuogig; kah monat wunnogteaonk neanuhque nepauzsauk.
72.8 Kah pish nanauúnnum yeadt ketahhanuuk: kah yeawutch sepuut onk yeáen aongkouohkomuk.
72.9 Neg wadohkitcheg tóuohkomuk, pish nauaeog ut anaquabit: kah ummatwomoh n8n8squodtamog puppissai.
72.10 Tass8tamwog wutch Tarshish kah munnohhannehtu, nag pish padtauog mag8ongash: tass8tamwog wutch Sheba kah Seba pish mag8og mag8ongash
72.11 Nux wame ketass8tamwog pish naaieog ut anaquabit: wame wutahtimoneunk pish 8wowussumouh.
72.12 Newutche pish pohquohwunau quenahukqunutcheh maunitteungqut: kah wonk matcheku, kah noh matta wodtannunneumwonkaneg.
72.13 Noh pish wohqônumau matchekuoh kah quenahukqunutcheh: kah pish wadchanau ukketeahogkon8oh quenahukqutcheg.
72.14 Pish pohquohwunau ukketeahogkoun8oh wutch as8k[e]kodteamowonganit, & woskehuwaonganit: kah 8squeheongan8 mishoadtu ut anaquabit.
72.15 Kah pish pomantam, kah gold wutch Sheba pish aninnumauun: kah nag pish úppeantamwonshauh nagwutteaeu, kah asekesukokish waeenomau.
72.16 Na pish yeonitchamunyeu8 ohkeit ut woskeche wadchuohkontu, ummeechummu8onk pish nunnukshau onatuh Lebanon: kah neg otanit pish wushketuog onatuh ashkoshqut, ut ohkekontu.
72.17 OOwesuonk michémoheau: 8wesuonk nagwutteohteau neane nepauzsauk: kah wosketompaog 8nanumóog ut wuhhogkat, kah wame wutohtimoneash pish wuttussowenouh 8nanumau.
72.18 OOnanumau Lord God, um-Manitt8 noh Israel, noh webe asit monchanatam8ongash.
72.19 Kah 8nanittamunach wussohsumm8angane 8wesuonk micheme; kah muttaohket numwohtaj wussohsumóonk. Amen kah Amen.
72.20 Uppeantam8ongash David wunnaumonuh Jesse, neit wohkukquohshin.
73.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
73.1 WUnnamuhkut God wunneneheau Israel, neg pahketeahoncheg.
73.2 Qut neen, nusseetash ômog t8nequshinneash: nutontannehtuongash omog t8nequshaash.
73.3 Newutch nutishkôônomp as8tuog, naumon 8naiyeuonk matchetowog.
73.4 Newutche wanne wehwhepappisseog ut wunnupp8ongan8out: qut ummenuhkesuongan8 menuhki.
73.5 Matta nag wuttammepunoog onatuh onkatogane: asuh matta wesauashauoog neane onkatogane.
73.6 Newutche pittuanumoonk 8wéenuhkouh onatuh móoshagquohtogqut: 8woskhuaongan8 hogk8og onatuh hogk8onganit.
73.7 Mogquskesukquaog wutche wunnogk8onk anuweetuog onk woh ne kodtantog metah.
73.8 Nag aninwog, kah matcheyéuog papaume woskehuwaonk, pittuwaog.
73.9 Wutt8n8 ayeuuhkônittue ponauwog kesukquéhtu, & wenañu pannupshaum8 ohkit.
73.10 Newajeh ummissinninnumoh yeu en qushkenit: kah nippe numwohteau sénumauoneau naghok.
73.11 Onk nag n8wàog, uttoh God wuttinwahteaun? kah wahteauonk sun wuhhogkat ohteau quanonkqappit?
73.12 Kusseh yeug matta anauongig Godoh, nag wunnaiyeuog ut muttaohkit, nag onchenaietuog.
73.13 Wunnamuhkut nuppaketeoh nuttah tahn8che, kah nukkussenitcham matwoskhu[a]onganinn8g.
73.14 Newutche n8wesauwusham qunnikesuk, kah nussasamakouwhit as[m]ohtompogish.
73.15 N8waon, yeu woh nussin, kusseh woh nummatchenehteoh uppométuongan8 keneechanog.
73.16 Yeu kodwahteauon, yeu siogkanakausuonk ut nuskesukqut,
73.17 Onk nô pajeh aoon 8neetupanatamwe weekit God, nenutit wohtamunat 8wohkukquoshinn8ongan8,
73.18 Wunnamuhkut nag kupponóog t8nequohteaouut: nag kuppinuhko[n]unk en paguaninneat.
73.19 Uttoh wuttin teanuk paguaninneau? pannuppu mohtuppaeog nashpe quequenauanum8ongash.
73.20 Onatuh anukquonk t8hkeit: woi Manit, t8hkean pish kutohquanittam wuttinnussuongan8.
73.21 Yeu nuttah wuttinneuánatamun; kah nukanukehteáwhutteap ut nutt8unussit.
73.22 Yeu nuttin as8kinneáh, kah mat n8wahteau8unáh: nutogquinneunkqussip puppinashimwut, ut anaquabean.
73.23 Qut nagwutteaeu k8weetomsh: kenutcheg nuttannuk nuttinohkôunit.
73.24 Kussomsháseh nashpe kuhkinn8suwonk: onk pish ompetagk kutattamunneh en kussohsum8onganit.
73.25 Howan wadtihee ut kesukqut webe ken? kah matta howan nutahchewonamoh yeu ut muttaohket webe ken.
73.26 N8weyaus, kah nuttah s[a]unumwog: qut God ukqussukquánumoh nuttah, kah nutchippiyeum micheme.
73.27 Newutche kusseh, nag n[o]8sukkongquéaneg, pish paguanúog: nag kuppaguanopanneg mamussitcheg wutch kuhhogkat.
73.28 Qut nen, wunnegen nuppas8sukauónat God: nuppabahtanum Manit Jehovah, onk woh n8tamwáhuwam wame kutanakausuongash.
74.0 {Maschil ut} Asaph.
74.1 WOi God tohwuch sohwóhkôseog micheme? tohwutch kummusquanittam8onk ayeuhkonáe pukittauúok ut sheepsut kenadtupp8wonganit?
74.2 Mehquontash kummikkinneonk, nôadt tabhumóp: souobpunk ne kutahtóonk ne man8hhomóp, yeu wadchúwe Sion ne wodohkéop.
74.3 Tahshinish kusseetash en nagwutteáeu paguanuongash: wame ne matchese asit matwau ut k8neetupanatamwu keekit.
74.4 Kummatwômog nishketunkqussúog ut nôeu kummukkinneonganehtu: tahshinnumwog ummittaákinn88sh wutch kuhkinneasuongash.
74.5 Wosketomp wáeenomp neane wuttogkunk tahshinuk ut metugk8kontu.
74.6 Qut yeuyeu tummethamwog mamansukwhongane anakausuongash moáeu, nashpe togkungash kah hammersash.
74.7 Unnuhteáog n8tau k8neetupanatamwe kekit, wunnisketeaúunnéau wutahtuonk k8wesuonganit, uppenuhkoneau en ohkekontu.
74.8 N8waog ut wuttahh8wóut, nag paguanontuh moáeu: nag wame chikohsumwog uppeantamwakomukquash God ut ohkeit.
74.9 Matta naum8mun nukkehkinneasuonganunnonash, wanne wonk manittowomp[a]no, asa matta howan kenugke nenawun, 8wahteaouun uttoh utt8che?
74.10 Woi God tohutt8che pish matwau kekóm8wau? sun pish matwau blasphemau k8wesuonk micheme?
74.11 Tohwutch wutóntinnumun kenutcheg, kuttinnohkou? wutontinush wutch kupp8chenauóunut.
74.12 Newutche God nukketass8timom nukkonneayeú8, ayik wadchánuwaonk ut nóeu ohkeit.
74.13 Kutchachaubenamup keihtoh nashpe kummenuhkêsuonk: kuppohquetahham uppuhkuk88ash p8tahpaog ut nippekontu.
74.14 Kussukquohtahhom uppuhkuk Leviathan: kah kuttinnumau ummeetsuongan8 missinninnúog wodohkutcheg touohkomuk.
74.15 Kuppohshittahham tohkékomuash kah tomogkon: kenunappéhteóh moge sepuash.
74.16 Kesukod kuttaihe, kah nukon wonk kuttaihe, kukquoshaeihtau wequai, kah nepauz.
74.17 Wame kupponum wunnashinniinnash ohke: kuttaiyim sequan kah popón.
74.18 Yeu mehquoantash, matwau kehkontuk, woi Jehovah; kah as8tuog missinninnáog blasphemaog k8wesuonk.
74.19 Woi ahque magish ukketeahogkôunoh turtle k8skuhwhanannom en monácheg: ahque wanánum ummukkinnéonk kummatchekeum micheme.
74.20 Mehquantash k8n8wáonk, newutche pohkenáoash ut ohkeit, wunnumwohteau wutohtu8ash mukk8kinneaenuog.
74.21 Noh waskhit, woi ahque qushkeitch akodchinát: matchekuog, kah quenaihukqutcheg waeenodtummohettich k8wesuonk.
74.22 Omkish, woi God, ken8tamwóntash kuttinnaiyeúonk: mehquontash as8tu kukkekomuk asekesukokish.
74.23 Ahque wanantash 8wadtauatongqussuongan8 kummatwomog: 8wogkoueongan8 nag ayeuuhkonittue waábetunkquéaneg náno missi nagwutteáeu.
75.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Altaschith: Ukketoohhomaonk} Asaph.
75.1 Kuttabuttantamaúunumun, woi God, kuttabuttantamaúunumun, newutche k8wesuonk paswôhteau, kummonch[á]natame anakausuonganash ne nahtitteaúm8.
75.2 Attumunnumon mukkinnéonk, pish nussampwe wussitum.
75.3 Ohke, kah wame neg noh wodohkutcheg saupás8og: nukkogk[ô]nnum ohkekonnumuk.
75.4 Nuttin as8tuog, ahque as8ke ussek, kah matcheetowog, ahque tohshin8k askon.
75.5 Ahque qunnunkqueu tahshin8k kutaskonn8wóog: ahque ket8hkunk nashpe chétaeu missittupuk.
75.6 Newutche wutt8anatuonk matta wutch wutchepwâóu, asa mat wutchéksuau, asa mat wutch sôúnnâeu.
75.7 Qut God wussittumwáen, pasuk8h kepúhteau, onkatogu omohkinaau.
75.8 Newutche wunnetcheganit Jehovah, noh wuttattamwáitchú8, kah wine musqui: numwaeu kenittepâunausu, onk ne wussékenumun: qut niskeneunkquok ohteau appésinit, wame matcheetowog ut muttaohket pish senuppânumauoneau, onk pish 8tattamunneau.
75.9 Qut nen nunnaihtitteam micheme: nuttinn8hhomon tabuttantam8onk ut um-Manitt8mut Jakob.
75.10 Onk wame wutáskon8oh matcheetowog nuttummetahwôog: qut wutaskonóuh s[a]mpweusséaenuog pish tohshinôog.
76.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Neginoth: Ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
76.1 GOD waheau Jodah: 8wesuonk missi ut Israel.
76.2 Onk week ohtau Salem, kah wutohtu Sion.
76.3 Nawuttit póhquenumun kôûhquodtash kah ahtompeh, ogqunneg kah togkodteg, kah ayeuwuttuonk. Selah.
76.4 Ken kumm8cheke sóhsum onk n nash mukk8kinnuwontamwe wadchúash.
76.5 Manúhketeahoncheg woskehéog, kouéog ukkoúeongan8: onk matta howan menuhkesu namehteau wunnutcheash.
76.6 Auskómuwáan, woi um-Manitt8moh Jakob, tatuppequânumog kah horsesog moáeu nupp8e kouéog.
76.7 Ken, ken woh kukqushit: kah howan woh neepau ut anaquabean musquánittamanish?
76.8 Ken8tamwahuwam wussittum8onk wutch kesukqut: muttaohke wabeseup kah chequnappúp.
76.9 Omohket God wussumont, onk woh wadchanau wame manunnissuoh ut muttaohkeit. Selah.
76.10 Wunnamuhkut ummusquantamóonk wosketomp pish k8wôweekomuk: ne asqueiyeu8g musquanittuonk ne k8tammehtean.
76.11 Quoshaum8k kah âadtúhkók Jehovah kum-Manitt8m8: wame neg wéinapitcheg paudtok mág8ongash noh woh quóhshit.
76.12 Noh pish tummehtahwhau wunnashauaongan8uh Santimôog: noh uhqunneunkqussu ut ketass8timwut ut muttaohket.
77.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Jeduthun, Ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
77.1 Nummaúunnitteau God nashpe n8wadtaúatongqussúonk, en Godut nashpe n8wadtaúatonkqussuonk, onk nukkeihketongkup.
77.2 Wadtamehpunnáan natwánam God: nukkehkechesuonk manéyeu8k nukonáeu, kah matta ohqutchúwanunn8: nukketeahogkou sekeneam pôanatamweheonat.
77.3 Nummequânumomp God, kah n8tamánatamup: n8tapóhsinneáh, kah nunnashaúonk nukkonchuwannup. Selah.
77.4 K8wôshwahtôh nuskésukquash: n8wsaume wuttamánatam, onk woh wanne nuttápenum8 ket8hkon.
77.5 Nunnatwóntamup nôadt aquompákup, kah kodtum8ash nóadt.
77.6 Nummehquantam nukket8homaonk nukkonáeu, nukkéket8hkau nehenwonche nuttah, kah nunnashaúonk menuhkodtinneohteau.
77.7 Sun micheme pish pogkes8au Jehovah? & sun matta wonk woh kitteamonteanitteaou?
77.8 Sun ummonáneteaonk micheme ámaémouk, quoshaumuaonk sun micheme panushano?
77.9 God sun wanántam ukkitteamonteánikónat: musquantog sun kuppóhhom ukkitteamonteánitteáeu kitteamonteanitteáonk. Selah.
77.10 Kah nussin, yeu nunn8chumwesuonk: qut nummehquantam wuttinnohkôunne ukkodtum8mash quanunkquappit.
77.11 Nummehquantam wutanakausuongash Jehovah: wunnamuhkut nummehquantam kenukkonne kummonchánatammuongash.
77.12 Nunnatwontam wame kutanakausuonk: kah n8weogquttum kutusseongash.
77.13 Kummay, woi God, en k8neetupanatamwe kekit, howan newuttinn8hqueu Manitt8in ne anukkenuk kum-Manitt8mun?
77.14 Ken God monchanatamwe usséan, k8wahteauwahuwam kummenuhkesuonk kenugke missinninnúut.
77.15 Kuppohquohwhunomp kummissinninnumog nashpe kuppit, wunnaumonuh Jakob, kah Joseph. Selah.
77.16 Nippe kenaúkup, woi God, nippe kenaukup: nag wabesúpanneg, kah mônâouash wuttammepunnom8pash.
77.17 Matokqus sokanumup nuppe, póhkok wunnont8wom8p, kah kukkôunkquodtash wonk sohwusháash.
77.18 Ummishant8wáongan8 keneempómog ut kesukqut: ukkutshaumun kutjisham88, ut muttaohket, kah ohke quéquanup kah nunnuksháp.
77.19 Kummay en kehtahhannet, kah kummay en missiyeuut nippe: kah kutóntánehtuongash mat wahteauoúunash.
77.20 Kummonchanomp kummissinninnumog onatuh flockut nashpe wunnutcheg Moses kah Aaron.
78.0 {Um-Maschil} Asaph.
78.1 WOi nummissinninnumog n8tiégk nuttinaumatuonk, ahchúsittam8k nuttinn8waongash ut nutt8nut.
78.2 N8wôshinum nutt8n ut kukkinneasuonganit nussim nupwóaongash negonne yeu8gish.
78.3 Nish n8tamágupash kah wahteauagupash: kah n8shinnónog nuttogqunna[n]ónup.
78.4 Matta nutadtat8unnanonash wutche wunneechân8oh, nuttinnonânonash pometuonk paaúm8uk waeenomaonk Jehovah, kah ummenuhkesuonk, kah ummonchántamwe anakausuongash nish asépash.
78.5 Newutche menûhketeau wauwáonk Jakobut, kah kehtimau naumatuonguh ut Israel, ne anunn8nomp k8shinnónoh, woh wunnohtinnáneau wunneechân8oh.
78.6 Ne pometuonk paaúm8ug woh 8wahteaúunneau, mukkiog neg woh nekitcheg: nag kesukkéhettit onk woh wuttinnoneau wunneechán8oh.
78.7 Onk woh anóunáog God, onk woh mo wanantamóog wutanakaúsuongash God: qut woh nanaihteáog wuttinn8waongash.
78.8 Kah woh mo unnaúo8og 8sh8oh, qussitt8mun8h kah nanánuwaonk ohquoantam8mun8h pométeonk, pometeonk matta sampwohtauógig wuttahh8óash: wunnashauongan8 matta menuhkenau8og Goduh.
78.9 Wunneechanoh Ephraim tapáaméog nemahtompáog, quehchiphouwáog wutch ayeúwuttinneat.
78.10 Matta nanaihteáog 8n8wáonk God, kah jishantamwog usseenat wuttinnaumatuonk.
78.11 Kah wunanatamwog wutanakausuongash, kah ummonchanatam8mash nahtinôhpash.
78.12 Monchanatam8ongash asépash 8shuoh ut anaquabhettit ut ohket Egypt, kah wutohteakonit Zoan.
78.13 Paúshinum kehtoh kah uppannupwushanon: wunnumwônkquáhteauun nippe onatuh nomwonkquag.
78.14 Kah kesukodteáeu ummonchanuh nashpe matokqs: kah nukkonáeu nashpe wequanáe n8tau.
78.15 Passehtham qussukquanah ut touohkomuk, kah 8tattamheuh, onatuh wutch m8nôayeúut.
78.16 Kah kussitchuwanteau wutch qussukquanit kah ayim jnippe anitchewánut sepuu[t].
78.17 Qut nano umm8cheke matchenehheouh, m8hm8squeáhettit quanunkquappinnutcheh ut touohkomuk.
78.18 Kah qutcheheaog Goduh wuttahouóut: kôkodtauwontamwe wehquetumm8hettit meetsúonk.
78.19 Nux ayeuuhkone ken8naog Goduh, n8waog, woh wunnahtau God ahhutashpimuk ut touohkomuk.
78.20 Kusseh togkodtamup qussuk, onk nuppe wuttitchuánup kah kussitchuan anuwutchuwan, sun woh assan wonk petukqunnunk? woh quoshaeihtam weyaus wutche ummissinninnumoh?
78.21 Newutche God yeu wunn8tamunnap, kah musquantamup namehkuh n8tau nashqunau ayeuuhkonae Jakob, kah musquanatam8onk ayeuhkonae nuhkuhkongquog Israel.
78.22 Newutche mat wunnamptauwo8og God: mat pabuhtantum8og 8wadchanuáonk.
78.23 Tohkónogque ukken8tamun matokqs wutch waabe: kah wohshinug kesukque squoantamash.
78.24 Kah sokanonteadt manna woh ummeechinnaoont: kah anumauont kesukque weatchiminneash.
78.25 Wosketompaog meechwog Angelsog ummeechumum8 wuttabe assamoh.
78.26 Wutchepwashinehteau ut mamahchekesukqut: kah nashpe ummenuhkesuonk pas8wau sowanishinneoh.
78.27 Kah ogque sokanonteau weyaus puppissaiyeuut kah ummequnne puppinshasoh onatuh kehtohhunnómukqut.
78.28 Kah uppenuhkon ut nôeu tuppuksinn8wonganit quinnuppu weekuwóut.
78.29 Onk meetsuog kah wamep8og: newutche wuttinnumauh nehenwonche kodtantamunit.
78.30 Matta penuantam8og ukkogkodtauóntam8ongan8: qut ash meechummuug wutt8n8wóash.
78.31 Ummusquantamowonk God nuhkuhkongquog, kah nushau késukkomunnutche: kah kepetahwau pepenaadcheh ut Israel.
78.32 Qut onch matcheséog: kah matta wunnamptamóog newutche ummonchanatamwe anakausuongash.
78.33 Newaj mohtupanuk ukkesukodtum88ash ut tahn8cheyeu8ut: kah ukkodum8m8ash ut onkuppunónat.
78.34 Nahnashont, neit wunnatinneawhouh: kah qushkeog, kah nompoaeu natinneahwhôog Goduh.
78.35 Onk mehquoantamwog God ukqussukquanum8oh. kah qunnunkappet Manit uppohquohwussuenúm8oh.
78.36 Qut onch 8wawunáunukum8ouh ut wutt8n8wout: uppannuwaheóuh wutch weenanuôut.
78.37 Newutche wuttahhou matta sampwan8h néh weeche, onk matta menuhkenum8og 8n8waonk.
78.38 Qut nomwahtunk ukkitteamonteanitteáonk, wutahquoantamauoh ummatcheseonganóash kah matta uppaguanuh, nux, m8chekit nompu puttikkinum ummusquantam8onk, kah matta wagkauonum8 wame ummusquantam8onk.
78.39 Newutche mehquantamup nag webe weyausog: waban pomushont, kah matta wonk peyau8.
78.40 Tohhen nohnompu umm8m8sqheouh ut touohkomuk? kah wunnohheouh ut touweu?
78.41 Nux, qushkeog kah qutchheaog Goduh, kah wuttogimóuh 8neetupanatam8moh Israel.
78.42 Matta mehquantamóog wunnutcheg: asa kesukod adt pohquohwhunósoh wutch ummatwomm8out.
78.43 Uttoh anákausip ukkuhkinneasuongash ut Egypt: kah ummonchanatam8ongash ut ohkit Zoan.
78.44 Kah quanuppinuk wussepumash en wusqueheonganit: kah wuttomogkon8m8ash, onk matta wane wuttattámwuhhettekkupash.
78.45 An8nop m8cheke unnissuoh m8suhquoh, nag woskhukhetticheh, kah mohmoskuhteasu, nah paguanukqhetticheh.
78.46 Kah assamau m8poh wame ne noh adtanegik: kah wutanakausuongan8 chansompsuh.
78.47 Matcheehteop 8weenomwussippag88ash nashpe mussegonoh: kah ummehtugkumm8oash sycomore nashpe t8hpu
78.48 Kah uppuppinashim8m8oh ukquashquttahwhonat musségon, kah flocksumoh ukkutshamun.
78.49 Wunnuhketahwhoh ummuttae musquantam8onk wutchenauausuonk, kah wutjishontamóonk, 8tamanatam8onk: an8nont matche angelsog.
78.50 Ayim may wutch ummusquantam8onk, matta wohquanumóou keteahogkounah wutch nuppunnat: qut aninnumauau uppomantamwowongan8 en wesaushaonk.
78.51 Nushau wame mohtammeginitcheh ut Egypt: negonne ummenuhkesuongan8 8weetuómut Ham.
78.52 Qut nehenwonche ummissinninnúmoh ohque wussohh8wunuh shepsoh kah wussompshánuh en touohkomuk onatuh floksut.
78.53 Kah 8wadchanuwae sampshanoh, onk matta wábeseog qut kehtoh nohkuhkauau matwâoh.
78.54 Kah uppas8oh nahog uhquaeu 8neetupanatamwe weekit; yeuut wadchuut wuttinnohkou tabhukup.
78.55 Kah sohwhohteau penuwohteaoh ut anaquabhettit, kah wutchachabenumaoh wutahtuongan8 nashpe kuhkohhamóonk: kah ayim wuttauadtuongan8 Israel 8weekittamunnaonut.
78.56 Onk onch qutchheaog, kah m8m8sqheouh quanunkquappinutche Manitt8h, kah mat nana[?]ihteaouog 8wauwaongash.
78.57 Qut nag qushkeog, kah mat nunnukqusseog onatuh 8shuoh: penshumaeog onatuh matsompwesekq ohtomp.
78.58 Newutche umm8m8sqheouh kussohkóaaúut: kah ummishem8sqheouh ennunneuhkontunkane Manint8konat
78.59 Yeu n8tog God musquantamup, kah m8cheke uhquânumau Israeloh.
78.60 Newaj ahquoantam wuttabernakleum ut Shiloh: weetu uttoh ponug nôeu woskétompa[u]htu.
78.61 Kah ponam ummenuhkesuonk missinnauhtu, kah wussohsumoonk matwaog wunnutcheganout.
78.62 Kah aninnumauau ummissinninnumohh togkodteg: kah musquanumau wutahtuonguh.
78.63 N8tau mahchekuswau 8skeum8uh: kah wutsquom8oh matta weetaetteau8oh.
78.64 Wussephausueneum8oh penushaog nashpe togkodteg: wussekousquom8oh matta mauémooh.
78.65 Neit God t8hkeu onatuh howan t8kit wutch kouenat: kah onatuh manuhkesit wosketomp toquessumwidt wutch wine.
78.66 Kah a[n]ehtahwau ummatwomoh wusseganit: ukkekontuwaheuh micheme:
78.67 Kah wonk wussekeneaumun wuttabernakleup Joseph, kah matta pepenamo wútchippanowonk Ephraim.
78.68 Qut pepenam wutchippanowonk Judah, wadchu Sion ne wâmontog.
78.69 Kah ayim wussanctuaryhum onatuh kâsuhkôag: onatuh ohke ne manuhketeunk micheme.
78.70 Kah pepenauau Davidoh wuttinnumoh, kah wunneemunoh wutch shepsog ohhappehettit.
78.71 Wutahque nanaushepsoneat ushquoshumwoh wompequauwoh, uppas8oh sohkom8nonat Jakov ummissinniñumoh, kah Israel wutahtoonk.
78.72 Onk wussohkomonuh nean sampwag wuttah: kah wussampshanuh neaunag wunnehtuhtauonk ut wunnutcheganit.
79.0 {Ukketoohomwaonk} Asaph.
79.1 WOI God, penuwohteaog peyauog kutahtoongánit, nishketeauog k8neetupanatamwu temple: nanomunkquatoog Jerusalem.
79.2 Assamaog psuksesoh mamachekesukqut nupp8eu hogkaoh kittinneumoh: 8weyausu k8neetupanatamomog ohkeit puppinnashimwog.
79.3 OOsqheongan8 seahhamwog onatuh nuppe, quinnuppe Jerusalem: onk wame howan upposekinuh.
79.4 Nukkekomukumun neetatteamungkonunnonog: nummamanauwanumitteamun kah nutá[h]anehteunteamun nag weenuhkunkqueogig.
79.5 Toh utt8che pish kummusquantam, woi God, micheme? sun pish nashqunnaú kummusquantamoonk onatuh n8taut?
79.6 Sokanumau kummusquantamoonk penuwohteaog, matta wahukk8unneg: kah ketass8t[a]m8onganit matta weehquetum8gig k8wesuonk.
79.7 Newutche mahchipwôog Jakob: kah matchehteauog 8tahtuonk.
79.8 Woi ahque ayeuuhkonittue mehquoantamaiinnean nóadt nummatcheseonganunnonash, kukkitteamonteanitteae kummonaneteaongash teanuk quoshae aninnumungqutteuh: newutche ahche nukkuttamungeyeumun.
79.9 Aninnumaiinnea[u] n8wadchanitteae Manitt8mun, newutche k8weseuongane sohsumoonk, kah pohquohwussinnean, kah jishkhomainnean nummatcheseonganunnonash, newutche k8wesuonk.
79.10 Tohwhuch woh n8wahettit penuwohteaog uttiyeuh um-Manitt8m8oh? noh wahhenaj ut penuwohteatu wutch anaquabeog; an8toan nashpe wsqueheongan8 kittinnumog ne s8ksquashongup.
79.11 Ummishanam8ongkan8 nég kobshagkinitcheg peyaum8utch anaquabean, néanummissag kummenuhkesuonk, wadchan naghog kohquttumauutcheg wunnupp8ongan8.
79.12 Nesausuk tahshit tashongquttau neetatteamunganonog ut upp8chenawounn8wout, ukkekom8aongan8 ne ash punnamukque[â]n, woi Jehovah.
79.13 Nemehkuh neenawun kummissinninnumog, kah kuttisshepsumwog wunnatupp8wongan8, kuttabuttantamauunnumun micheme: pish nunnohtinnomun k8waweenomitteaonk, wame pometuonganash.
80.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Sh[o]shannim Eduth, ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
80.1 NOOtash woi ken wunnanashepsaeneum8oh Israel, ken sampwushshanop Joseph onatuh flockut, ken wadohkea[n] nôeu cherubimsut wohsish.
80.2 Anaquabit Ephraim kah Benjamin kah Manasseh wogkauunish kummenuhkesuonk, kah peyaush wadchanean.
80.3 Quinnuppewussinnan wonk woi Jehovah, kuskesuk wohsumwahtoush, kah pish n8wadchanitteamun.
80.4 Woi Jehovah ken um-Manitt8m8oh ayeuhteaog, toh utt8che pish kummusquantam uppeantam8ongan8 kummissinninnumog.
80.5 Nag kussohkomm8nôog missuppegunne petukqunnunk: kah k8tattamheaog missuppequnnupog m8cheku.
80.6 Kuttayimaimun penuanittuonk neetatteamunganunnonut: kah nummatwomunno nog ahanuog môeu.
80.7 Quinnuppeninnean wonk, woi um-Manitt8m8oh ayeuteaog, kuskesuk wóhsumwahtoush, kah pish n8wadchânitteamun.
80.8 Kussohh8wuttóh weenómwussippog wutch Egypt, kussohwôhteam pénuwot, kah kutohkekôn.
80.9 Negonnu kukquoshaeihtamup ayeuonk, kum̃enu[h]ku wudchábitteuhkónap, kah numwáontukquinnukkodtup ohke.
80.10 Wadhcuash onkaohtópash, kah wuttuhqunash ogqunneunkquodtupash ut qunnu[h]que chikuppit.
80.11 Unóntukquinukod kehtohhannet, kah wuttuhqunnémesash en sepuut.
80.12 Neit tohwutch sohqunnuman uppummenutunkanash: nemehkuh neg wame pâmushácheg mayut wuttit mukk8pwunneau?
80.13 Touohkomukque boare mahchipwun: kah touohkomukque puppinashim ummahchipwun.
80.14 Qunnupish kenanumpassumunnumun woi um-Manitt8m8oh ayeuteaog, wómompish wutch kesukqut, kah naush, kah nátauwôhtaash yeu weenomsippog.
80.15 Kah weenominneohteuk adohkehteáán kuttinnohkôunit kah wudtuk ne mánuhkehteáán wutch nehenwonche ken.
80.16 Chikohteau ut n8táut, tumméthamun: awakompanaog kuttinnussûonk auskomont náhog.
80.17 Kenutcheg missuhkongqutch noh wosketomp kittinnohkôunit: wosketomp wunnaumonuh wutch nehenwonche ken manuhkeheadt.
80.18 Nemehkuh matta kukqushkéhtauunómun: keteáhinnean, kah n8wehquetumumun k8wesuonk.
80.19 Quinnuppeninnean, woi Jehovah um-Manitt8m8oh ayeuteaog, kuskesuk wôhsumwahtauush, onk pish n8wadcha[n]itteamun.
81.0 {Nohompuhpequodt ut Gittith, Ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
81.1 MIshont8wa8hhamok God nummenuhkesuonkanun weekontamwe mishont8wak en um-Manitt8moh Jakob.
81.2 Neemunnum8k ket8homaonk: kah paudtau8k timbrel, wunnont8wáeu harp, weeche psaltery.
81.3 Péquagk monopuhpeg nepâuz weske oguamwidt: án kuhk8wámukup, moaeu tabuttantamwáe kesukodt.
81.4 Newutche yeu an kuhk8wámukup wutche Israel: wuttinnaumatuonk um-Manitt8moh Jakob.
81.5 Yeu en kuhk8wona ut Joseph wutch wauwaonk, panupwushadt ohkit Egypt, na nuutt n8tamun unóntowaonk, matta n8wáhtam8un.
81.6 Nutóntahtoh 8wéanun wutch wuttúkedt: wunnutchegash pohquohwuttaúunash wutch ayeuónat akuhquog.
81.7 K8wehquetumaiip wadtamehpunaan kah kuppohuohwununup, kenamp8hamaúunup ut asampamukquodtut neempau: kukqutchhenup nippekontu Meribah. Selah.
81.8 N8tam8k woi nummissinninnumog, kah k8wauwaonsh, woi Israel, n8tiéan.
81.9 Wanne woh penôwe Manit kutappetunk8h: kah matta woh k8wowuss[u]móh pénowe Manit.
81.10 Nen Jehovah kum-Manitt8m, waj sohhűwunukuéup Egypt: wóhshinush m8cheke kutt8n, kah pish numwôhtaun.
81.11 Qut nummissinninnúmog matta nukkeiketunk8og: kah Israel matta nuttápeneunkk8og.
81.12 Nemehkuh nukkonôog nehenwonche wutahchewontam8ongan8 ut wuttahh8wóut: kah usseog nehenwonche ukkinn8nittuongannóut.
81.13 Woi nummissinninnúmog kukkeihtáhettis: kah Israel áhettis nummayut.
81.14 Woh teanuk nuppéeheóog ummatwóm8oh: kah woh ayeuhkônittue nukqushkenumup nunnetcheg nag sokeneunkqhetticheh.
81.15 Sékeneauóncheg Goduh, woh wutogquehtáuóuh: qut wutaquompaiyeum8 woh michemahtop.
81.16 Onk woh wutassumopah wanégikish wheatash: onk honey wutch qussukquanit woh k8wámepwununup.
82.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
82.1 GOD neepau ummukkinneunganout manukkesitcheg: wussumau kenugke Manitt8oh.
82.2 Tohutt8che matta kussampwe wussittumumw8 kah k8wohquanumomw8 matchetou? Selah.
82.3 Wadchán8k matchékuog, kah mô wadt8sh8gig: sampwenehheuk, onkapunnát kah quenahukquit.
82.4 Pohquahwhun matcheku kah quenahukquit: soh8wus wutch wunnutchéganuóut machetowog.
82.5 Matta wahteauóog, asa mat wahtamóog: pomushaog pohkênaoùat: wame quenohtag ohkeit ontohtaash.
82.6 Nussip kenaau manittoog: kah kenaau wame wunneechânoh quanonkquappit.
82.7 Qut pish kenupmw8 neáne wosketompaog: kah pish kuppenushaumw8 neáne howohs8tum.
82.8 Omohkish, woi God, wussittish ohke newutche pish kutahtoh wame wutohtimôneash.
83.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} Asaph.
83.1 Ahque netashshùash, woi God, ahque ohk8ash, ahue chéqunapsh, woi God.
83.2 Newutche kusseh, kummatwômog wogkouéog: kah neg sekeneunkqueaneg tohshinnumwog uppuhkuk8h.
83.3 As8kekodteamwe ken8nittúog ayeuhkône kummissinninnumut kah ayeukóne wetuodtuok neg adtahshadcheg.
83.4 Unn8waog, éhoh peyunk tummehtawhontuh, onk woh matta wutohtimm[o]éog: 8wesuongan8 Israel woh mat mehquoantam8un wonk.
83.5 Newutche wetuodtuog pasukqunnú metah: 8n8waog áyeuhkonetue ken.
83.6 Wodohkitcheg Edom, kah Ishmaelitsog: Moab kah Hagarensog.
83.7 Gebal, kah Ammon, kah Amalek, Philistiansog kah wodohkitcheg Tyre.
83.8 Wonk Assur 8weetuómoh; aninnumauwóog wunnaumonuh Lot. Selah.
83.9 Unnehheuk onatuh Midianits neánheáp, Sisera, neanheup Jabin, up sepuut Kishon.
83.10 Neg pagwanehhettit ut Endor: ohqueneunkqusseuppanneg ánohkeit.
83.11 Wutt8wosketompaog ogqunneunkqusséhettich Oreb, kah Zeeb, kah wame wussantimóm8oh ogqunneunkqussehettich Zeba, kah Zalmunna,
83.12 Nag n8waog, neemunnumuttuh weekash God wutch kutahtauonganun.
83.13 Woi num-Manitt8m nag énneh onatuh wheelut, onatuh sequssunkanash ut wabanut.
83.14 Onatuh chaugohtag touohkomuk, kah onatuh kogkussompuneau nashqussuk wadchuash;
83.15 Ne woskeh nashpe kummehshittashshinneum: kah wabuwus nashpe kummehshittashshineum.
83.16 Numwohtaash akodchuonk wuskesukk8wout, onk woh natinnehamwog k8wesuonk, woi Jehovah.
83.17 Akodjhettich, kah wuttammepunâhettich micheme: nux, akodjhettich kah pagwanehettich.
83.18 Onk woh wosketompaog wahteauog, ken webe k8wesuonkan JEHOVAH: kukqunnunkquap yeu ut wame ohkeit.
84.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ut Gittith: ukketoohhomâonk wunnaumonuh} Korah.
84.1 Toh nuttinnu tápeneum keekash, woi wut-Jehovah áyeuhteáunit!
84.2 Nukketeahogkou nontweánumw8, nux sauantam wutch uppeantamwahkomukqut Jehovah; nuttah kah n8weyaus mishant8waog wutch pomantamwae God.
84.3 Nux maméshasquish namehteau wetu, kah papaskhas 8wadshayeu, uttoh woh apinit wunneechansuh, ut kut-altarumit woi wut-Jehovah ayeuteaunit, nukkehtass8tamom, kah num-Manitt8m.
84.4 Wunnanumoog neg keekit apitcheg: nag nano kuttabatta[n]tamunkquog. Selah.
84.5 Wunnanumau wosketomp ummenuhkesuonk apehtunkquean, ut wuttahh8wout ummayash.
84.6 Neg panupwushahettit 8naohteai Baka 8thamunkanuhkónneau: kah sókanon numwohhagwutteau nuppissepagwos.
84.7 Nag auog wutch menuhkesuonganit onk yean menuhkesuonganit: wame nogqussuog ut Sion anaqu[à]bit God.
84.8 Woi wut-Jehovah áyeuhteaunit, n8tash nuppeantam8onk, kuhkeihtah: woi um-Manitt8moh Jakob. Selah.
84.9 Naish woi Manit nutogqunneganun: kah monunneash wuskesuk sasequnukquean.
84.10 Newutche pasuk kesuk keekuwót negonne wunnegen onk nequt mutannunganogkodtash: ain woh negonne nunnanaeihteóh squont num-Manitt8m week, onk neit 8weeketamon matchet8wog wekuwout.
84.11 Newutche Jehovah Manit nepâuz kah ogqunneg: Jehovah magou wunneetupanatam8onk kah sohsumoonk, wanne wunnegenninn8gk woh ukqushkinnumauh wutch nah sampwshanutcheh.
84.12 Woi Manit ayeuteaunit, wunnanumau wosketomp nnoh pabahtanumukquean.
85.0 {Nohtumpuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk wunnaumoauh} Korah.
85.1 IEhovah, ken kuttápeneamup kutohke, kukquihchuwunnomp ummissinnóonk Jakob.
85.2 Kutahquontamauóp ummatcheseonk kummissinninnumog, kupputtagkuhum wame ummatcheseonk. Selah.
85.3 Kutamaunumup wame kummusquanatam8onk: kukqushkep wutch kummishe musquanatamunat.
85.4 Quinnuppinninnean Woi Manit k8wadchanuwonganun: kah kummusquanummuonganun netahshehteoush.
85.5 Sun micheme kummusquanumimun? sun kukqunteoh kummusquantam8onk ut wame pometuonganit?
85.6 Sunnummatta wonk kuppomantamwahumun: onk kummissinninnumog woh k8weekontam8wônukquog?
85.7 Nahtussinnean kummonaneteaonk, woi Jehovah, kah aninnumaiinnean k8wadchanuwaonk.
85.8 Nukkéhkitam ut toh án8wodt Manit Jehovah, newutche unnau wunnóhteaonk ummissinninnumoh, kah 8neetupanatam8moh: qut ahque nag qushkéhettich wonk as8tuonganit.
85.9 Wunnamuhkut 8wadchanuwaonk uppas8sukongqunneau nag qushóncheg: onk woh sohsum8onk ayeum8 nutohkinnonut.
85.10 Monaneteaonk kah wunnamuhkuteyeuuk nogkiskôittuog: sampwesusséonk kah wunohteaonk chipwutt8nápwuttúog,
85.11 Wanummuhkuteyeu8k pish sonkun wutch ohkekontu, kah sampweusséonk pish womómpu wutch kesukqut.
85.12 Nux, Jehovah pish magou ne wanegik, kah kutohkin pish mogkékin.
85.13 Wunnomwausseonk pish wunnegónoh[-]kouoh, kah pish kupponukqun ummayu[t] wutántanehtuonganit.
86.0 {Uppeantamoonk} David.
86.1 Ach8sittah, woi Jehovah, n8tah: newutche nummachek, kah nukquená[h]ik.
86.2 Wadchan nukketeahogkou newutche nen kodtumonteanuméan: woi num-Manitt8m, wadchan kittinneum n#noh pabahtánumugquean.
86.3 Monanumeh, woi Jehovah, newutche kummauunnitteaush asekesukokish.
86.4 Weekontamwáh ukketeahogkôunnouh kittinnum, newutche woi Jehovah kuttuspinnumaush nukketeahogkou.
86.5 Newutche ken Jehovah k8neetum, kah teanuk kutahquoantus: kah m8chekehteau kummonaneteaonk, nag wame wehqutumunkqueaneg.
86.6 Ahchúsitash, woi Jehovah, nuppeantamóonk: kah kukkeitash n8wadtauatongqussuonk nanompasumunon.
86.7 Wuttammepunnaon k8wéquetumoush, newutche pish kenamp8homah.
86.8 Kenugke manitt8wog, matta pasuk kuttinnongk8, woi Jehovah: asa anakausuongash matta ogqunneongquodtinnowash kutanakausuonganit.
86.9 Wame wutahtimóneash nish kesteauupash, nag pish peyauog, pish k8wowussumukquog anaquabean woi Jehovah: onk pish sohsum8wóntamog k8wesuonk.
86.10 Newutche ken kummissugken, kummonchanatamwe ussem: ken webe Manit.
86.11 Kuhk8tomah kummay, woi God, nuppomusham k8nomwaonganit: pasukquinteaush nuttah quihtamunnat k8wesuonk.
86.12 Kuttabuttantamoush, woi Jehovah num-Manitt8m ut mamusse nuttahhut: onk nussohsum8wontam k8wesuonk micheme.
86.13 Newutche missi kummonanumúonk: onk kuppohquohwhun nukketeahogkou, wutch chepiohkomukque omohqut.
86.14 Woi Manit, pittuanumóog n8ápetunkquog: kah mukkinéog onkkuppunnáhteaénúog kodtinneanâog nukketeahogkôunoh, matta kuppónukk8og anaquabhettit.
86.15 Qut ken, woi Jehovah, Manit num-wohtea[u] kitteamonteanitteaonk, kah womoausu: kah sepe pahtsu, kah monat ummonaneteaonk, kah 8nomwaonk.
86.16 Woi qushkish en hogkadt kah monanumeh, aninnumau kummenuhkesuonk kittinnúm: kah wadchan wunnaumonuh mittumwossisse kittinnúm.
86.17 Nahtusseh kukkinneasuonk wanegik, neg sekeneunkqueaneg woh wunnaumunneau, kah woh akodchúog newutche ken Jehovah kutannumaup kah k8weekontamwáhip.
87.0 {Ukketoohomaonk wunnaumonuh} Korah.
87.1 Ukquenohtagóm ohteau ut 8neetupanatamwu wadchukóntu.
87.2 Jehovah womantam squoantamash ut Sion, m8cheke onk wame 8tahtuonganit Jakob.
87.3 Sohsum8ongash unneapash papaume ken woi wut8tan God. Selah.
87.4 N8weeadtim Rahab, kah Babylon, neg wahukquéaneg, kusseh Philistia kah Tyre, weech Ethiopia, yeuoh wosketomp nawuttit neekit.
87.5 Papaume Sion pish n8waog, yeuoh kah n$noh nawuttit nekinneah, kah quanunkquappit nagum pish ummenuhkeheuh.
87.6 Jehovah push wutogkétamun wussukwhóut missinninnuh, yeuoh wosketomp nawuttit nekinneau. Selah.
87.7 Naut nahtô8hhomóncheg matta webe nohtompuhpequodcheg: wame nuttohkékomeúmash kutahtaunash.
88.0 {Ukketoohomaonk wunnaumonuh} Korah, {nohtumpuhpequodt ut Mahalath Leanoth um-Maschil} Heman {Ezrahite}.
88.1 WOi Jehovah n8wadchanitteae Manit, nummauh ut anaquabean kesukodáeu, kah nukonáeu.
88.2 Nuppeantamóonk peyaum8utch ánaquabean ahchúsitash nummaúonk.
88.3 Newutche nukketeáhogkounit numwohteau wuttammepunnaongash: kah nukketeaonk pas8sukom weenohkeet.
88.4 N8wetogkeemit nag aô[n]cheg weenohkeet: onatuh neen wosketomp matta manuhkesit.
88.5 Nutchippéhtau kenugke nupp8og, onatuh náhshitcheg apitcheg weenohkeet, neg matta waánummóacheg wonk: kah nag tummehtahwhôog wutch kenutchéganit.
88.6 Kussépsumeh quanónogok pasohtheonk: pohkénaoúut, ut m8naiyeúut.
88.7 Kummusquantamm8onk nukquensumm8wónukqun: kah k8taméhpunáseh nashpe wame kuttugk8mog. Selah.
88.8 Kutamaunumah neetatteamunganuk nôadtit: kenehchánittamwâheneunk naghok, nukkuphâs, kah matta woh nussohhom8h.
88.9 Nuskesuk mau, newutche n8taméhpunnáonk, Jehovah, kenanampassumush asekesukokish, kuttushpunnumaush nunnutchegash.
88.10 Sun kenohtin monchanatam8wongash nupp8og? sun pish nupp8og omohkeog kah k8wowussumukquog. Selah.
88.11 K8womoausue kitteamonteanitteaonk sun pish wateauwaheau nnah wenohket? kah k8nomwausseonk paguanuonganit?
88.12 Kummonchànatam8ongash sun pish wohteauunash ut pohkenaouut? kah kussomweusseonk ut wanantamwae ohket.
88.13 Qut kummauunnitteaush, woi Jehovah kah nompoaeu nuppeantamoonk teanuk peayum8.
88.14 Jehovah tohwutch sohwohteaon nukkete[á]hogkou? tohwhutch puttoghuman kuskesuk wutche neen?
88.15 Nutonkkuppunnam kah nahen nunnup, wutch n8skenuuñeat yeu pajeh: waamattamon kussaiaskishohteaongash nukkogkeam.
88.16 Kummishe m8squantam8onk nunnuhkukongqun: kussaiaskishohteaongash nuttummetohuk,
88.17 N8weenuhkongquog asekesukokish onatuh nippe, n8weenuhkongquog moaeu.
88.18 N8womoneg, kah neetatteamong kena8tashaog: kah yeug waanumogig kupponaog pohkenaouut.
89.0 {Um-Maschil Ethtan Ezrahit}
89.1 Nuttin8homom ummonaneteaongash Jehovah micheme: nutt8n pish wahteauwahuau k8nomwausseonk ut wame pometuonganit.
89.2 Newutche nussip monáneteaonk pish micheme weekuhkon, kuppaubuhtanumitteaonk pish kummenuhkehteoh ut kesukquehtu.
89.3 N8n8wamunnonup n$noh pepen8ogkup, nutchadchekeimomp David nuttinnum.
89.4 Nummenuhkeh k8skannemeneog micheme: kah n8weketeam kutappuonk ut wame pometuonganit. Selah.
89.5 Kah kesukquash waeenodtumwog kummonchanatammuongash, woi Jehovah, kah kuppaubuhtanumitteaonk ummukkinneongan8wout k8neetupanatam8mog.
89.6 Newutche howan woh ut kesukqut tatuppinit Godoh? howan masukkenuk kenugku nah wunnaumonainneunk woh tatupinat Jehovah$noh?
89.7 Manit mishu wabesuonou ummukkinneongan8wout wunneetupanatamwog, kah ukquehtianumonaout wame nag quanupapitcheg.
89.8 Woi Jehovah, um-Manitt8moh ayeuteanit, howan manuhkesit Jehovah agquinne[n]gqussit kuhhogkat asa k8nomwausseonganit weenuhkongquean?
89.9 Kenanaunum kehtohhane mishont8waonk tukk8og waapehettich, kutchequnashaog wonk.
89.10 Kussukqtahwhomp Rahab, neane noh nohshit: kusseoh kummatwomog nashpe menuhke kuhpit.
89.11 Kesukquash kuttaiheash, ohke wonk kuttaihe, papaume muttaok, kah ne adtahshimmeechumik, nish kummenuhkohtinash.
89.12 Nanumit kah soanish, neg kukkezheoog: Tabor kah Hermon nag pish weekontamwog ut k8wesuonganit.
89.13 Kutahto menukhesue muhpit: menuhki kénutch, kah kuttinnohkou qunuhquodt.
89.14 Sampweusseonk kah wussittumoonk menehketeau8m8 k8sittumwe appuonk: monaneteaonk kah wunnamuhkuteyeuuk pish negonshaum8 ut kuskesukqut.
89.15 Wunnanamoog missinninnuog neg wahteunkeg wekontamwae wuttauatonkqussuonk: nag pomushaog, woi Jehovah ut wequaiyeue kuttinnussuonganit.
89.16 Ut k8wesuonganit weekontamwog nehteagu kesuk: kah ut kussampweusseonganit mishsheheoog.
89.17 Newutche ken wussohsumoe menuhkesuongan8: kah ut kukkitteamonteanitteaonganit nutaskonun pish tohshinau.
89.18 Newutche Jehovah nutushpuhh8waonganun: kah 8neetupanatam8moh Israel, noh nukketass8tamómun.
89.19 Neit kukkinn8nomp wunneetupanatamweyeuit, ut monamansinneat, kah kussip, nupponamau aninnumóadtuonk noh manuhkesit: nummisheh noh pepenauit wutch missinninnutu.
89.20 Nummiskau David nuttinninnúm: kah nussusséqun n8neetupanatamwe pummee.
89.21 Ut wuhhogkat nunnutcheg pish menehkhik: nuhpit wonk pish menuhkesuáhik.
89.22 Matwau matta pish wuttóadtéhtáheuh: kah wunnaumonuh matcheetowonk matta pish wutunkquanumwáheuh.
89.23 Kah nunn8ketah ummatwomoh ut anaquabit: kah nussasámatahwhóog neg sekeneauoncheg.
89.24 Qut nuppaubatanumitteaonk, kah nummonaneteaonk pish weetomuk: kah ut n8wesuonganit, wutaskonoh pish tahshin[ó]ninneuh.
89.25 Kah nupponam wunnutcheg ketahhannit: kah wuttinnohkou sepuwehtu.
89.26 Noh pish nummauunnitteunk, ken n8sh: num$Manitt8m, kah qussukquanue n8wadchanitteaonk.
89.27 Kah noh nummohtommégitteaeh: ánuunkqussúmau muttaohku ketass8timwoh.
89.28 N8wadchanumau nummonaneteaonk micheme: kah n8n8waonganun pish menuhkohteau.
89.29 Kah 8skannemunneoh nummichemappeheóog: kah wuttappuonk neane kesukque kesukodtash.
89.30 Wunneechanuh ohquánumáhettit nuttinnaumatuonguh, kah matta pomushaontamwahetteg n8sittum8ongash.
89.31 Nag pohquenummohettit nukkuhk8waongash, kah matta nánauwehteauwéhetteg nuttinnaumatuongash.
89.32 Neit nátauohtóh uppanneseonganoash nashpe sasamatáheg, kah ummatcheseongash nashpe tattogkodtuongash.
89.33 Qut onch matta nuppápaquanne amaunumauoh nukkitteamonteanitteae womoausuonk: kah nuppaubuhtanumukqussuonk matta panushógk8.
89.34 N8n8waonk matta nuppohquenum8, kah matta nutontcheteá8 ne sohham8m8 wutch nussisset8nit
89.35 Pasukqut nutchadchekeyeuop nashpe n8neetupanatam8onk, matta nuppann8waheoh David.
89.36 OOskannem pish michemohteau, kah wutappuonk onatuh nepâuz ut anaquabeh.
89.37 Pish michemenuhkohteau onatuh nanepauhshad, kah onatuh paubuhtanumukqussue wauwaen ut kesukqut. Selah.
89.38 Qut kuppogkenop kah kutjishanumop: kummusquanumau sasequnadt.
89.39 Kuttahn8cheéhteoh 8n8waonk kittinnúm: kenishketeoh wutchetuhquab, unnohkónat ohkeit.
89.40 Kussukquetahham wame uppummenutunkash: kummahchumwéhteoh 8manskash.
89.41 Wame neg paumshacheg mayit ummukk8kinóuh: noh ushpunnomâonk weetatteamunguh.
89.42 Kuttohshinum wuttinnohkôun8 ayeuuhkonukqutche: k8weekontamwah wame ummatwomoh.
89.43 Kah k8wehqueteoh en kenag wuttogkodteg, kah matta keneepauweheuh ayeuwuttinneat.
89.44 Wussohsumoonk ne kutteahsheáhto: kah kuttinnuhteam wutappuonk ohkeit?
89.45 Kuttiohquehteóh 8skenue kesukodtash: kupputtog8h akodchuonk[.] Selah.
89.46 Tohutt8che, woi Jehovah, pish kupputtogquem? micheme? sun pish kummusquantam8onk ogqunneau n8taut?
89.47 Mehquoantash nutaquompiyeum uttoh[in] tióhqui: tohwaj tahn8cheáheadt wame wosketompaog?
89.48 Howae noh wosketomp pomantog matta woh naum8g nupp8onk? sun woh pohquohwhunau ukketeahogkôunoh wutch wunnutcheganit weenohke. Selah.
89.49 Lord uttiyeush negonnáe k8womoausuongash, nish chadchekeimuhpash David ut k8namuhkuteyeumut?
89.50 Mehquoantash, woi Lord, kehkômaongan8 kittinneumog: uttoh nuttin nashpe[u] ut nup8chenauóunit, nukkehkómuk8ongan8 wame matikkenukeg.
89.51 Nish nashpe kummatwomog, woi Lord, ashpunáadtummoh[e]ttiche: nish nashpe ushpunnumáhetticheh wutontanehtuongash sasequnadt.
89.52 Wunnanumunach Jehovah micheme. Amen, kah amen.
90.0 {Uppeantamooonk} Moses {Manittoowomp}.
90.1 WOi Lord, ken nutayeuonganun ut wame pometuonganehtu.
90.2 Asquam wadchauash neekininn8g, kah asquam kahkénauwehtéauouan ohke kah muttaok, wutch micheme onk yaan micheme ken kum-Manitt8.
90.3 Kukquinnuppin wosketomp en paguanuonganit, kah kussim, quskeek kenaau wunneechan8oh wosketompaog.
90.4 Newutche nequt muttannongane kodtumm8 tatuppeyeu8, ut anaquabean, wunnonkou, pamshunk, kah onatuh nukkonáe askuhwheteaonk.
90.5 Kutogque moncheaheoog tommogka[u]it, nag onatuh kaémuk: nompoaeu tatuppeyeu8og m[á]skit sonkuk.
90.6 Nompoáe n8n8han, kah neekin: wunnonk8uk tummehthamun, kah uhp8teau.
90.7 Newutche nummohtuppaémun nashpe kummusquanittam8onk, kah nashpe kummishe musquanitteaonk n8taméhitteamun.
90.8 Kupponum nummohtuppaémun nashpe kummusquanittam8onk, kah nashpe kummishe musquanitteaonk n8taméhitteamun.
90.9 Newutche wame nukkesukodtumunnonash mahtshaash ut kummishe musquanitteaonk: nutogque mahtshadtomun nukkodtum8munnonash aunchem8enuut.
90.10 Nukkesukodte nukkodtum8munonash nesausuk tahshinchagkodash: kah shwosuk tahshinchagok, nashpe menuhkesuonk, onch ummenuhkesuonk sauámam8onk kah onkquomom8onk: newutche teanuk tummehthamun, kah nutt8wemun.
90.11 Howan wahteunk kummusquantam8e menuhkesuonk? neaunak kukqushitteaonk, ne nnih kummusquanitteaonk.
90.12 Ne$ne kuhk8tomaiinnean ogketamunat nukkesukkodtumunonash, onk woh nupponamumun nuttahhunnonash waantam8onganit.
90.13 Qushkish, woi Jehovah, toh utt8che? kah aiushkiantash papaume kittinnneumog.
90.14 Woi tapeneauoshussunan teanuk nashpe kummonaueteaonk, onk woh n8wekontamumun, kah nummuskauanatamumumun ut wame nukkesukkodtumunnonut.
90.15 Weekontamwáhinnean neáe kesukodtash onkkuppunnanéog, kah kodtum8ash ne adt naumog machuk.
90.16 Kutanakausuonk pahkém8utch ut kuttinnumut: kah kussohsumóouk en wunnechan8wout.
90.17 Kah 8neetuonk kum-Manitt8mun God nukkuhkongqutteuh, kah menuhketeaiinnean wutanakausuonk nunnutcheganunnonash: nux, wutanakausuonk nunnutcheganunnonash menehketeaush[.]
91.1 NNoh wadohkit asampâmukquadtit quanunkquapit, pish appeu wutonkauhtomut wame manuhkesit.
91.2 Nussim papaume Jehovah, noh nutusphouwaonk, kah n8wonkónous: num-Manitt8m, noh nuppabahtanum.
91.3 Wunnamuhkut pish kuppohquohwhunuk wutch wutappéhanoh adchaénit: kah wutch wutann8e wesausháonk.
91.4 Kupputtagkúhhup umméqunoh, kah agwu wunnuppawhunnit kuppabahtantam: 8nomwayeuonk kutogqunnégonóhkom kah kutóngkouwóhquoss8.
91.5 Matta pish k8wábesuontam8h sauskshánittuongash nukkonáeu: asa kôúhquod pomushonk kesukodáeu.
