91.6 Asa wesausháonk ne pomushaúm8uk pohkenaouut: asa paguanuonk paguateaum8ug puhshahquái.
91.7 Nequt muttánnonganogkussuog penushâhettit ut kishke ken, kah piukqut muttannonganogkussuog ut kuttinnohkôunit: qut pish matta kuppas8sukkongk8un.
91.8 Webe kuskesukqut pish k8che naumun, kah pish kenaum wutonkquatunk matcheetou.
91.9 Newutche kuttaiimup Jehovah, noh nuttusp8waonk, quanunkquapit, kutayeuonganit.
91.10 Matta pish kummáchoppino: asa pish matta wesaushaonk pas8sukk8mm8 k8tahtuonk.
91.11 Newutche ahtuhshau wut-angelsumoh wutche ken: woh kenanaaihhukquog nish noh kummayut.
91.12 Nag kutahshinukquog ut wunnutchegan8out: ishkont kuttogkussittassun qussuk.
91.13 Pish kuttashkukau qunnônou kah adder: wuskoshim8m qunnônou kah dragon pish kuttashkukau agwe kusseetut.
91.14 Newutche 8womoausuonk nupponamungqun, newajeh pohquohwhunog: nukqunnunkqueh, newutche wahteoun n8wesuonk.
91.15 N8weequetummunk, onk nunnamp8hamau: n8weetom ut wuttammepunnónat, nuppohquohwhun, kah nukquihtiánum.
91.16 Pish nuttápe sepepomantamóonk: kah nunnaumwah n8wadchanuwaonk.
92.0 {Sabath dayeu unn8homaonk}.
92.1 Wunnegen tabuttantamauun Jehovah, kah unn8homun k8wesuonk, woi quanunkquapean.
92.2 Nahtikon k8womoausue kitteamonteanitteaonk nompôáeu: kah kuppabahtanumitteaonk ásenukóhkish.
92.3 Ut puhpequoánit piukquómposik pémuneóhtanash, kah ut psaltery, kah ut harp wônónt8wag.
92.4 Newutche ken Jehovah k8weekontamwáhe nashpe kutanakausuonk: nummishe muskouanatamóntam nashpe wutanakausuongash kenutcheg.
92.5 Woi Jehovah, uttoh en missi kutanakausuongash, kah kuttenantam8ongash m8nâiyeu8ash.
92.6 Puppinashimwe wosketomp matta 8wahteauoúun: asuh mattammog matta wahtam8un.
92.7 Matchetou sonkutche onatuh moskétuut, kah wame anakausitcheg matcheseonk adtanneghettit, ne onkwoh micheme pagwanôog.
92.8 Qut ken Jehovah quanunkquappean micheme.
92.9 Newutche kusseh kummatwómog, woi Jehovah, newutche kusseh kummatwómog pish paguanúog: wame anakausitcheg matcheseonk pish séahwhôog.
92.10 Qut nutaskon kutáshin onatuh wutáskonit nequtyeuwun; nussussequnit wuske pumme.
92.11 Kah wonk nuskesuk pish naum nukkodtantamóonk ut nummatwomut, kah nuttaúogash pish n8tamwog ne kodtantamon papaume matchetowog neg waabetunkquéaneg
92.12 Sampweusseaenúog kussétuog onatuh palme mahtug: pish unneetu onatuh musquohtugkusseit ut Lebanon.
92.13 Yeug ahkuhteámukeg ut weekit Jehovah, nag pish dtannetuog wutchippenutunkanit num-Manitt8mun.
92.14 Nag pish yeayatcheh dtannegen meechum, mahtantamwáhettit, nag pish wunnogk8og, kah ashkoshk88og.
92.15 Onk woh nahtitteáog Jehovah sampwésu: noh nukqussukquánum, kah matta penoweseonk ahtóou.
93.1 IEhovah wutass8timun, hogk8 wohquáunissónk, Jehovah hogk8 menuhkesuonk, puttugquábussu: kah muttaok menehketeauun, onk woh matta ontohtano.
93.2 Kutappuonk meneketeauun nôadt; ummicheméyeu.
93.3 Tommogkon mishont8wau, woi Jehovah, tommogkon mishontowau wuttauatongqussu, tommogkon mishéheau wuttugk8moh.
93.4 Jehovah quanunkquappit m8cheke missugken onk 8wadtauatonkqussuonkan8 monaog nippéog, onk kehtóntukquog ut kehtahhannit.
93.5 K8wauwâongash ahche wunnamuhkutéyeu8ash: wunneetupanatam8onk tapeneunkquod ut kekit, woi Jehovah micheme.
94.1 WOi Jehovah Manit noh ann8táonk wadchiyéu8k, woi Manit noh ann8táonk wadchiyéu8k, wôhsish.
94.2 Tahshin kuhhog woi ken wásittuman ohke: onkquattau pittuánum8.
94.3 Woi Jehovah toh utt8che matcheetowog, toh utt8che matchetowog pish weekontamwog?
94.4 Toh utt8che pish kutt8og, kah keket8kóntamwog woskehittuongash: kah wame anakausitcheg matcheseongash pish waéenowaog?
94.5 Nag sokqshanáog kummissinninnumoh, woi Jehovah, kah onkkapunnataúog kutahtáuonk.
94.6 Nusháog sekousqua, kah penowóhteuh: kah nusháog mowadt8sh8neg.
94.7 Qut onch n8waog, Jehovah matta wunnaum8un: asuh um-Manitt8moh Jakob matta 8t8wóntam8un.
94.8 Wohtam8k kenaau puppinashimwe wosketompaog kenugke missinninnuut: kah kenaau mattammágwog aquompak pish k8waantamumw8.
94.9 Noh áhkitteadt mehtaúog, sunnummatta woh n8tam8? noh áyig muskesuk sunnummatta woh naum8?
94.10 Noh sasamatahwhont penuwohteuh, sunnummatta woh sansamatahwhôu? noh kohk8tomauont wosketompuh wahtunteáonk, sunnummatta woh wahteauouun?
94.11 Jehovah wahteóh wuttenantam8ongash wosketompoh nish tahn8cheyeú8gish.
94.12 OOnánumau wosketomp sasamakoúwhadt, woi Jehovah: kah kahk8tomauadt wutche kuttinnaumatuonganit.
94.13 Onk woh kittinnumau anwôhsin8onk wutch onkquommom8onganit: nô pajeh pahsahthamadt matcheetowog.
94.14 Newutche Jehovah matta pogkenáou ummissinninnumoh: asuh matta nukkodtum8 wutahtouonk.
94.15 Qut wussittumóonk qunnuppémo en wunnomwausseonganit, kah wame sampwutteahóncheg wutásukkomunneau.
94.16 Howan wáabehtamwanshit ayeuuhkonittue matchesécheg? howan neepaiéhtamwánshit ayeuuhkonittue anakausitcheg matcheseongash?
94.17 Jehovah matta áninnumaiégis: nukketeahogkou teanuk woh chéquneiyeu.
94.18 An8wáon nusseet t8nequshin: kummonaneteáonk, woi Jehovah, nukkogkanukkup.
94.19 Mônak nuttenántám8wongash nuttahut, k8nenéhhuwaongash wuttáphukqunash nukketeahogkou.
94.20 Wutappuonk matcheséonk sun woh k8weechayeúmukqun? ayik woskéhuwaonk nashpe naumatuonk.
94.21 Nag moéog ayeuuhkonittue ukketeahogkôunoh sampweusseaen: kah 8sumaúoh en nuppunnat matta woskéhuwâe wsqueheonk.
94.22 Qut Jehovah nuttusphouwaonk: kah num-Manitt8m nuttusphouéongane qussuk.
94.23 Kah noh pish upputtagquehtáhwhôh nehenwonche ummatcheseonganoash, kah pish wuttúmmetáhwhoh ut nehenwonche ummatcheseongan8óut: nux, Jehovah kum-Manitt8mun pish wuttummetahwhoh.
95.1 HO peyonk ket8homauontuh Jehovah: weekontamwe mishont8wohkôontuh qussuk k8wadchanitteáonganun.
95.2 Peyontuh anaquabit nashpe samp8waonk: kah weekontamwe mishónt8wóhkôontuh nashpe ket8homaongash.
95.3 Newutche Jehovah missugken God: kah missugken ketass8t anuwe wame manit8og.
95.4 Ut wunnutcheganit m8nôeiyeuash ut ohkekontu ohteau: kah kodúhkâuágu madchúash wuttáiheash.
95.5 Kehtoh wuttaihe, kah wutáyimunap: kah wunnutchegash kestau8p nunnóbohke.
95.6 Ho peyunk waussumóntuh, náaétuh, appésittukqussinuttuh ut anaquabit Jehovah kezhúkqueagup.
95.7 Newutche noh kum$Manitt8mun, kenaau ummissinninnumoh wunnadtupp8wonganit, us-shepsoh ut wunnutcheganit: yeu kesukok n8tamóg 8wadtauatonkqussuonk,
95.8 Ahque manuhketeáágk kuttahhuwoash, onatuh penuánittuonganit, kah onatuh qutchehuwae kesukodtut touohkomukqut.
95.9 K8shhuwóog quajhukquéan, kah natinneakôshettit, kah naumohettit nutanakausuongash.
95.10 Yauuncháge kodtumwáeu yeu neuantamhukqunah pométeonk, kah nussip, neg missinninnuog panneaûoh wuttahh8oh, kah matta wahteauog nummayash.
95.11 Nag musquanumog nutchadchekéimog: onk woh matta petutteauóog, nutanwôsinn8onganit.
96.1 WOi ket8homok Jehovah weske an8homaonk: ket8homok Jehovah ut wame ohkeit.
96.2 Ket8homok Jehovah, 8nantam8k 8wesuonk: nahtitteak 8wadchan8waonk kesukodáeu.
96.3 Pahketauok wussohsumóonk kenugke penuwohteatu: ummonchanatam8wongash ut kenugku wame missinninnútu.
96.4 Newutche Jehovah missugken; kah mishe waásumâu: noh woh m8cheke qushau ánue wame manitt8og.
96.5 Newutche wame manittóog ut wutohtimoneat neukontunkanog: qut Jehovah ayimup kesukquash.
96.6 Quttianatuonk kah wohquanissuonk anaquabit ohteau: menuhkesuonk kah 8netuonk ohtaash ut 8neetupanatamwe wekit.
96.7 Aninnumók Jehovah, woi kutauwadtuonganou missinninnuog, aninnumók Jahovah sohsum8onk, kah menuhkesuonk.
96.8 Aninnumok Jehovah wussohsum8onk newadchiyeu8k 8wesuonganit, paudtau8k mag8onk, kah peyunk wutchippunnutunkanit.
96.9 Woi waasumok Jehovah ut 8neetupanatamwe 8netu[og]anit: wabesek ut anaquabit wame ohke.
96.10 N8wag ut kenugke penuwohteaut Jehovah ass8tum, kah muttaok menuhketeauun kah mat pish ontohtano: noh sampwe wussumau missinninnuh.
96.11 Kesukquash weekontam8m8utch, kah ohke muskouantam8m8útch: kehtóh mishont8om8utch kah ne noh ohtag.
96.12 Ohteuk muskouantam8m8utch, kah wame ne noh ohtág; neit pish wame metugquash touohkomukqut weekontam8m8ash.
96.13 Ut anaquabit Jehovah newutche peyau newutche peyau wussittumunat ohke: sampweusseae wusittum muttaok: kah missinninnuh nashpe 8nomwayeuonk.
97.1 IEhovah wutass8timun, muttaok weekontam8m8utch, monakish munnohhánash muskouantam8m8utch.
97.2 Mahtokqs kah pahkenai 8weenuhkongqun: wunnomwausseonk kah wussittumoonk wuttappuongane menuhkesuonk.
97.3 N8htau wunnegonuhkongqun, kah chikohswau ummatwomoh neit weenu.
97.4 Ukkuts[n]aumunash wohsum8m8ash muttaok: ohke wunnaumun onk nunnukshau.
97.5 Wadchuash sabahtaash onatuh wax ut anaquabit Jehovah: ut anaquabit uketass8tam8moh wame ohke.
97.6 Kesukquash nahtitteom8ash 8nomwausseonk, kah wame missinninnuog naumwog wussohsumoonk.
97.7 Wame neg waasumoncheg neuhkontunkane Manitt8 akojhettich, waeenomoncheg neukontunkane Manitto: n$noh waeenom8k kenaau wame Manittoog.
97.8 Sion wunn8tamun onk weekontamup, kah wuttaunoh Judah weekontamwog: newutche k8sittum8wongash woi Jehovah.
97.9 Newutche ken Jehovah kukqunnunkquap yeu ut wame muttaohket: ken kuttashinit anue onk nag wáme Manitt8og.
97.10 Kenaau womonogish Jehovah, sekeneam8k matchit: noh wadchanau ukketeahogkou8oh 8neetupanatam8moh, nah uppohquohwunoh wutch wunnutchegan8wout matcheetowog.
97.11 Wequaj ohkehtaeu wutche wunnomwausseaenuog, kah weekontam8onk wutch sampwutteahoncheg
97.12 Weekontam8unok Jehovah kenaau wunnomwausseogish: kah tabattantamóg mehquoantamóg 8neetupanatam8onk.
98.0 {Ketoohomwaonk.}
98.1 WOI ket8homok Jehovah wuske n8homaonk newutche mahche n8homaonk newutche mahche ussu monchanatamwe usseongash, wuttinohkou kah 8neetupanatamwe w8hpit ayimm88 wadchanuaonk.
98.2 Jehovah wahteauwahuwop 8wadchanuwaonk: 8nomwausseonk nahtitteop ut anaquabhettit penuohteaog.
98.3 Mehquántamup ummonaneteaonk kah 8nomwayeuonk nogque en weekuwout Israel: wame aongkouohkumukquash naumwog 8wadchan8waonk kum-Manitt8mun.
98.4 Weekontamwaeu wuttauatongqussek en Jehovah wame ohke mishontowagk, kah muskouantam8k, kah ann8hamunk tabuttantamoonk.
98.5 Ket8hamok Jahovah mashpe harp: nashpe harp, kah wadtauatongqussue ket8homaonk.
98.6 Weeche monopuhpequoanash, kah 8wadtauatongqussuonk cornet: weekontamwae mishant8wagk ut anaquabit Jehovah ketass8t.
98.7 Kehtoh mishont8waj, kah ne noh ohtag: muttaok kah neg noh wodtôhkutcheg.
98.8 Tommogkonog pohponkanitchahwohettich: wadchuog weekontamwuhhettich moaeu.
98.9 Anaquabit Jehovah, newutche peyau wussittumunat ohke: nashpe wunnomwausseonk wussittum muttaok, kah missinninnuog nashpe tatuppenehettuonk.
99.1 IEhovah wutass8timun missinninnuog nunnukshahettich: appu ut cherubimsut, ohke kukkuhqushquem8utch.
99.2 Jehovah missugken ut Sion: kah qunnonkquappu anue wame missinninnuh.
99.3 Nag wasittumohettich mohsag kah ohqunneungquok k8wesuonk, newutche wunnetupanatamweyeu8.
99.4 Ummenuhkesuonk ketass8t womantam wussittumoonk, kummenuhkehteoh sampweusseonk, kummenuhkehteoh sampweusseonk: kutussen wussittumoonk kah sampweusseonk ut Jakob[]ut.
99.5 Tahshin8k Jehovah kum-Manitt8mun, kah waussumok ut ukquensittassum8unit newutche wunneetupanatam.
99.6 Moses kah Aaron ut kenugku wussephausueneumut: kah Samuel kenukku nag weequetukeg 8wesuonk: weehquetumauaog Jehovah, kah noh wunnamp8homauoh nahog.
99.7 Ukkinn8nuh ut qunnukque mahtokqsit nanaiteauog 8wauwaongash, kah kuhk8aongash nish anummaóhpash.
99.8 Nag kenamp8hhamauoog woi Jehovah kum-Manitt8mun: ken God nag aquoantamauadt, qut kussasamatahwhopanneg wunnatinneham8wongash.
99.9 Tahshin8k Jehovah kum-Manitt8mun waussum8k ut 8neetupanatamwe wadchuut: newutche Jehovah kum-Manitt8mun wunneetupanatam.
100.0 {Tabuttantamoe ketoohomaonk}.
100.1 WEEkontamwae mishantowohtok Jehovah kenaau wame wutahtimoneunk
100.2 Weekontamwae waussumok Jehovah ket8hom8e peyunk anaquabit.
100.3 Wahteau8k, Jehovah n$noh God, n$noh kezhukqueagkup, qut matta kenawun kenawun n$noh ummissinninnumoh, kah wuttishepwussumoh wunnadtupp8wonganit.
100.4 Tabuttautamoe petutteagk 8squoantamut, kah ut wutchippinnutunkanit nashpe waeenomaonk tabuttantam8k 8nanatam8k 8wesuonk.
100.5 Newutche Jehovah wunneetou, ummonaneteaonk michemohteau: kah 8nomwayeuonk nagwutteohteau wame pometeonganit.
101.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
101.1 Nuttinn8homom monaneteaonk kah wussittum8onk: ken woi Jehvovah ket8homoush.
101.2 N8wáantammúun nuhhog en pahke mayut, woi aquompak kuppeyaauseh? pahketeaháe nuppompomusham nuttinnomukkomukqut.
101.3 Matta nupponam8 matcheseonk anaquabeh: nussekeneam wutanakausuongan8 nag pohchacheg, matta pissogqsháno nuhhogkat.
101.4 Musquantamwu metah nutamahkongqun: matta n8waheau matcheetowaenin.
101.5 Howan kemeu matchénont wetatteamunguh, noh nuttummetoh: noh páhtuanumweanungqussit, kah pahtuánumwutteáhhont, matta nutchéqunehteauóh.
101.6 Nuskesukquash naum pabahtanumutcheg wutohtuout, onk woh nag n8wetomukquog: noh pomshadt pahke mayut pish n8tinnunnúmun.
101.7 Noh as8k[i]komwe anakausit, matta woh n8weetô[m]uk8h: noh pann8waégit, matta woh appeu anaquabeh.
101.8 Nompoáeu nuppaguanôog wame matchesecheg ut wutohtimóneat: onk woh nuttummetoh wame matchesecheg wutch wut8tanit God.
102.0 {Onkkupinadt uppeantamoonk, kooshkoadt, onk sokanuk ummauunnittassuonk ut anaquabit Jehovah}.
102.1 NOOtash nuppeantamóonk, woi Jehovah: kah nummauonk peyaaúnukqush.
102.2 Ahque puttaghumah kuskesuk wutche neen wuttammepunnáon, ahch8sittah, weehquetumauúnon, teanuk namp8homah.
102.3 Newutche nukkesukkodtumash mohtupaémoash onatuh pukutáut, kah nuskonash chikohtaash onatuh kishkenau.
102.4 Nuttah togkodtamun, kah muss8pohteau onatuh askoskqut: newaj wanántam nummeechinat nupputtukqunnunk.
102.5 Newutche n8wadtauatongqussue chéquttumm8onk nummáhchekonáim.
102.6 Nutogqunneunkqus pellikanit ut touóhkomukqut: nutogqunneunkqus weésuut ut touóhkomukqut.
102.7 Nutaskwéteam, kah nutogqunneunkqus wameshashquésuut nonsieu ut woskéche kommuk.
102.8 Nummatwomog nummeech pukquée onatuh puttugquanunkanit: kah nukkinnetópánum n8tattam8onk nussippéquash.
102.9 Newutche nummeech pukquée onatuh puttugquanunkanit: kah nukkinnetópánum n8tattam8onk nussippéquash.
102.10 Newutche kutjishánitteaonk kah kummishe musquánitteaonk, newutche kuttáhshinip kah wonk kuppenuhkoneh.
102.11 Nukkesukkodtumash ogqunneunkquodtash onkaóhtaut amaeém8uk: onk nummuss8pás onatuh ashkoshqut.
102.12 Qut ken, woi Jehovah, pish kummichemap, kah kummequanumitteaonk en wame pometuonganit.
102.13 Pish kutomohkem, kah pish kummonanum Sion: newutche ahquompi kitteamonteánumonat, nux kuhquttum8e ahquompi peyaum8.
102.14 Newutche kuttinninnumog tapeneaúmwog ukqussukquanumash: kah womantamwog uppuppiseiyeum.
102.15 Nemehkuh penuohteaog wabesuóntamwog 8wesuonk Jehovah: kah wame tahs8tamwog ohkeit, kussohsumóonk.
102.16 Jehovah weekehteadt Sion, nogqussu ut wussohsum8onganit.
102.17 Wutt8antam uppeantam8onk noh nonsiyeuut, kah matta jishóntam8 nag uppeantam8ongan8.
102.18 Yeu pish wussukwh[ó]su ut paaúm8ug pometuonk: kah missinninnuog neg kezheámukùppanneg, waeenomáog Jehovah.
102.19 Newutche womompu wutch quanunkquapit 8neetupanatamwe week: wutch [kesukqut sukkut] Jehovah naum ohke.
102.20 Wunn8tamunat wutchéquttumm8onk kopshagkunit: wutompinneónat yeug káhtimutcheg nupp8onk.
102.21 Wahteauwáhuwonat 8wesuonk Jehovah ut Sion: kah wasumáonk ut Jerusalem.
102.22 Missinninnuog mo[é]hettit, kah as8tam8ongash waussumónat Jehovah.
102.23 Noh n8chumwéhteau nummenuhkesuonk ut mayut, tióhqutteau nukkesukkodtumash.
102.24 Nussip, woi num-Manit8m, ahque amáuneh nôeu ut nukkesukkodtumut, kukkodtum8mash pannuppóhtaash ut wame pometuonganit.
102.25 N8wadt kupponamup quenohtag ohke, kah kesukquash wutanakausuongash kenutchegash.
102.26 Nag pish mohtupaémoash, qut pish ken kummichemap, nux wame pish nekonneaiyeu8og onatuh hogk8onganit: nag pish kutôs8wunnôog onatuh petúsqushaonk, kah nag pish ôs8wunnôog.
102.27 Qut ken noh nan, kah kukkodtum8mash matta pish wohkukqushinninn8ash.
102.28 Wunnaumónneunk wutch kittinnumog pish nagwutteaéyeúog: kah wunneechann8oh pish menuhkhéoog ut anaquabean.
103.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
103.1 Wunnanum Jehovah, woi nukketeahogkou kah wame ne apetunkqueh 8neetupanatamwe wesuonk.
103.2 Wunnanum Jehovah woi nukketeahogkou: kah ahque wanontash wame 8nenehhuongash.
103.3 Nnoh kutahquoantamunk wame kummatcheseongash n$noh neetskehteau wame kummahchinnaongash.
103.4 N$noh pohquohwuttau kukketeaonk wutch paguanuonganit: noh kutchetukquabunuk 8womoausuwu womoausuonk, kah ukkitteamonteanitteae monaneteaongash.
103.5 Noh tapehteau kutt8n nashpe wanegukish: k8skenu8onk wuskehteáuun onatuh wompsukukquáut.
103.6 Jehovah wunnehteau sampweusseonk, kah wussittumoonk wame neg was[h]hitcheg.
103.7 Wahteauwaheau ummayash Mosesuh, wutusseongash ut wunnaumonat Israel.
103.8 Jehovah momaneteau, kah kitteamonteaneteau, chekeu musquantam, kah monat ummonanéteaonk.
103.9 Matta nagwutteáeu auskomuwau, asuh matta micheme musquanitteauou.
103.10 Matta kuttinhukk8unan neane matcheseog asuh mat kuttinonkquatunk8unnan neane panneusseog.
103.11 Newutche néane kesuk qunuhquok anue onk yeu ohke: nenukkukqun ummonaneteaonk nag quashoncheg.
103.12 Wutch wutcheksuau onk yeu pajeh wutchepwoou: na n8hque kutontahtunk qunnan kummatcheseonganunnonash.
103.13 Onatuh wut8shimáu kodtumonteanumont wunneechanoh, ne wuttinne Jehovah kitteamonteanumon neh quoshukqutcheh.
103.14 Newutche wahteau toh anhenogus: mehquoantam nuppuppissaiyeumun.
103.15 Qut wosketomp ukkesukkodtumash ogqunneonkquodtash moskehtuut: onatuh ohteakone uppeshaônit, ne wuttinnegin.
103.16 Newutche wabanuppamukaumun, neit mohtupaemo, kah ne ohtagkup matta wonk pish 8wahteauouun.
103.17 Qut ummonaneteaonk Jehovah wutche micheme onk yean micheme nag quoshoncheg: kah wussampweusseonk wunnechaneunk onk wunnechan8oh.
103.18 Neh nauaihteanutcheh 8n8waonk: kah neg mehquontogig wuttinn8waongash woh wutussenaoash.
103.19 Jehovah quaquoshweetam wutappuonk ut kesukquehtu kah wutass8tamoonk wunnanauwunumun wame.
103.20 Wunnanumo'k Jehovah kenaau wut-Angelsumoh mishimmenuhkeseog kah usseog wuttinn8waongash, kukkehtámog 8wodtauatonkqussue kutt8wonk.
103.21 Wunnanumok Jehovah kenaau wame wutayeuwehteomuh kenaau wuttinnumoh usseog uttoh unnantog.
103.22 Unnanumok Jehováh kenaau wame wutanakausuongash[,] papannuppe wutass8tam8onganit: wunnanum Jehovah woi nukketeahogkou.
104.1 Wunnanum Jehovah, woi nukketeahogkou, woi Jehovah num[-]Manitt8m muttae missugken: kuthogq sohsumoonk kah wohquanissuonk.
104.2 Kupputhogk8 kuhhog wequai onatuh hogk8onk: kupishquáginum kesukquash onatuh wadchukem8up.
104.3 Nohponum wuttabasseash wekit ut nippekontu, noh ayik matohqs wuttatuppequanumuk, noh pomushohkonau wunnuppuhwhunuh ut wabanit.
104.4 Noh ayeuau wut-Angelsumoh nashauauitt8in: wuttinnumoh n8n8wunnaeu n8htau.
104.5 Noh wunnohtau quenohtag ohkeh, matta woh ontohtan8h micheme
104.6 Kupputagguhhumun mônoi onatuh hogk8wonganit: nuppe wohqutohteauonk nish wadchuash.
104.7 Nag auskomádche wussemowog: 8wadtauatongqussuongan8 keneempomog nag kenupshaog.
104.8 Nish kukkuhquem8ash wadchuut nish wowussum8ash en 8nohteaouut, uttoh adt quoshaeihtamop.
104.9 K8nohtoh kuhkinneganash, matta woh anuushomun8ash nish matta woh qushkemun8ash nuhkuhkomunât ohke.
104.10 Ann8nau tohkekomeuh ut passohteaiyeuut, ne anitchuog wodchuuhkontu.
104.11 Wattattamwuhheaog nish noh puppinnashimwoh ut ohteakonit: touohkomukque assesog ontham ukkonkkuht8n8onk.
104.12 Kishke nag puppinshasog mamachekesukqut 8adshaiyeuog: nen kutt8waog ut wuttuhquinnehtu.
104.13 Wuttattippadtaou wadchúash wutch quanunkquok week: ummeechummuonk kutanakausuonk tapehteau ohke.
104.14 Ayim moskéhtuash nékinit wutche puppinnashimwog: kah wunnépogquash wutch wutauwohteaonganit wosketomp: onkwoh paudtau meetsuonk wutch ohkekontu.
104.15 Kah wine ne weekóntamwáhteunk wosketomp wuttah, kah pummee ayim8m8uk wuskesuk wohsittàut: kah petugqunnunk mánuhkehteaháhont wosketompuh.
104.16 Ummehtugkumash Jehovah numwóhteau, utchikupog ut Lebanon neahketeahpoh.
104.17 Nawuttit wadjisheahkoneau psuksésuk: kah stork 8wetu k8wáoh.
104.18 Kussókôiye wadchuash, wutusphuaongan8 touóhkomukque goatsoh: kah qussukquanuhtu wôhtuhquásog.
104.19 Kehtimau nanepâuzshádtuh utt8cheyeú8ut, nepâuz wahteau toh woh adt wayont.
104.20 Kutayim pohkenâi, onk nuhkon: neit wame puppinashimwussog touôhkomukqut uppimmaiinneau.
104.21 Wushkoshimwe qunnónouwemésog nehnehkóntamwog neawuttamwuhhettit: kah natinnehámwog ummeetsuongan8 wutch Godut.
104.22 Pashpishonche, mohmoéog kah sepsinwog assampamukquodtut.
104.23 Wosketomp sohham en wutanakausuonganit, kah 8tamanatamonganit na en wunnonk88wut.
104.24 Woi Jehovah tahshinnú8ash kutanakausuongash? kutussénash wamu ut waantam8onganit: ohket numwohteau k8ween[a]ieetuonk.
104.25 Kah missi kah mishigski kehtoh, uttoh adt pumáhhomwúhhettit matta woh wôáun[un]kig, naneeswe papeississitcheg kah matikkénukeg puppinashimwog.
104.26 Na pomushaum8g kuht8nogquosh, noh p8tab kuttaiyimau, nawuttit pûhpin neat.
104.27 Yeug wame kutannaónukquog, onk woh n[a]g kutassamóog nish noh utt8che.
104.28 Uttohassamadt ne mukkinnumunneau: k8wôhshwunum kenukutcheg onk nag kuttáphéoog nashpe wanégik.
104.29 Kupputtagguhhum kuskesuk, nag wuttammepunnáog: kutamaùnumun wunnashauongan8, onk nupp8og, onk quinnuppéog en puppissiyeúunneat.
104.30 Kutann8n kenashaúanit onk nag kezhéaog: kah k8skéhteóh woskéit ohke.
104.31 Wussohsum8onk Jehovah michemohteau: Jehovah weekontam ut wutanakausuonganéhtu,
104.32 Móninneam ohke, kah nunnukeshau: mussinnum wadchúash, onk nish qussóhtóouash.
104.33 Nukkutt8homau Jehovah tisohkepomantam: nuttinn8homau tabuttantam8ongash num-Manitt8m, ash papomantamop.
104.34 Nunnatwânumáonk weetumungquot: n8weekontam ut Jehovah.
104.35 Matcheseáenúog mohtupaéhettich wutch ohket, kah ahque wonk matcheetowaenúutch: wunnânum Jehovah woi nukketeahogkou waeenom8k Jehovah.
105.1 WOi tabuttantamok Jehovah, wehquetumok 8wésuonk: wahteauwahuwagk wutússeongash ut kenugke missinninnútu.
105.2 Ket8hamok, an8hamok ket8hamaongash: wéogquttom8k wame ummonchánatamwe anakausuongash.
105.3 Waeenomok ut wunneetupanatamwu 8wesuonganit: wuttahh8wóash weekontam8m8utch neg natinnewhóncheg Jehovah.
105.4 Natinneh8k Jehovah kah ummenuhkesuonk: natinneham8k wuskesuk micheme.
105.5 Mehquontam8k monchanatamwu wutanakausuongash nish asépash: ummonchanatam8wongash, kah wussittum8ongash ut wutt8nut.
105.6 Woi kenaau Abraham 8skannemuneoh: kenaau wunneechanoh Jakob pepénaômpuh.
105.7 Noh Jehovah kum-Manitt8mun: 8sittum8ongash yeuut wame muttaohkeit.
105.8 Mehquantam 8n8waonk micheme: wuttinn8wáonk ne án8wop nequt muttannongane pometeongash.
105.9 Ne 8n8wáonk ayikup nashpe Abrahamoh, kah wadchadchekéimáonk Isaakoh.
105.10 Kah ummenuhkéhteaun ne nan Jakoboh, wutche naumatuonk: kah Israeloh wutch machemohtag wunn8waonk.
105.11 An8wadt, ken kuttinnumaush ohket Canaan, kutahtaongane ohteuk.
105.12 Ohguhshettit wosketompaog: nux, kutohgussumw8, kah kuppénuwohteamw8 naut.
105.13 Aáhettit wutch wutohtimóneat onk yaan wutohtimóneat: kah wutch as8tam8onganit, en onkatogane missinninnûut.
105.14 Matta unnánumôou howáne woskéhuk naghok, nux áushkómau ketahs8timwoh wutche nagumôu.
105.15 Ahque mussinh saséqunog, kah ahque woskéheuk nummanittowompomog.
105.16 Wonk weehquetum mashógqunneáonk ut ohket: póhquanum wame anwôhh8unne petugqunnunk.
105.17 Noh an8nau wosketompoh negonáeu nag wutche, Joseph noh magumukup wutche wuttinnúmun.
105.18 Noh wusseetash woskéhuk8m8 m8óshagquogtag: m8ôhshog aúm8 ukketeahogkôunit.
105.19 Onk nô pajeh wuttinn8waonk paaúm8uk: wuttinn8waonk Jehovah qutchhukqun.
105.20 Ketass8t an8teám8, kah wutómpinneuh: nanaanuaenin ut missinninnútu, kah wussohwhunoh.
105.21 Wutáyeuoh wunnánaunnumenin week: kah nanaánumun wame wutahtóonk.
105.22 Onk woh tahtágkuppinau wussontimaumoh unnantog: kah onk woh kuhk8tomauau ukkéhchaiyeumoh waantamóonk.
105.23 Kah Israel peyau Egypt, kah Jakob pen8wahteao ut ohkeit Ham.
105.24 Kah m8chekéheau ummissinninnumoh misheu, kah umm8cheke menêhkheuh onk neh ummatwom8oh.
105.25 Qunnuppinum wuttahh8woash sékeneauonat ummissinninneúmoh, as8kekomonat wuttinninnumoh.
105.26 An8nau, Mosesoh wuttinninnumoh: kah Aaronoh neh pepenaúmpoh.
105.27 Nag nahtitteáog ukkehkinneasuongan88ash kenugke nahoh: kah ummonchanatam8ongash ut ohkeit Ham.
105.28 An8nau pohkenáiyeuoh, onk ayim pohkenái: kah matta pa[n]néusseog wuttinn8waonk.
105.29 Qunnuppinnum nuppéash wusqueheonkanú8ut, kah paguanau namohsoh.
105.30 Ohke pas8au monaoh tenogkequasog: ut wutchamberum8óut kehtass8tamwog.
105.31 Ket8kóp, onk monaog peyâog m8sesúhquog, kah yeuhquog wame ne ohkit.
105.32 Sokanonteau mussegon wutche sokanoni kah n8n8unneau ohke.
105.33 Kah sóquetahham weenómesippaguash, kah figse mehtugquash, kah póhquetahham matugquash ne ohkeit.
105.34 Ket8hkop kah quahquequéshontáog peyauog, kah m8páog, matta woh wâômukeg.
105.35 Kah mahchep8og wame wunnépaquash ne ohkeit, kah mahchep8og ummeechummúonk wutohtuout.
105.36 Kah nushau mohtommégitcheh neit ohkeit: negonne wame ummenuhkesuongan8.
105.37 Kah wussohh8wu[n]oh ohtóog silver kag gold: kah matta pasuk n8chemwése neadtashaùwadthettit.
105.38 Egypt weekontamup, nag monchéhettit: newutche wábesuongan8 nag wunohkukkongqunneau.
105.39 Sepagnunum matokqs upputtagúhwhou: kah n8tau 8wôhsumauóh nukkonáeu.
105.40 Weehquetumohettit, uppaudtaoh p8hp8hqutteh kah 8wamepwuhheuh petukqunnunk wutch kesukqut.
105.41 Wohshinnum qussuk, kah nippe wuttitch8wan: nunnobpahteaouut pomitchuwan nippe onatuh Sepuut.
105.42 Newutche mehquoantam 8neetupanatamwe ukquosh8waonk: Abramoh wuttinneumoh.
105.43 Kah sohh8wunau ummissinninnumoh nashpe weekontam8onk pepenauonche nashpe ket8homaonk.
105.44 Kah aninnumauau wutohkeiash penuohteaog: onk nompanumwog wutanakausuongan8 missinninnuog.
105.45 Onk woh usseog ukkuhk8aongash kah nanaiheaog wuttinnaumatuongash waeenomok Jehovah.
106.1 Waeenomok Jehovah: woi tabuttantam8k Jehovah newutche wunnetou, newutche ummonaneteaonk michemeyeu8.
106.2 Howan woh mahshont8sog mogagish wutanakausuongash Manit? howan woh nahtitteadt wame tabuttantamoongash?
106.3 OOnanumoog nag nanaaihteunkig wussittumoonk, kah noh sampweusset nagwutteaeu.
106.4 Mequanumeh woi Jehovah, nashpe kukkitteamonteanumaonk kummissinninnumog: woi nattouwahhe náshpe k8wadchanuwaonk.
106.5 Onk woh nunnaum 8netuonk pepen8wadt, onk woh n8wekontam 8wekontam8onganit kutohtimoin: onk woh k8woweenomsh weeche kutohtoonk.
106.6 Nummatchesemun weeche n8shinnonog; nutussemun matcheseonk, nummahche neeskesemun.
106.7 N8shinnonog matta wahteauoog kummonchanatam8ongash ut Egypt; nag matta mehquoantamoog monakish kummonaneteaongash, qut umm8m8sqheouh ut ketahhannit, msqui ketahhannit?
106.8 Qut uppohquohwhunoh newutche 8wesuonk, woh wahteauwahuwonat ummishe menuhkesuonk.
106.9 Kah auskontam msque kehtoh, nunnobpau8p: nemehkuh uppannuppuwunuh m8noiyeuut onatuh touohkomukqut.
106.10 Kah uppohquohwunoh nahog wutch wunnutchegan8out jishanumoncheg: onk pohquohwunoh wutch matwaog wunnutchegan8wo[u]t.
106.11 Onk nuppe nogkuhkouau ummatwom8oh, onk nag matta pasuk squinneanoun,
106.12 Neit wunnamptámwog ukkutt8wongash: an8homoog tabuttantamoongash.
106.13 Teanuk wananatamwog wutánakausuongash: matta pahtau8og ukken8nuwaonk.
106.14 Qut m8cheke matchekodtantamwog ut touohkomukqut: kah qutcheheaog Goduh ut touohkomuk.
106.15 Kah wuttinnumauoh ne weequetumungqut: qut 8nausheau nag ukketeahogkounóuh.
106.16 Kah ishkounoog Mosesoh ut tuppuksinn8onganit kah Aaron 8neetupanatam8moh.
106.17 Ohke wôhshweem8 kah misheask8 Dathanuh: kah nuhkuhkauou Abiram weechauoncheh.
106.18 Kah n8tau nashqunau naut weechaugwutcheh: n8n8neau chikkoswau matcheet8woh.
106.19 Kezheaog Calfeoh ut Horeb: kah waussumaog mohtuppohtaeu nuñeukontonkoh.
106.20 Yeu wuttinne os8wunnumunneau wussohsumoonk, agqueneungqussit ox noh meechik moskehtuash.
106.21 Nag wunnanumaog Goduh uppohquohwussunenum8uh: noh mahche usseit mógagish ut Egypt.
106.22 Monchanatámwe ânakausuongash wutohket Ham: kah uhqunneunkquokish kishke msqui ketahhannet.
106.23 Newaje n8wadt, nuppaguanoog: mat Moses neh pepenauoncheh neepauokis anaquabit adtauwunneusik woh ukqushkinnumunat ummusquantam8onk iskont na[h] uppaguanuh.
106.24 Nux wutjishontamunnaop kohkodtantamuk ohke: matta wunnamptamoog wuttinn8waonk.
106.25 Qut m8m8sk8waog ut weekuwout kah matta kukkehtamoog 8wadtauatonkqussuonk God.
106.26 Newajeh ayeuuhkonittue tohshinumauont wunnutcheg: onk woh uppaguanonat ut touohkomuk.
106.27 Woh u[k]kepuhkonat 8skannemunnuuh kenugke wutohtimoneat; onk woh náh wusseahwonat ut ohkeit.
106.28 Kah wunn8waog weeche Baal Peoroh: kah meechwog mag8wongash nag napukeg.
106.29 Yeu wuttin m8sqheonneau nashpe neane natwoantamohettit, kah wesaushaonk nah wunuhkuhkauoh.
106.30 Neit Phineas neepau, kah sampweussittumoonk wuttussen, neit wesaushaonk o[n]tappu.
106.31 Kah yeu wussittumauon wutch sampweusseonganit: ut wame pomet[o]onganit micheme.
106.32 Kah umm8sqheouh ut penuanittue nippeit: onk nemehkuh Moses sasamakuhwhau nagwutchu.
106.33 Newutche m8sqheaog wunnashauanitto, newaje koshkomme matcheunnont ut wussisset8nit.
106.34 Matta pagwottauoog wutohtimoneash papaume nish anompash Jehovah.
106.35 Qut kenukshaog penuwohteaut, kah kodnetuhtoog wutanakausuongan8oash.
106.36 Kah nag waussumaog, nag wuttinneuhkontunkaneu Manitt8m8oh, neghog ahpehhanu8og nagwutchu.
106.37 Nux, nag sephaus8og wunnaumonaoh kah wuttaun8woh Mattannitt8h.
106.38 Kah soksquaheaog nah mo woskhuwanegeh, 8sqheongan8 wunnechan8oh kah wuttaun8oh: n$nag maghettiche en nunneuhkontunkanu Manitt8moh Canaan, kah ohke nishketeauun nashpe wsqueheonk.
106.39 Yeu wuttin nisketeauunneau nehenwonche wutanakausuongan8oash: onk mamussuog wutch nehenwonche wunnatwontam8ongánoóash.
106.40 Newajeh Jehovah ummusquantam8onk ayeuuhkonittue nashqunna nashpe ummissinninnumoh: newajeh ohquontaog nehenwonche wutahtoonk
106.41 Onk noh ummagunoh ut wunnutcheganoout penuwohteaog: kah nag sekeneauuncheg nah wunanaunouh.
106.42 Kah ummatwom8uh woskehukquog: onk agwappeheoog nag wunnutchegan8wout.
106.43 M8cheket uppohquohwhunoh nahoh: qut umm8m8sqheouh nashpe ukkinn8nittuongan8: kah n8chumweheoog newutche ummatcheseongan8.
106.44 Qut ukkitteamonteanumoh ut wutonkapunnaoont, n8tog ummauongan8.
106.45 Onk mehquoantam 8n8waonk wutche naghog, kah auskoiantam neaunummonakish monanéteaonganash.
106.46 Kah wutayimauoh ukkitteamonteanummonaout nag wame masinohteacheg.
106.47 Wadchanean woi Jehovah num$Manitt8mun, kah mómounninnean wutch kenugke penuwohteaut, onk woh kuttabuttantamauunnumun ut wunneetupanatamwe k8wesuonganit kah weekontam8wontamunat kuttabuttantamonteaonk.
106.48 Wunnanumunaj Jehovah um-Manitt8moh Israel wutch machemohtag onk yean machemohtag: kah wame missinninnuog n8wahettich Amen, waeenomók Jehovah.
107.1 Tabuttantamok Jehovah, newutche noh wunneetou, newutche ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
107.2 Nag pohquohwhunoncheh Jehovah ne n8wahettich: uttiyeuh pohquohwhunumpuh wutch wunnutcheganit matwau.
107.3 Kah n$nah ummagkinuh wutche wutohtimoneát, wutche wutchepwoáyeu, kah wutch wutchesúau kah wutch nannummau, kah wutch sôanaiyeu.
107.4 Wâônuog ut touohkomuk matta máanóg: wanne miskaum8og otan 8tohkónneaôont.
107.5 Kadtupwéhettit, kah konkuht8nohettit: ukketeahogkôunn8oh sôunumwoh ut wuhhogkaóut.
107.6 Neit mauunnitteauwaog Jehovah wutche wuttammehpunnaongan8: onk nah uppohquohwhunoh wutch 8taméhpunnaongan8out.
107.7 Kah wussagkompaganuh en sampwe mayut: onk woh nag aúog 8tanit toh woh wodohkéhettit.
107.8 Woi waeenomáhettit Jehovahnoh, wutche 8neetowonk: kah wutch monchanatamwe anakaúsuongash en woskeetompaog wunnaumónaóut.
107.9 Newutche tápheau kodtántamwe keteahogkôunoh: kah tâpupwúhheau kodtupp8wu keteahogkôunoh wanégik.
107.10 Neg apitcheg pohkenaouut, kah wutonkauhtomut nupp8onk: tohtogkupséhettit onkapunnaonganit, kah m8óhshogwohtogwash.
107.11 Newutche ayeukóntamwog wuttinn8wáongash God: kah mamánauwontamwog ukkinn8nuwáonk quanunkquappit.
107.12 Newajeh ayig hohpómau metah nashpe anakausuonk: nag kepsháog, onk matta howane aninnumunk8og.
107.13 Neit mauunnitteauáog Jehovah ut 8tamehpunnonnaóont: kah uppohquóhwhunoh nahog wutch 8taméhpunónaôout.
107.14 Wussohh8wunoh wutch pohkenaooúut, kah wutch wutonkaóhtomut nupp8onk: kah poskishadtau wuttohtogkuppissuonganóash.
107.15 Woi wosketompaog waeenomahettit Jehovah wutche 8neetowonk: kah wutche um̃onchanatamwananakausuongash ut wosketompaog wunneechan8wout.
107.16 Newutche pokshadtaúop wompûhshogque kuppuhhoúnash: kah póhquetahham m8óhshogque neepatúhquonkash.
107.17 Mattammagwog onkapunnáog newutche uppanneseonganoash, kah ummatcheseonganash.
107.18 Ukketeahogkôun8oh ôhquánittamwoh nish noh unummeechumogkod: onk pas8sukkómwog 8squoantamash nupp8onk.
107.19 Neit mauunitteauâog Jehovah wadtamehpunáhettit: uppohquohwhunoh wutch 8tamehpunanaóont.
107.20 Ann8nau wuttinn8waonguh, onk nah wunneetskeheuh: kah uppohquohwhunoh wutch uppaguaninneaôont.
107.21 Woi wosketompaog waeenomáhettit Jehovah wutche 8nene`hhuwáonk, kah wutche ummonchanatamwe anakausuongash ut wosketompáog wunneechan8woont.
107.22 Kah nag maghettich tabuttantamwae mag8ongash kah muskauánatamwe, wahteauwahuwáhettich wutanakausuongash.
107.23 Nag áoncheg kehtahhannit, ut kuht8nogquehtu: wutanakausuongan8 ohtag nuppekontu.
107.24 Yeug naumwog wutanakausuonganash Jehovah, ummonchanatam8wongash ut m8náiyeuut.
107.25 Newutche an8team8, kah ayim mishshetahshin: noh tohshinont tukk8oh.
107.26 Nag tahshéog en kesukqut: kah wômussúog en m8náiyeuut: keteahogkôun8oh mohtupaéoh nashpe wuttaméhpunáonk.
107.27 Kehkepshaog, kah kehkeétukquommog onatuh kogkeissippamou: kah wôwohquiànum8og.
107.28 Neit mauunnitteauwaog Jehovah wadtamehpunáhettit: kah nah wussohh8wunoh wutch 8tamehpunnaongan8ôut.
107.29 Aippanehteau mishittashineuh neit tuhk8óg mánunappûog.
107.30 Neit weekontamwog newutche mánunappuog: nemehkuh uppâs8oh ne ohke kodtantaminit.
107.31 Woi wosketompaog waeenomáhettit Jehovah wutche 8net8onk: kah wutche ummonchanatamwanakausuongash ut wosketompaog wunnaumonnaont.
107.32 Nag misheheahettich ut ummukkinneongan8wout missinninnùog, kah waasumahettich ut ummukkinneongan8óut nanaánuacheg.
107.33 Os8wunum sépuash ut touohkomuk, ôs8wunum tohkékomuash en nunnabohteaóuut.
107.34 Mahmusségik ohkée ahquékin: newutche ummatcheetowongan8 neg noh wadohkitcheg.
107.35 Touohkomuk quinnuppinnum en nuppeyeu8ut: kah nanabohteáagish tohkékomwúhteau.
107.36 Kah na 8tohkéheun kodtupwunutcheh, onk woh ququashwehtamwog ayeuongane otánat.
107.37 Onk woh ohkehteaog ohteuhkónash, kah woh ohkehteáog weenominneohtekonash woh adtnegik m8cheke meechummú8onk.
107.38 Kah nah 8nânumoh, onk nag monáog; kah matta unnánumaou wunnétasseumoh ohguhségig.
107.39 Wonk, ohguhshéóog kah n8chumwehêoog nashpe woskehettúonk, 8tammepunnaongan8, kah auwohkontánumóonk.
107.40 Wussóhkanumauau ôhquanittuonk sontimoh: kah wauwónheuh ut touohkomuk uttoh mo adt mán8k.
107.41 Qut onch qunuhquoshau matchekuoh wutch wuttammehpunnaonganash: kah wutayimauoh weetu mishôénat onatuh flokut.
107.42 Sampweusseaenuog pish wunnaumunneau, kah pish weekontamwog: kah wame matcheseonganog pish kupputt8naéog.
107.43 Howan waantog kah yeushog káhkinneâsit: nag pish wahtamwog ukkitteamonteánitteae 8womoausuonk Jehovah.
108.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
108.1 WOi Manit nuttah menuhkohteau: pish nukket8homom, kah k8woeenomush, nashpe nussohsumóonk.
108.2 T8hkish psaltery kah harp: nunnómpoáeu t8hkem.
108.3 K8waweenomush, woi Jehovah, ut kenugke missinninnúhtu: kah kuttinn8homoush tabuttantam8ongash ut kenugke wutohtimóneat.
108.4 Newutche kummonáneteaonk missi ongkouwe kesukqut: kah k8nomwaonk mussisshin ut mahtoksqut.
108.5 Anuunkqussehetteash, woi Manit, kesukquash: kah kussohsumòonk waábe ohtaj onk wame ne ohke.
108.6 Noh womónat woh pohquohwhunau: kuttinohkou wadchanukquttei, kah namp8hamah.
108.7 God n8wop ut 8neetupanatam8onganit: pish n8weekontám, pish nutchippun Sechem: kah nukquogquádhum 8nôuhkôi Succoth.
108.8 Gilead nuttaihe, Manasseh nuttaihe, kah Ephraim ummenuhkesuonk nuppuhkuk: Judah noh ayik nuttinnaumatuonk.
108.9 Moab nukkutshahkukquom, nutánuwôohteam nummokis Edom, nummuskouanatam8won Philistiansog.
108.10 Howan pas8queh menuhke 8tanat? howan sagkompáginit en Edom?
108.11 Sun~ummatta ken woi Manit, noh sôhwhókônukqueógkup? kah sun~um̃atta ken woi God k8weechaiómun nutayeuhkoñanónut?
108.12 Aninaumaiinnean wutch wuttammepunnónat: newutche tahn8cheyeu8 wutaninnôsuonk wosketomp.
108.13 Nashpeu God pish nummenuhkesénan, newutche noh pish tahtahskúshkoauont kummatwómunnonuh.
109.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk} David.
109.1 Ahque netashúash, woi Manit, ken wâussumun.
109.2 Newutche wutt8n8 matchetowog, kah wutt8n8 as8keaodteaum8og woshweem8, ayeuuhkone neen nuttinunkquog ayeuuhkone nen nashpe pann8wae meenan.
109.3 Kah nukquinupuhkongquog nashpe sekeneadtue kutt8wongash: kah nutayeuquog tahn8che.
109.4 Newutche n8womoausuonk, onk nag nummatwomog: qut neen nuppeantam.
109.5 Kah nag nutunkquatunkquog máchuk wutche wanegik, kah sekeneáadtuonk wutch n8womoausuonk.
109.6 Anuwe pon matcheetowaenu ut nagum, kah Satan neepaitch ut wuttinohkôunit.
109.7 Wussumit, wussumunaj nuppunnat: kah uppeantamoonk matcheseongannutch.
109.8 Ukkesukkodtumash ogguhsen8utch; onkatuk neemunutch wuttanohsuonk.
109.9 Wunnechanoh mo wut8shunnéitch kah ummittamwussoh sekousquaunitch.
109.10 Wunneechan8oh nagwutteaeu nanwaihettich kah weenshaunitch, natinneham8hettich uppetukqunnunkan8 wonk ut touwe ayeuonganehtu.
109.11 Woskehuwaenin amaunich wame wutahtauonk: kah penuwot matchehtaunitch wutanakausuonk.
109.12 Ahque howan monanumonch: kah ahque howan kitteamonteanumonch wuttouaesumoh wunneechan8oh.
109.13 Wutontseonk tummetahhamunaj ne nahohtôohtag pometeonk, 8weseuonkan8 jishkhamunaj.
109.14 Ummatcheseongash 8shoh mehquantamunaj ut anaquabit Jehovah: kah ummatcheseonk ohkasoh ahque jishkhomunaj
109.15 Nish nagwutteohtaj anaquabit Jehovah, onk woh tummehtham wàánumaongan8 wutch ohkekontu.
109.16 Newutche matta mehquoantamop monánekon, qut woskeheau matchekuoh, kah quenáhukqunutche, onk woh nushonat pohqutteahonutcheh.
109.17 Nean8womontog ummatchenáneteaonk, neneh peyaaunukqutch: neane matta tápeneaum8g wunaneteaonk, nene nô8sukkongqutch.
109.18 Neane hogqut matchenaneteaonk onatuh hogk8onganit: nein peyaaunukqutch ut wunnogkussit onatuh nippeit, kah ogqunneungquodtich pummeit ut wuskonut.
109.19 Tatupontaj wuthogk8onganit neagqut: kah upputtugquobis ne padtukquobussit nagwutteaeu.
109.20 Yeu wutonkquatunkanehettich nummatwomog wutch Jehovahut: kah neg machenóncheg ayeuuhkone nuketeahogkou[]noh.
109.21 Qut usseansheh woi Jehovah Manit, newutche k8wesuonk: newutche kummonanteaonk wunnegin: pohquohwusseh.
109.22 Newutche nummatchek kah nukquenahik, kah nuttah n8chumwetahwau nuttinnomhogkat.
109.23 Nutamaim onatuh onkohohteau aumaitcheh: nuppâpamunkônit onatuh quaquequéshont.
109.24 Nukkuttukquog n8chumwesuog nashpe matmeetsein: kah n8weyaus wannehteau wunnogk8onk.
109.25 Nag nukkekomukuppanneg: moneaihettit, nunnukkukquosháog.
109.26 Naninnumah woi Jehovah num-Manitt8m, unn8wadchaneh neaunag kummonaneteaonk.
109.27 Onk woh nag wahteauog yeu kenutcheg: ken Jehovah kutussenap.
109.28 Matchenánitteahettich, qut ken wunnanumiteash: nag neepaahettit akodjhettich, qut kittinneum muskouantaj.
109.29 Nummatwomog hogquehettich akodchuonk: kah hogquehettich nehenwonche wunnanwayeuongan8 onatuh hogk8onganit.
109.30 Nummishuwaussum Jehovah ut nutt8nut: nux n8wawussum ut kenugku monacheg.
109.31 Newutche pish neepau wuttinohkôunit matcheku: 8wadchanonat wutch neh waussumónutche ukketeahogkôunoh.
110.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
110.1 Manit unnau num-Manitt8moh, apsh nuttinohkounit, nô pajeh nutayéuonaonk kummatwomog, kuttappannehtuonk.
110.2 Jéhovah pish an8nau kummenuhkesue pogkomunk wutch Sion: nanaunh ut nôeu kummatwomut.
110.3 Kummissinninnumog pish wuttinanatamunneáu, ne kesukok menuhkesean, ut 8neetuongane wunneetupanatam8onganit wutch nompoae oontomukout kutahto k8skenue neechipog.

110.5 Manit ut kuttinnohkounit pish pannuppetahwhau kétass8timwoh musquantog.

111.1 Waeenomok Jéhovah: nowoweenom Jehovah nashpe mamusse nuttahhut, ummukkinneonganit sampwesitcheg, kah ut moeonganit.

115.1 Matta neenaan, woi Jehovah, matta neenaan aninnumaiinnean waeenomóonk; qut k8wesuonk sohsum8ontamunach, newutche kummonaneteaonk kah k8nomwâyeuonk.
115.2 Tohwutch woh pénuwot unn8wadt, yeuyeu uttiyeu um-Manitt8m8oh?
115.3 Qut kum-Manitt8mun ut kesukquehtu: mahche usseu nish noh kodt[a]ntamun.
115.4 Wuttinnukontunkanu Manitt8m8oh silvertù8woh kah goldeú8woh: wutanakausuongan8 wunnutchegan88ash wosketompaog.
115.5 Nag wutt8núog, qut matta ket8hkau8og wuskesuk8og, qut matta naum8og.
115.6 Nag wehtauog8og, qut matta n8tam8og, wutchanuog, qut matta munnóntatteaoúog.
115.7 Wunnutcheganúog, qut matta mussúnnum8og: wusseetuog, qut mat pomushauóog assa mat ket8hkauóog ut ukquttunkanouwóut.
115.8 Neg kezheoncheg wutógqunneunkqussinneáoh: kah nish noh pasuk noh nah pabahtanumont.

115.10 Woi week Aaron pabahtánum Jehovah, noh wutannohsuenúm8oh kah wutogqunnégan8oh.
115.11 Kenaau quashógish Jehovah, pabahtanumok Jehovah: kah nnah wutannohsuenúm8oh, kah wutogqunnégan8oh.
115.12 Jehovah kummomehquánumugqun, k8nanumugqun, wunnánittam weekuwóash Israel: wunnanittam week Aaron.
115.13 Nah wunnánumou quoshánutcheh Jehovah: mátekénutche kah papéississinitcheh.
115.14 Jehovah pish náno kumishhukou kah náno: kenaau kah keneechânuwóog.
115.15 Kenaau k8na[n]umugkou Jehovah, noh ayikup kesuk kah muttaok.
115.16 Kesuk nux kesukquash wuttaihe Jehovah: qut ohket wuttinnunnumaun wunnaumonauh wosketompaog.
115.17 Nupp8og matta waeenomau8og Jehovah; asa mat neg wómussitcheg in chequnapinneat.

119.1 WUnnaánumog pannuppe pahkositcheg ut mayut, neg pomshacheg wuttinnaumatuonganit Jehovah.
119.2 Wunnanumoóg nag nanaáitunkig 8wauwaongash: kah néh natinneohukqutche nashpe mamusse wuttah.
119.3 Nag wonk matta matcheseog: auog ummayut.
119.4 Kutussumunnonup, nánaaihteau8k nuttinnaumatuongash menuhkeu.
119.5 Woi nummayash sampwuhteaumuk, nanawehteáuunat kukkuhk8waongash.
119.6 Neit pish matta nutakodchu, quttiántamon wame kuttinn8waongash.
119.7 K8wáeenomsh nahpe sampwutteaheáonk: mahche netuhtaon kussampwewussittum8ongash.
119.8 Nen nanaáihteoh kukkuhk8waongash: ahque papaquannu ohquanumeh.
119.9 Uttoh woh wuttin wusken pahketeauun ummayash: nashpe nunnukqussit neaunag kukkutt8onk.
119.10 Nashpe mamusse nuttah kenatinne[a]whush: ahue wáónittei wutche kuttinn8waonganit.
119.11 Kuttinn8waonk nutadtahtauun ut nuttahut, onk woh matta kummatchenehenno.
119.12 K8nanumit ken Jehovah: kuhk8tumah kukkuhk8waongásh.
119.13 Nashpe mussisset8nash n8wahteauwahuwam wame kutt8ne wussittum8ongásh.
119.14 N8weekontamup ut k8wauwaongáne mayut, neaudtashik wame weenaieetuongash.
119.15 Nunnatwoantam ut kuttinn8waonganit, kah nanaomputtam kummayash,
119.16 Nuttapeneamwah nuhhog kukkuhk8waonganit mátta n8wananâtam8 kuttinn8waonk.
119.17 Mishonkquatau kittinninneum, onk woh nuppomantam kah woh nanaaihteoh kuttinn8waonk.
119.18 Wohshinish nuskesukquash onk woh nunnaum monchánátam8wongash ut kuttinnaumatuonganit.
119.19 Nuppen8wóhteau yeu ohket, ahque adtohtah kuttinn8waongashh.
119.20 Nukketeahogkou pokshau nontweontamon k8sittum8ongash nagwutteaeu.
119.21 Kutauskomomp pittuanumutcheg matchenanumutcheg, né pañeoncheg wutch kuttinn8waonganit.
119.22 Ontohtah kekont8wonk kah jishanittuonk newutche nanaaihteoh k8wauwaongash.
119.23 Sontimoog wonk appuog, kah nutayeuuhkonittue weadtimukquog qut kuttinneum natwontamup kukkuhk8waongash.
119.24 K8wauwaongash wonk nûttapeneaum8ungash, kah neg kahtimitcheg.
119.25 Nuhketeahogkou pissógquomou papissiyeúut: quaquakqheh neaúnag kuttinn8waonk.
119.26 N8wateauwáhuwop nummayaassh, kah ken8taip: kuhk8tomah kukkuhk8waongash.
119.27 Wahtamwaheh kittinn8waongane mayash, onk pish n8weogquttum kumonchanatamwe anaksausuongash.
119.28 Nukketeahogkou mohtuppáeu nashpe neuantam8onk: menehkheh neaunag kuttinn8waonk.
119.29 Pannep8uneh wutch pann8wae mayut, kah aninnumah nanouwe kittinnaumatuonk.
119.30 Nuppepénum wunnomwayeue may: k8sittam8ongash nupponamunash anaquabeh.
119.31 Nummenhuhkinnum k8wauwaongash: woi Jehovah akodjheh.
119.32 Nummittumasham kuttinn8waongane may: mishshehtauan nuttah.
119.33 Kuhk8tumah, woi Jehovah, kukkuhk8waongane may, onk pish nánawehteauunash na ut wohkukquoshik.
119.34 Aninnumah wohwohtamoonk neit nunnanaih kittinnaumatuonk: nux, nosweetamun nashpe mamusse nuttah.
119.35 Ayeuweh nuttônat kuttinn8waongane may: newutche nish nuttapeneaumunash.
119.36 Nuttah uss8utaush k8wauwaonganit onk matta en i[á]hchewontamunát.
119.37 Qunnuppunush nuskesukquash wutche naumunat tahn8cheyeu8uk: kah quaquakqheh en kummayut.
119.38 Menehketeau kuttinn8waonk kittinninneum: noh quoshhukquean.
119.39 Quinnuppenumah nukkekomitteaonk ne quohtam, newutche k8sittum8wongash wu[n]negenash.
119.40 Kusseh, nummishshe kodtantam kuttinn8waongash; quaquakqheh ut k8nomwausseonganit.
119.41 Kummonaneteaongash wonk peyauunukquttei, woi Jehovah, k8wadchanuwaonk neaunag kukkutt8wonk.
119.42 Neit toh woh nuttinne namp8hamau kehkómit howan: newutche nuppâbahtantam kuttinn8waonk.
119.43 Kah ahque papaquanne amaunsh wunnamuhkutee kutt8onk wutch nutt8nut; newutche nutannous ut k8sittam8onganit.
119.44 Nemehkuh pish nanawaheoh kittinnaumatuonk yeauyatcheh, micheme kah micheme.
119.45 Kah pish nanouwe pomusham: newutche nunnátinneahham kukkuhk8tomuhteaongash.
119.46 Kah nuttinn8wam k8wauwaongash anaquabhettit ketahs8tamwog, kah matta pish nutakodchuh.
119.47 Kah n8wekontamwah nuhhog ut kuttin8waonganit nish womantamónish.
119.48 Kah wonk nunnetchegash nuttashinum ken kuttinn8waonganit nish womantamónish: kah nunnatwontam kukkuhk8waongash.
119.49 Mehquontash kuttinn8waonk ut kittinneumut, uttiyeu annóoshikqueáp.
119.50 Yeu n8niyeuonk ut nutonkapunnaonganit newutche kuttinn8waonk nukquaquakqhúk.
119.51 Pittuanum8og m8cheke nutahánehtunkquog: qut onch askq nunnukonoh kittinnaumatuonk.
119.52 Nummehquoantam nukkône k8sittam8ongash, woi Jehovah, káh n8weekontamwah nuhhog.
119.53 Nunnukshaonk nunohkukonk, newutche matchetowog ohquânumaog kittinnaumatuonguh.
119.54 Kukkuhk8waongash n8ket8hommaonganinneash ut weetuomut adt penuwohteaeomp.
119.55 Nummehquoantamup k8wesuonk woi Jehovah nukkonaeu, onk nunnanaweh kuttinnaumatuonk.
119.56 Yeu nuttinahtauun newutche nanaéhteap kukkuhk8tomuhteaongash.
119.57 Ken nutáhtauonk woi Jehovah, nussip, woh n[á]nauwehtauun kuttinn8waonk.
119.58 Nanómpassum k8womoausue nussuonk, nashpe mamusse nuttah, monanumeh neaunag kuttinn8waonk.
119.59 Nunnatwontamup nummayassh, onk nukquinnuppinnumup nusseetash en k8wauwaonganit.
119.60 Nukkinnuppeusséip matta nuppitchinwoeh nanauwéhteauunat kuttinu8waongash.
119.61 Wutchippiyeuongan8 matcheetowog nummukk8kinnukquog: qut matta n8wanánumoh kittinnaumatuonk.
119.62 Nôuttipukok nutomohkem woh kuttabuttantamoush, newutche sampwe k8sittam8wongash:
119.63 N8weéchaiyeumóog neg wame quoshhúkk8aneg: onk neg nanawéhtunkeg kukkuhk8tomuhteaongash.
119.64 Ohke woi Jehovah numwohteau kummonáneteaonk, kuhk8tomah kukkuhk8waongash.
119.65 K8nenéhheump kittinneum, woi Jehovah, neaunag kuttinn8waonk.
119.66 Kuhk8tomah wunnegen wussittumóouk, kah wahteauonk; newutche n8namptamup kuttinn8waongash.
119.67 Asquam onkapunnaan n8wauwónip: qut yeuyeu nanauwéhteóh kuttinn8waonk.
119.68 Ken k8netum, kah k8nésem: kuhk8tomah kukkuhk8waongash.
119.69 Pehtuanumóog nutayeuuhkone ayimunkquog pann8wáonk; qut nanauwéhteuh kukkuhk8tomuhteaongash nashpe mamusse nuttah.
119.70 Wuttahh8woash wunnogk8m8ash onatuh pumméit; qut nuttapeneau kittinnaumatuonk.
119.71 N8nehkongqun n8tamehpunaonk onk woh nunnetuhtóh kukkuhk8waongash.
119.72 Kutt8ne naumatuonk ne nutánue wunnenehikqun onk muttañonganogkodtash gold kah silver.
119.73 Kenutchegash nukkezhukqunapash kah nukkuhkenaihikqunapash: aninnumok wahwáhtam8onk, onk woh nunnehtântoh kuttinn8waongash.
119.74 Neg quoshhúkouanneg, pish weekontamwog nógquean: newutche nutannoóntam kuttinn8waonk.
119.75 N8wahteoh, woi Jehovah, k8sittam8wongash sampwâouash: kah kutonkapúnausup wutch wunnamuhkut k8womoausuonk.
119.76 K8weehquetumoush, kummonaneteáe womoausuonk taphúkquttei, neaunag kuttinn8waonk ut kuttinneum ut.
119.77 Kuttumungke kummonaneteaonk peyaaûnukquttei onk woh nukkete[à]m: newutche kittinnaumatuonk nuttapeneam.
119.78 Pittuánum8og akodchehettich, newutche tahn8che nummusquanatamwe matchenetunkquog, qut pish nunnatwontam kukkuhk8tomuhteaongash.
119.79 Yeug quashk8unneg, quinnuppéhettich en nuhhogkat kah neg wahtunkeg k8wauwaongash.
119.80 Mussaj nuttah ut kukkúhk8waonganit: onk woh mat nutákodchúh.
119.81 Nukketeahogkou sauwunnum wutch k8wadchanuwaonk, qut nutannowóntam kuttinnowaonk.
119.82 Nukesukquash sauwunnum8m8ash wutche kuttinn8waonk an8wáon, aquompak kuttápheh.
119.83 Newutche nutogqunneunkqus nônohtag wisk ut pukuttaut: onch matta n8wanantam8h kukkuhk8waongash.
119.84 Tohshinash ukkesukkodtumash kittinneum? aquompak kittinhéog k8sittum8onk neg woskhúkqueaneg?
119.85 Pittuanum8og wônteaog wutche neen: neg matta ánussegig neánussit kittinnaumatuonk.
119.86 Wame kuttinn8waongash paubuhtanumukquodtash: tohnunn8che woskehukquog, aninnumah.
119.87 Nahen nummohtupánukquog yeu ut ohkeit: qut matta nutahquoantam8h kukkuhk8tomuhteaongash.
119.88 Quahquáhqkheh neaunag kukkitteamonteanitteae k8womoausuonk, nemehkuh woh nanauwehteóh k8auwaongash ut kutt8nut.
119.89 Micheme, woi Jehovah, kuttinn8waonk menuhkoh[t]eau ut kesukqut.
119.90 Kussampwenéhuwaonk en pometuonganit onk yean pometuonganit: kummenuhkeéhteau ohke, onk ahteau.
119.91 Nash nagwutteohtaash yeu pajeh neaunag kukkuhk8waongash: newutche wame kittinneumog.
119.92 Matta tapeneauwôógus kittinnaumatuonk: woh nutauwakompáneaup ut nutonkquommom8nganit.
119.93 Matta pish n8wananatam8h kukkuhk8tomuhteaongash: newutche nish nashpe kukquogquahqhenneapash.
119.94 Neen kuttaihe, wadchaneh; newutche nunnatinneáham kukkuhk8tomuhteaongash.
119.95 Matchetowog nutaskwhonuk nunnushhukqunnaóut, qut nunnatwontam k8wauwaongash.
119.96 Nunnanaúmup adt wohkukquoshik wame pannuppe wanegik, qut kuttinn8waonk mishsheski.
119.97 Woi numm8cheke womontam kenaumatuonk, ne nummissantam8wonk quinni kesuk.
119.98 Kumm8cheke waantamwahhe onk neg nummatwomog nashpe kuttinn8waongash: newutche nagwutteae n8weetomukqunash.
119.99 Numm8cheke wohwohtám onk neg wame kohk8tomaiitcheg: newutche k8wauwaongash nummissantam8wongash.
119.100 Numm8cheke wohtam o[n]k neg kutchiog: newutche nanawehteoh kukkuhk8tomuhteaongash.
119.101 Nukqushkinnum nusseetash wutch nishnoh matchee may: onk woh nanawehteoh kuttinn8waonk.
119.102 Matta nutam8h wutch k8sittam8onganit: newutche ken kukkuhk8tomah.
119.103 Uttoh nukkukque weekonash kuttinn8waongash wutch nukqutchtamunat, m8cheke weekonash onk ne hony ut nutt8nit.
119.104 Nashpe [u]kuhk8tomuhteaongash n8wohwotam: newajeh nussekeneam nish noh pann8wae may.
119.105 Kuttin8waonk wequananteg ut nusseetut kah wequai ut nummayut.
119.106 Nutchadchekeyeuwap, kah pish nutusseh, onk woh nánawehteoh kussampwe wussittum8wongash.
119.107 Numm8cheke onkupunam quaquakqhe, woi Jehovah, neaunag kuttinn8waonk.
119.108 K8wequetumoush tapeneash nanouwe nummag8ongash wutch nutt8nut, woi Jehovah, kah kuhk8tomah k8sittum8waongash.
119.109 Nukketeahogkou nagwutteapu ut nunnutcheganit: onch matta n8wannanumoh kuttinnaumatuonk.
119.110 Matchetowog nupponamunkquog appehhanoh, qut matta nuppanneoh wutch kukkuhk8tamwehteaonganit.
119.111 Nunneemunnum k8wauwaongash onatuh nutaht8onganit micheme: newutche nih n8weekontamwahukqunash ut nuttahut.
119.112 Nutahchuwunnum nuttah ussen kukkuhk8waongash nagwutteaeu naut wohkukquoshik.
119.113 Nussekeneam tahn8che unnantamowongash, qut kuttinnaumatuonk n8womantam.
119.114 Ken nutassampamukquodt8m, kah nutogqunneg; nutannowontam kuttinnowaonk.
119.115 Amaeihtaek kenaau matcheseogish: newutche neen nunnanaweehteoh wuttinn8waongash num-Manitt8m.
119.116 Unnemenuhkinneh neaunag kuttinn8waonk, onk woh nuppomantam: kah ahque akodchitti wutch nuttannoosuonk.
119.117 Pabahtinéh onk woh n8wadchanit: onk nagwutteaeu n8t8anatam kukkuhk8waongash.
119.118 Kutahtashkuhkauomp nag wame panneaoncheg wutch kukkuhk8aonganit: newutche wutas8kekodteam8wonkan8 pann8wayeuonk.
119.119 Kutamaun wame matchetowog apitcheg ohkeit onatuh nishkeneunkquok: newaje womontam k8wauwáongash.
119.120 N8weyaus nunnukshau wutche kukqushin8wonk: kah n8wabissuwontam k8sittam8wongash.
119.121 Nummahche ussem 8sittum8wonk kah sampweusseuonk: ahque poneh nummatchenehitteanat.
119.122 Pabachteau kittinneum wutch wanegik: ahque pittuanum8og matchenehettich.
119.123 Nuskesukquash sauunum8m8 wutche k8wadchan8waonk: kah wutche kussampweusseongane kuttinn8waonk.
119.124 Enneh kittinneum neaunag kummonaneteaonk kah kuhk8tomah kukkuhk8waongash.
119.125 Nen kittinneum, aninnumah wawohtamowonk: onk woh n8wahteoh k8wauwaongash.
119.126 Utt8cheyeu8 woh neadt anakausean woi Jehovah: newutche tahn8cheteaog kittinnaumatuonk.
119.127 Newajeh ánue womantam kuttinn8waonganash onk ne gold, nux, anue onk ne wunnegik gold.
119.128 Newajeh n8t8wontam wame kuttiñ8waongash papaume wame teanteaquashinash sampwayeúut: kah nussekeneam nishnoh pannowáe may.
119.129 K8wauwaongash monchanatamoyeu8ash: newajeh nukketeahogkou nanawehteunk nashog.
119.130 Petutteau n8ug kuttinn8waongash wohsum8m8ash: aninnumauau wahtam8wonk as8tuoh.
119.131 N8wohshinnumup nutt8n kah nummehmehshanómup: newutche m8cheke nutahchewontamup kuttinn8waongash.
119.132 Monneah, kah monanumeh: neáhennehheadt yeug womontogig k8wesuonk.
119.133 OOnahtaash nutóntanehtuongash kuttinn8waonganit: kah ahqueh matcheseonk nanawunitch.
119.134 Pohquawhunch wutch 8woskhuaonganit wosketomp, nemehkuh pish nanawehtaun kukkuhk8tomuhteaongash.
119.135 Kuskesuk wohsumwahtoush ut kittinneumut: kah kuhk8tumah kukkuhk8waongash.
119.136 Sepúpog wuttitchuwan nukesukqut: newutche nag matta nanawehheauóoh kittinnaumatuonk.
119.137 Kussampweussem, woi Jehovah, kah sampwiyeuash k8sittum8ongash.
119.138 K8wauwaongash nish kussinneápash sampwáyeuash: kah ahche pabuhtanumukquodtash.
119.139 Nus[-]zealum nummóhtupanukqun: newutche nummatwomog wananatamwog kuttinn8waongash.
119.140 Kuttinn8wáonk m8cheke pohki: newajeh kittinneum womóntog.
119.141 Nen nuppeissis, kah nutjishanumit: onch matta n8wananittamm8 kukkuhk8tomúhteaongash.
119.142 Kussampweusseonk micheme sampweusseonganú8: kah kittinnaumatuonk wunnamu[h]kuteyeú8.
119.143 Wuttammepunáonk kah wohwohkukquiánum8onk nukkógkaanunuk: ônch kuttinn8waongash nuttapeneaumunash.
119.144 K8wauwaongane nussampweusseonk michemohteau, aninnumah wahwahtamóonk onk woh nuppomantam.
119.145 Nummau nashpe mamusse nuttah: n8tah woi Jehovah, nanawéhteuh kukkuhk8waongash.
119.146 Kummaúunnitteanup, wadchaneh, onk woh nunnanauwéhteuh k8wauwaongash.
119.147 Asquam mohtompann8g nummaup: nutann8wontam kuttinn8waonk.
119.148 Negonne nuskesukquash woshweem8 onk neg askuhwh[ó]sitcheg: onk woh nunnatwontam kuttinn8waonk.
119.149 N8tash n8wadtauatongqussuonk neaunag kukkitteamonteanitteáe womoausúonk, woi Jehovah, quhquahkqhe neaunag k8sittum8wonk.
119.150 Nag asuhkogig woskehuwaonk nuppas8sukkongquog: nò[ú]ssukomwog kittinnaumatuonk.
119.151 Kuppaswop woi Jehovah: kah wame kuttinn8waongash wunnamuhkuteyeu8ash.
119.152 Papaume k8wauwaongash, nôadt n8wahteaueap, kummenuhkehteanapash micheme.
119.153 Natwontash nutonkapunáonk, kah pohquahwusseh: newutche matta n8wananumeh kenaumatuonk.
119.154 Ken8tamwansheh, kah pohquahwusseh: quahquahqhe neaunag kuttinn8waonk.
119.155 Wadchanittúonk wunnôussukongqun matchetou: newutche nag matta natinneham8og kukkuhk8waongash.
119.156 Mogkiyeuash kukkitteamonteanitteáe monanitteaongash woi Jehovah: quahquahqhe neaunag k8sittum8ongash.
119.157 M8naog woskhukqueóneg, kah nummatwomog: qut matta nuppanneoh wutch k8wauwaonganit.
119.158 Nunnauomp matchetowog, kah neuanatamup: newutche matta nânaaihteauóog kuttinn8wáonk.
119.159 Natwontash uttoh nuttinne womontamun kukkuhk8tomúhteaongash: quahuahqhe woi Jehovah, neaunag kukkitteamonteanutteáe womoausuonk.
119.160 Kuttinn8waonk wunnamuhkuteyeú8 wutche weske kutchissik: kah nish noh pasuk kussampwe wussittum8ongash michemohtaash.
119.161 Santim8og tahn8che n8woskehukquog: qut nuttah quttianatam kuttinn8wáonk.
119.162 N8weekontam wutche kuttinn8waonk: neane howan maskog mishe woskehteauongash.
119.163 Nussekeneam kah nutjishontam pann8wayeuonk; qut n8womantam kittinnaumatuonk.
119.164 Nesausuk tahshit nompe pasukkesukqut kuttabuttantamoush: newutche kussampwe wussittum8ongash.
119.165 Mishu wunnohteáog neg womantogig kittinnaumatuonk: kah matta pish teaug wuttamhukk8og.
119.166 Jehovah nuttannoontamup k8wadchanuwáonk: kah nummahche ussenash kuttinn8waongash.
119.167 Nukketeahogkou nanawehteaóup k8wauwaongash: kah nash numm8cheke womontamunash.
119.168 Nanawehteauop kukkuhk8tomuhteaongash, kah k8wauwaongash: newutche wame kummayash anaquabeh ohtaash.
119.169 Nummauonk pas8tshaum8utch anaquabean, woi Jehovah: áninnumah wahwahtamóonk néaunag kuttinn8waonk.
119.170 N8weequetum8onk peyaum8utch anaquabean: pohquahwusseh neaúnag kuttinn8wáonk.
119.171 Nussissitt8nash yeum8ash tabuttantam8onk: mahche kuhk8tomauean kukkuhk8waongash.
119.172 Neenan pish yeum8 kuttinn8waonk: newutche wame kittinn8waongash sampwiyeuash.
119.173 Kenutcheg aninnumaiitch: newutche nuppepenam kukkuhk8tomuhteaongash.
119.174 Numm8cheke kodtantam k8wadchanuwaonk, woi Jehovah: kah kittinnaumatuonk nuttapeneau.
119.175 Nukketeahogkou pomantaj onk pish k8waeenomuk: kah k8sittum8wongash aninnumungqutteuh.
119.176 N8auwóin onatuh shepsut waónit, natinneah kittinneum: newutche matta n8wannantam8 kuttinn8waongash.
120.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomawonk}.
120.1 WAdtaméhpunaon nummauunitteaop Jehovah, onk n8tunkup.
120.2 Pohquohwus nukketeahogkou, woi Jehovah, wutch pann8wae mussisset8nut, kah wutch as8kekodteam8e meenannúut.
120.3 Toh pish kittinne aninnumont, asa toh pish kittinhit, woi ken pann8wáe meenan?
120.4 Masugkenuk keénu ukkôúhquodtash, weeche k8wáe mohkóssaash.
120.5 Missi nuttammepunáonk newutche nuttinneapeyon Meshek: onk nuttaiin Kedare weetuomehtu.
120.6 Nukketeahogkou wussépe weetómuh neh sekeneaumunutcheh wunnohteáonk
120.7 Nussim wunnohteagk: qut ket8hkaon kodtantamwog ayeu wuttuonk.
121.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomaonk}.
121.1 Nuttashinum nuskesukquash en wadchuuhkontu ne w8m8uk nuttannumonteáonk.
121.2 Nuttannumonteáonk 8m88 wutch Jehovah, noh ayikup kesuk kah ohke.
121.3 Kusseet matta unnantam8 ontattaun8it: noh nanahukquéan matta woh kogkouequâou.
121.4 Kusseh, noh nanaúnont Israeloh, matta kogkoúequau kah matta kouewu.
121.5 Jehovah kenanaunuk: Jehovah kutonkaóhtom wutch kuttinohkôunit.
121.6 Nuppâuz matta pish kussa[u]ukissuk8h kesukodáeu, asa nanepaôhshad nukkonáeu.
121.7 Jehovah kenanauunuk wutche wame matchitit, wadchanau kukketeahogkôunuh.
121.8 Jehovah nanaaihteau kuppomusháonk, kah kuppeyaonk: yeu wutche onk yean micheme.
122.0 {Hohtoesahteae ketoohomaonk} David.
122.1 NOOweekontamup ashettit, óntuh weekit Jehovah.
122.2 Nusseetunonash pish ohtóash anóme k8squontamut, woi Jerusalem.
122.3 Jersualem unnéhtaun onatuh otanit môsogquéhtag.
122.4 Wuttauadtuongang8 na aum8, wutchippann8ongash Jehovah, 8wauwaongan8wóut Israel: onk woh tabuttantamwog 8wesuonk Jehovah.
122.5 Newutche nâ ohteau wussittum8we appuonganash, appuonganash weekit David.
122.6 Peantamwansh wunnóhteáonk Jerusalem: neg womônukqueáneg wunniyeuog.
122.7 Wunnohteáonk ohtaj kittinnómeneutonganehtu, kah wunniyeuonk kittinnomekomukqut.
122.8 Wutche neematog kah weechiyeumogig: yeuyeu nussim wunnohteáonk appehtunkqush.
122.9 Newutche week Jehovah kum-Manitt8mun, nunnatinneham k8neetuonk.
123.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomaonk}.
123.1 Kuttuspunnumoush nuskesukquash: woi ken apean kesukquehtu.
123.2 Kusseh, wuttinneumunneunk nean kenompatam8hettit wussantimaum8uh wunnutcheg, kah wuttinneumun mittamwussis nean kenompatog wunnutcheg wussonksquomoh: netatup nuskesukqunonnash kenompamágut Jehovah num-Manitt8mun nô pajeh monanumugqunnanonut.
123.3 Monanuminnean, woi Jehovah, monanuminnean: newutche ahche numwaméechimimun nutohquánumugk8onganun.
123.4 Nukketeahogkôunnun ahche numwameechumeu ummamán8wantam8ongan8 saságeneogig: kah wutóhquánum8ongan8 pahchuanumwutcheg.
124.0 {Hohtoesohtae ukketoohomaonk} David.
124.1 Matta Jehovah nunn8gis wutche kuhhogkanonit, yeuyeu Israel woh n8wau.
124.2 Matta Jehovah nunn8gis wutche kuhhogkanonit, wosketompaog waabehtunkqueog.
124.3 Neit woh nag kummisseusquónukqunnonuppanneg, ummusquantam8ongan8 ayeuuhkonittue nashqunag wutche kenaan.
124.4 Neit woh nippeash kenuhkekongqunnan, kussehtanup nukketeahogkôunnuñonoh nukkuhkau[ó]p.
124.5 Neit pittuanumwe nuppeash nukkuhkauop nukketeahogkounoh.
124.6 Wunnanumunaj Jehovah matta mag8unat kuhhogkanonuh meetsuongan8 ut weepittuwout.
124.7 Nukketeahogkounnun pohquohham onatuh psukses wutch ukquomphonganit noh adchont: ohpe pokshau, onk nuppohquohhamumun.
124.8 Kutanninumonteaonganun ohteau 8wesuonganit Jehovah, noh ayigkup kesuk kah ohke.
125.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomaonk}.
125.1 Neg Pabahtanumoncheg Jehovah[,] ogqunneunkqussuog wadchuut Sion, ne matta woh ontuhtano, micheme ohteau.
125.2 Onatuh wadchuash nish quanupohtagish Jerusalem, neane Jehovah quinnuppekauont ummissinninneumoh: yeu wutche, onk yean micheme.
125.3 Newutche uppogkomunkan8 matcheetowog matta pish sepohtano wutoht8ongan8wout sampwesecheg: ishkont sampweseaenuog summagunnumwog wunnutchegan8woash en matcheseonganit.
125.4 Wunne énne woi Jehovah, neg waneetukeg: kah nag sampwesitcheg ut wuttahh8wout.
125.5 Qut neg áoncheg 8wôóngke may8wout Jehovah pish nah 8weechuwunuh matcheseaenutu: qut wunnahteáonk pish ohteau Israelut.
126.0 {Hohtôesohteae ketoohomaonk}.
126.1 JEhovah, quashkunont ummissinomuh Sion; nutohgqunneunkqussimunnonup neg anukquonkeg.
126.2 Neit nutt8nonut numwohta ahanuonk, kah neenanuunnonut ket8homaonk: neit nag n8waog k8wutche penuwohteaog, Jehovah ummishanakausuwehtaoh nahog.
126.3 Jehovah kummishanakausuwehtunkqun: newaj weekontamog.
126.4 Qushkinnean wutch nummissinnaneanonut woi Jehovah onatuh kussitchuwan wutche sowunnaeu.
126.5 Neg ahketeacheg wussippeg8woash, pish kepenumwog weekontamowonk.
126.6 Nnoh sohhog kah mauug nashpeit mahshoadtik wuskannem, wunnamuhkut pish peyau weeche weekontamowonk paudtunk 8sheavsumash.
127.0 {Hotoesohteae ketoohomaonk wutche Solomon}
127.1 IEhovah matta ayim8g weetu, tahn8che an[a]kausuog neg ayikeg: Jehovah mat nanawehtea8g otan askuhwheteáenin tahn8che askuhwhosu.
127.2 Tahn8cheyeu8 kutomohkenau nompoaeu, kah cheke kukkoueneau, meechinat, neuanatam8we petukqunnunk: ne wuttinne unninnumauun neh kaenutcheh womononcheh.
127.3 Kusseh mukkiesog wutahtoonk Jehovah kah wutóontomukae meechumuonk ne wut onkquatauuonk.
127.4 Onatuh kôuhquodtash wunnutcheganit manuhkesit wosketomp, neane keneechanog woskenuean.
127.5 OOnaiyeu woskeetomp not uppetanwonit nomwapenit, matta pish akodchuog, qut pish ken8naog mátwaoh ut squont[ā]ut.
128.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomaonk}
128.1 Nish noh quoshont Jehovah 8nanumau: noh aont ummayut.
128.2 Newutche pish kummeech kenutchegane anakausuonk: k8wuni, kah pish k8nenehukqun.
128.3 Kummittumwus pish ogqunneungqussu mahshemeechumik we[n]omesippog ut kishke keekit: keneechanog pish ogqunneungqussuog Olive puntukquemesit, quinnuppe ahuttashpean.
128.4 Kusseh, yeu pish unne wunnanumon noh quoshont Jehovah.
128.5 Jehovah pish k8nanumuk wutch Sion: onk pish kenaum 8netuonk Jerusalem n[e]sahkepomantaman.
128.6 Nux pish kenaau keneechanog onk na wunneechan8, kah 8nohteaongan8 Israel
129.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomaonk}.
129.1 MOOcheke nompu nummatchenehukquog wutch n8skenuunneat, Israel woh yeuyeu n8wau.
129.2 M8cheke nompu nummatchenehukquog wutch n8skenuunneat: onch matta nussohkunk8og.
129.3 Anaskhomwaenuog anaskhamwog ut nuppi[s]hquanit: quohquonitchagquamwog.
129.4 Jehovah sampweussu: tummetham uppemunneohton8óash matcheetowog.
129.5 Wame akodjhetticheh[,] kah qushkehettich, sekeneog [g] Sion.
129.6 Ogqunneungqussehettich moskehtuuk woskeche komukqut: ne ahpohtag asq waummékininnokup.
129.7 Nish nashpe tisashquaenin matta nomwohto8g wunnutcheg: asuh noh woshpununk sheavesash upp8chinnauwoonnut.
129.8 Asuh matta neg noh kishke paumushacheg unn8wau8og, 8naneteaonk Jehovah apehtunk8k: k8nanum[u]numun ut 8wesuonganit Jehovah.
130.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomank}.
130.1 Wutche m8naiyeut kummauunnitteanup woi Jehovah.
130.2 Jehovah, n8tash n8wadtauatongqussuonk: kehtaúogsh ahchusittamohettich n8wadtauatongqussue weequeum8onk.
130.3 Tohneit Jehovah kukkinneaséan matcheseongash, woi Jehovah howa woh neepauwit?
130.4 Qut kutahquoantausúonk kutahtaum: onk woh kukqushit.

130.6 Nukketeahogkou m8chekeu páhheau Jehovah, onk nag askuhwhósicheg nompoáeu, onk nag askuwhósitcheg nompoáeu.
130.7 Israel annoónonch Jehovah, newutche Jehovah neit ohteau monaneteaonk, kh unnohmónat umman8h8waonk.

131.0 {Hohtoesohteae ukketoohomaonk} David.

132.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomáonk}.
132.1 IEhovah mehquantash David wame wuttuhquanum8onganit.

132.3 Wunnamuhkut matta nupetutteoh tabernakle neekit, kah matta nusseepsinn8 nutappinneat.
132.4 Matta nuskesukquash koiémun8ash, naneadtaskesukquash matta supweémun8ash.

132.6 Kusseh, nunn8amûnan ut Ephrata, nummiskomúnan touohkomukqu ohkeit.

132.9 Kussephausueneumg hogquehettich nashpe wunnomausseonk kah k8neetupanatam8mog muskouanatamwe mishontowáhettich.
132.10 Newutche k8tinninneum David, ahque quinuppemau wuskesuk noh saséquinadt.

132.12 Keneechánog nanauehteaúhettit n8n8waonk, kah n8wauwáoash, nish woh kohk8tomauogish nag: wunneechân8oh pish wonk nanuk wutáppinneau kutappuonganit micheme.
132.13 Newutche hovah pepenam Sion: wutahchewontamun nohwuttin wutohkinnet.
132.14 Yeu nutanwôhsin8onk micheme: yeu n8tohkin, newute nukkodtantamun.
132.15 Numm8chke wunnantamau ummeechumum: nuttápeteau ummatcheteumoh nashpe petukqunnunk.
132.16 Wussephausuéneumoh wonk nutogquannónineuh wadchânittuonk: kah 8neetupanatam8moh pish weekntamóe mishont8wáoh.
132.17 Na nuttit ayeúon wutaskonoh David wussonkhékineat: nukkúhquttumaomp wequananteg wutche noh saséqunog.
132.18 Ummatwomoh pish nutogquodtumaónuh akodchuonk: qut nagum ut wuhhogkat wutchétuhquab pish wunnenégen.
133.0 {Hohtoesohteae ukketoohomaonk} David.
133.1 Kusseh, uttôh en wunnegen, kah uttôh en muskauantamenunkquodt, 8weematittuog 8weechaiyeútinneaout kah uppasuk8inneaóut.

134.0 {Hohtoesohteae ketoohomaonk}.
134.1 Kusseh, wunnaum8k Jehovah, wame kenaau wuttinnumoh Jehovah, nukkonaeu nepaéógish weeki Jehovah.
134.2 Spunnum8k kenutchegan8ash ut wunneetpanatam8onganit, kah wunnanum8k Jehovah.
134.3 Noh Jehovah kesteunk kesuk kah ohke, wunnanumukqush wutche Sion.
135.1 Waeenomok Jehovah, waeenodtom8k 8wesuonk Jehovah, waeenomonk, woi kenaau wuttinneumoh Jehovah.
135.2 Kenaau neepaué[a]gish weekit Jehovah, wutchippanutunkanit weekit kum-Manitt8mun.
135.3 Waeenomok Jehovah, newutche Jehovah wunneetou: waeenodtam8k tabuttantam8ongash ut 8wesuonganit, newutche tapeneunkquot.
135.4 Newutche Jehovah uppepénau Jakoboh en wuhhogkat, kah Israeloh wutche nehenwonche 8nenompak8unoh.
135.5 Newutche n8wàhteauun Jehovah noh missugken, kah kum-Manitt8mun wame aneuhkauau manitt8h.
135.6 Tôh án wunnántog Jehovah ne wutussen, ut kesukqut kah ut ohkit: kehtahhannehtu kah wame mam8noagish.
135.7 Oúwan waapunumwahtau wutch papogkodche ohkeit, ayim kutshaúmunnu8ut wutch sókanonut: pás8au mehshetahshinneoh wutch nô adt umm8chekodchanont.
135.8 Noh tôgkomup mohtomméginitcheh ut Egypt, wosketompoh kah puppinashimwoh.
135.9 An8nau kuhkinneasuongash, kah monchanatam8wongash ut nôeu ken woi Egypt, ut Pharaohut, kah wame wuttinninnúmut.
135.10 Noh tôgkodtogkup môgagish wutohtimóneash, kah paguanau matikkénutcheh ketass8timwoh.
135.11 Sihon ketass8t ut Amoritsut: kah Og ketass8t ut Bashan, kah wame as8tam8wongash ut Canaan.
135.12 Kah mag8 nag wutohkéim8 wutohkéinneat, 8tohkéinnéaóut Israel ummissinninnumoh.
135.13 K8wesuonk woi Jehovah michemohteau, kah kummehquanumitteáonk papannuppu wame pometuonganit.
135.14 Newutche Jehovah wussumau ummissinninneumoh, kah aiuskoianatam papaume wuttinneumut.
135.15 Wuttinunneuhkontonkan8oh penuohteá[o]g, nag silver kah gold, wutanakausuongan8 wosketompaog wunnutchegan88ash.
135.16 Wutt8nnúog, qut matta keket8hkau8og: wuskesuk8og, qut matta naum8og.
135.17 Wahtauog8og, qut matta n8tam8og: asa matta nashauóog wutt8n8wóut.
135.18 Nag kesheoncheg wutogqunneunkqussinneáuh, kah neyáne wame neg pabahtanumoncheg.
135.19 Wunnánum8k Jehovah, woi week Israel, wunnanum8k Jehovah, woi week Aaron:
135.20 Wunnanum8k Jehovah, woi week Levi, kenaau quoshógish Jehovah wunnanum8k Jehovah.
135.21 Wunnanumunach Jehovah wutch Sion, noh wodohkit Jerusalem: waeenomok Jehovah.
136.1 TAbuttantam8k Jehovah, newutche noh wunneetou, newutche ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
136.2 Tabuttantam8k um-Manitt8m8oh manitt8og, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.3 Tabuttantam8k wunnánaunnuaéneumoh nanaánuaénúog, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.4 N noh nehtaue ásit misheu monchanatam8wongash, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.5 N$noh nashpu waantam8onk ayim kesukquash, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemóhteau.
136.6 N$noh kodtunuk ohke wutch nippekontu, newutche ummonaneteâonk michemohteau.
136.7 N$noh ayikup môgagish wequaiyeuash, newutche úmmonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.8 Nepâuz onk woh nanaánum kesukod, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.9 Nahnepaushad kah anogqsog onk woh nanawunumog nukon: newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.10 Nnoh nahshóp mohtommégitteomoh Egypt, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.11 Kah soh8wunnau Israeloh nahwutch kenugku, newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.

136.13 N$noh pohshinugkup musque kehtoh: newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.
136.14 Kah Israeloh pannupwushaheau pahshaúeu: newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.

136.18 Kah nushau tahs8timwoh wáeenómutcheh: newutche ummonaneteáonk michemohteau.

136.20 Kah Og ketass8t ut Bashan: newutche ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.

136.26 Woi tabuttantam8k Jehovah kesukqut apit, newutche ummonaneteaonk michemohteau.
137.1 KIske sepuwehtu ut Bábilon, na nutapinnean, nux nummaumun, mehquontamog Sion.

138.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
138.1 KOOwaweenomsh nashpe wame nuttahut: anaquabhettit Manittóog kuttinn8namoushk 8waweenomitteaonk.
138.2 K8wawu[s]sumsh unogqueu k8neetupanatamwe Templeut, kah nuttabuttantam k8wesuonk, newutche k8womoausue womoausuonk, kah k8nomwaonk: newutche kummishteop kuttinn8waonk anue onk wame k8wesuonk.
138.3 Ne kesukok mauon, kenamp8hamaiip; kummenuhkehip nashpe menuhkesuonk ut nukketeahogkounit.
138.4 Wame ketass8tamog yeu muttaohkit pish k8woweenomukquog, woi Jehovah, nag n8tamwehettit kuttinn8waongash wutch kutt8nut.

139.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt ukketoohomaonk} David.
139.1 WOi Jehovah, kenátinneakôsip kah k8wáheh.
139.2 K8wahteuh nummatappuonk, kah nutomohkeonk, k8wahteuh nuttenantamoonk en nô adtit.
139.3 Kukquinnuppuhkom nummay, kah nussepsinn8onk: kah k8wahteuh wame nummayash.
139.4 Newutche matta kutt8onk ohtáno neenanut qut kusseh, woi Jehovah, pannuppu k8wahteauunash.
139.5 Kuppon kuhhog anaquabeh kah nuppisquanit, kah kenutcheg kupponamah.
139.6 Yeu wahteauonk wussaume monchanatam8onganú8 wutche neen, qunnuhquodt, matta woh nummissunnum8un.
139.7 Toh nogqueu woh nutton wutch kenashauanitt8mut? asuh toh nogqueu woh nutussishon wutch anaquabean?
139.8 Aùon kesukqut na kuttappin, ayimon nutappin ut chepiohkomukqut, kusseh, na kutappin.
139.9 Neemunog umméqunoh nompoáeu, kah appeon aongkouwe ketahhannit,
139.10 Na kenutcheg nuttinsagkompagunukqun kah kuttinnohkou pish nukkogkôunuk.
139.11 N8waon, wunnamuhkut pohkenái pish nunnohkukkonk: nukon pish wequái quinuppe neen.
139.12 Nux, pohkéni matta kutassómpattamm8un qut nukon wohsum8m8 onatuh kesukok: pohkenái kah wequái naneeswe netatupeaúnak wutche ken.
139.13 Newutche kuppetukauomp nutt8unnussog: kupputtogk8hip ut nôkas wutoontomukqut.
139.14 K8waweenomsh newutche wabesúe kah monchanatamwe nukkezhitteup: kutanakausuongash monchanatamweyeu8ash, onk yeu nukketeahogkou menuhke wahteoun.
139.15 Nuhhog matta mô puttogwhosu wutche ken, keme kezhimuk: kah wanehimuk ut agwe ohket.
139.16 Kuskesukquash naumwog nuhhog asquam pa[n]nuppe n8nekezhett[e]aunk, kah kup[-]b8kumut wame nuppompuhcháiyeumash tanussukkuhwhôsu, nish nano kake[na]áihteomukish mata pasuk ohtan8g.
139.17 Uttôh mishôadtu kittenántam8ongash en nuhhogkat, woi num-Manitt8m? toh ain muttâânit?
139.18 Nag ogkémog, nano monatash onk ne nágunt: t8kshon ash k8weétomsh.
139.19 Wunnamuhkut pish kuppaguan matcheetowog, woi num-Manitt8m, newutche amaéhtaegk kenaau nushshehteaenúog.
139.20 Newutche kummatchenukquog ayeuuhkône ken kah kummatwomog tahn8che ken8tamwog.
139.21 Sunnummatta nutjishanum8og, woi Jehovah, jishanumugquéaneg? kah sunnummatta neuánum8og yeug ayeuuhkonittue waábetunkquêaneg?
139.22 Nussekeneauóog nag nashpe pannuppe sekeneaittúonk: nag nutogquonumóog nummatwomut.
139.23 Natinnekôseh, woi num-Manitt8m, kah wahteaush nuttah: qutchéheh, kah wahteaush nuttenanatam8ongash.
139.24 Kah naish uttiyeu matchemay ut nuhhogkat, kah sagkompaguneh en mayut máchemohtag.
140.0 {Nohtompuhpequodt, Ukketoohomaonk} David.
140.1 Pohquahwusseh, woi Jehovah, wutch matcheseanúut: wadchaneh wutch musquantamwe wosketompaut.
140.2 Neg mohmissóntogig woskehuwaonk wuttahh8wóut: nagwutteáeu momoéog wutch ayeuwuttúonk.
140.3 Ayimwog weenannu8ash kéniyeuash onatuh ask8kut: úhquoshket sesequáog agwu wussisset8n8wóut. Selah.
140.4 Wadchaneh, woi Jehovah, wutch wunnutcheganit matcheetou, nanaáihheh wutch musquantamwe woskeetompaut neg ahchewontogig kepuhkon nutauonganash.
140.5 Pitchuanumwog adtahsháog wutappehhann8oh wutche neen, kah pémeneohtanémesash: sepagenáog wutashabp8uh kishke m[a]yut; nupponamunkquog appehanah. Selah.
140.6 Nuttin Jehovah, ken num-Manitt8m, n8tash n8wadtauatonkqussue weequetum8onk woi Jehovah.
140.7 Woi Jehovah Manit, n8wadchanitteae menuhkesuonk: kupputtagguhhamup nuppuhkuk ne kesukok ayeuwuttimuk.
140.8 Ahque wéht8wom, woi Jehovah, matchetowog ne kodtantamóhettit: ahque kutchittánumau ummatcheetupanatamwe ompuwissuonk, ishkont mishehheáog wuhhogkaoh. Selah.
140.9 Yeug weenuhkoiitcheg, 8woskehuwaonk ut wussisset8nit nuhkeem8utch ut nehenwonche uppuhkukk8wóont.
140.10 Nashqunáe mokossaash nuhkuhkongk8hettich, nohkónach n8taut, en m8nâeu passahthonganit, onk woh mo waápéog wonk.
140.11 Ahque menehkhénach mamatchen8waenin ut ohkeit: woskehuwáonk pish ayeuau woskehuaenuh ukképôhkônat.
140.12 N8wahteóh Jehovah ken8tamwonshheuh kuttummungeh wuttammepunnaeninneuh: kah wussampweteaum8onk matchekuoh.
140.13 Wunnamuhkut sampweusseaenin pish tabuttantam k8wesuonk: sampwesit pish ayeu anaquabean.
141.0 {Ukketooh[o]maonk} David.
141.1 JEhovah, kummauunnitteaush, kenuppe peyaauseh, kukkeitash n8wadtauatongqussuonk mauunnitteáuunán.
141.2 Nuppeaantam8onk sampwespeem8utch ut anaquabean, onátuh incenseut kah nuttishpunnumunnat nunnutcheganash onatuh wunnonkwaeu sephausuonk.

142.0 {Um-Maschil} David: {Peantamowonk apit puppuhkotteaouut.}
142.1 Nummauunnitteau Jehovah nashpe n8wadtauatonkqussúonk: nashpe n8wadtauatonkqussuonk nutayimup n8weequetum8onk en Jehovahut.

142.3 Nunnashauonk quodtaogkomésit ut nuhhogkat, neit k8wahteoh nummay: mayik ne âôump, kemu nupponamunkquog appehanah.
142.4 Nuttinnuhquaip nuttinohkôunit kah nuppabahsamputtamunah, qut mâtta howan n8wahuk8, spuhh8waonk nunnukkonnukqun: wanne howan tohhentupanumoou nukketeahogkounoh.

142.6 Kukkeihtash nummauonk, newutche nuttiuhquonkqhit: pohquawusseh wutch n8woskhuwaeneumut, newutche nag nutanuwunuhkesumukquog.
142.7 Sohh8wush nukketeahogkou wutch kuppishagkinittuonganit onk woh n8woweenodtum k8wesuónk: sampweusseaenuog pish quinnupuhkongquog: newutche pish kumummisku wunneneheh.
143.0 {Ukketoohomaonk} David.
143.1 NOOtash nuppeantamowonk woi Jehovah kuhkeitash n8weehquetum8wonganash: ut kussampwanumukqussinneat namp8hamah, kah ut k8nomwausseaonganit.
