143.3 Newutche matwau woskeheau nukkéteahogkounoh, unnehtham nuppomantamoonk ohkekontu: n8tohkehhik pohkenahtu onatuh yeug sepe nuppukeg.
143.4 Newajeh nunnashauonk wuttaoukomesit ut nuhhogkat: nuttáh nuttinnomiyeumut nonsiyeum8.
143.5 Nummehquontam n8adt kesukkodtash, nunnatwontam wame kutanákausuongash, nummissantam kenutchegane anakausuongásh
143.6 Kussumogkunumoush nunnutcheganash: nukketeahogkou wutche ken, onatuh kunkohteatae ohke. Selah.
143.7 N8tah teanuk woi Jehovah, nunnashauonk sa[u]wunnum: ahque ahtohtah kuskesuk ishkont nutógqunneunkqus nag aoncheg possahtheganit.
143.8 N8tamwaheh womoausue k8womoausuonk nompoaeu, newutche kuppabahtanumoush wahteauwaheh may toh wóh ayôi, newutche kutahshinnumaush nukketeahogkou.
143.9 Pohquawusseh woi J[é]hovah wutch nummatwomog: kuppogsinn8wonsh noh kittin ahtahshinneat.
143.10 Kuhk8tomah ussen kuttinanatam8onk, newutche ken num-Manitt8m kenashauanitt8m wunnetu, sagkompaguneh en wutohtuwout sampwéusseog.
143.11 Quaquahqheh woi Jehovah, newutche k8wesuonk: newutche kussampweusseonk sohhouwus nukketeahogkou wutch wuttammepunnonat.
143.12 Kah wutch kummonaneteaonganit tumméhtah nummatwomog, kah pagwas wame nnag onkapunnanoncheg nukketeahogkonuh: newutche nen kittinneum.
144.1 Wunanumunach Jehovah nummenuhkesuonk, noh kuhk8tomwontog nunnutchegash ayeukonat, kah nuppahchanitcheash wutayeuuhkon[?]ôut.
144.2 N8neét8onk kah n8wonkonous, nukqunnunkqukkommuk kah nuppohquohwussuaenin, nutogqunneg, kah nnoh pàbuhtanumog: noh sohkauont nummissinninneumoh agwu neen.
144.3 Lord howan wosketomp nnoh ken waheadt? asa wunnaumonuh wosketomp onk woh kututtanantamau?
144.4 Wosketomp ogqueneunkqussu tahn8cheye[n]8winneat: ukkesukodtumash ogqueneunkquodtash onkaohtaut, ne pamushaum8uk.
144.5 Puskepukash kuskesukquash woi Jehovah, kah n8kish: mussinush wadchuash, kah nash pish pukittau8ash.
144.6 Sohwôhtaush ukkutshaumun kah nag séeah: pepumish kukkô[u]hquodtash kah nag pagwas.
144.7 Ann8s kenutcheg wutch waabe, sohh8wuneh, & pohquohwusseh wutche mishe nippekontu: wutch wunnutchegan8wout pénowe mukkiog.
144.8 N[o]h wutt8n tahn8che keket8kóm8ug, kah wuttinnohkoun8wóut, pann8wayeue wuttinnohkou.
144.9 Kuttinn8hómoush wuske ket8homwaonk woi Jehovah: ut psaltarehut, & puhpeg paukquompósik kuttinn8homoush waeenodtuongash.
144.10 Noh aninnumauau ketahs8timoh wadchanittúonk, noh pohquohwhunau Davidoh wuttinneumoh wutch woskehettue togkodteganit.
144.11 Sohwhuneh, kah pohquohwusseh wutch wunnutcheóont penowe mukkiog, noh wutt8n tahn8che an8wom8uk: kah wuttinnohkonn8woont pann8wae wuttinohkou.
144.12 Naumonanonog woh ogqunneunkqussuog wuskontugk8mesit sonkqhettit ut wuskenúunneat: nuttaununnonog woh ogqueneunkqussuog qussuk náshik wunneetatuppussumun onatuh wunne qussukquanekommuk.
144.13 Onk woh nutogqunakomukqunonash numwameechummuash, nishnoh teag ne woh wuttinnumun: nuttisshepsumunnouog woh 8chekeneau muttannonganogkussuog nashomáogqunnonut.
144.14 Nutoxinumunnonog woh menuhkanakausuog, mattá woh howan uppetuhkontam8un, asa mat sohhamm8: matta woh mauaonganinno nunnaushomaogqunnonut.
144.15 Wunnaiyeuog missinninnuog neg ne adtuhkég: wunnaiyeuog missinninnuog noh wamanitt8mut Jehovah.
145.0 {Waeenomuae ukketooohomaonk} David.
145.1 Kummishesh num-Manitt8m, woi ketass8t: kah n8nantam k8wesuonk micheme kah micheme.
145.2 Asekesukokish k8nánumoush: kah n8wóweenodtum k8wesuonk, micheme kah micheme.
145.3 Jehovah missugken, kah noh woh mahshe waeenomit: kah ummissugken8wonk, mat woh howan uppogkodadttinnekóntam8un.
145.4 Pasuk pometuonk pish waeenodtum kutanakausuongash onk yean onkatoganit; kah pish wahteauwahuwau kummishanakausuongash.
145.5 N8wéogquttum wussohsumówe quttiánumáonk kummissugkenuonk, kah kummonchanatamwanakausuongash.
145.6 Kah pish keket8hkontamwog ummenuhkesuonk kutunkquanuhkausuongash: kah pish n8wahteauwahuwam kummissugkenuwonk.
145.7 Nag pish m8cheke weogquttimwog mehquoantam8onk kummishe wunneetowonk, & pish ket8homaog k8nomwausséonk
145.8 Jehovah monaneteau, kah numwohteau ukkitteamonteaneteaonk, cheke musquantam, kah mishe ummonaneteaonk.
145.9 Jehovah 8neneheuh wame; kah ukkitteamonteanitteáe monaneteaongash nuhkuhkomwog wame wutanakausuongash.
145.10 Wame kutanakausuonganash pish k8woweenomuk, woi Jehovah: kah k8neetupanatam8mog pish k8nanumukquog.
145.11 Nag pish weogquttumwog sohsumóe kukkeass8timóonk kah pish keket8hkaog kummenuhkesuonk.
145.12 Onk woh wahteauwáheaog wosketompaog wunnaumonaoh, ummishanakausuongash, kah wussohsumóe missugkenue ukkehtass8tam8onk.
145.13 Kukketass8timóonk micheme ohtag ketass8timóonk: kah kenánaánumôonk pannuppe wame pometuonganash.
145.14 Jehovah pabahtinau wame panushonutcheh: kah tahshinau wame yeuh naausukompaunutcheh.
145.15 Wuskesukquash wame kukkenompomukqunash, kah nag kutassamoog nish noh utt8che.
145.16 K8woshinum kenutcheg, & kuttapehteóh ukkodtantam8onk nishnoh pamóntog.
145.17 Jehovah sampweussu ut wame ummayut, kah wunneetupanatam wame wutanakausuonganit.
145.18 Jehovah uppas8sukauoh wame neh weehquttumungqutcheh: wame weequttumungqutcheh wunnamuhkut.
145.19 Noh tapeteaoh ukkodtantamoonk neh quashikqutcheh: kah wonk wunn8tamauoh ummauongan8, kah pish 8wadchanuh.
145.20 Jehovah 8wadchanuh wame neh womonukqutcheh: qut wame matchetowoh uppaguanuh.
145.21 Nutt8n pish yeum8 waeenomaonk Jehovah: kah wame weyaus wunnanatamohettich wunneetupanatamwe 8wesuonk micheme kah micheme.
146.1 Waeenomok Jehovah waeenom Jehovah, woi nukketeahogkou.
146.2 As pamontam n8woweenom Jehovah: nukket8homau Num-Manitt8m tabuttantam8wongash, as yeu apeh.
146.3 Ahque pabahtanum8k santimoog, wunnaumonuh wosketomp, noh matta aninnohsuonk ohtoog.
146.4 Wunnashauonk amaemouk, quinnuppu en nuppuppissiyeumut: ne kesukok wuttenantam8ongash monteagwuninnoash.
146.5 Wunnaiyeu n noh wodtanninnohsumit um-Manitt8moh Jakob, noh annoonont Jehovah um-Manitt8moh.
146.6 Noh aigkup kesuk kah ohke, kehtoh kah wame neg noh apitcheg: noh wadchanuk wunnomwayeuonk micheme.
146.7 Noh asit 8sittum8onk wutussehtaon waskhitcheh noh assamont kodtupwunutcheh: Jehovah ompinneau kobshagkinutcheh.
146.8 Jehovah wôhshinum wuskesukquash pogkenumunutche: Jehovah tohshinau neh nâuhsukompaunutcheh: Jehovah womonuh samweusseaenuh.
146.9 Jehovah wadchanau penuwohteuh: aninnumauau mat wod8sh8nigeh, kah sekousquoh: qut ummay matcheetou 8numuhkinumun.
146.10 Jehovah pish nanauunnuau micheme, kum-Manitt8m woi Sion ut wame pometuonganit: waeenom8k Jehovah.
147.1 Waeenom8k Jehovah: newutche wunnegen ket8homauonat tabut tantam8ongash kum-Manitt8mun: newutche weekontamweyeu8, kah waeenomaonk tapeneunkquot.
147.2 Jehovah weekitteau Jerusalem: mukkinnau môaeu yeug sohwohteamukig wutch Israelaut.
147.3 Neetskeheau sohqutteahonutcheh: kah tohkupunau 8woskesewongan8ash.
147.4 Ogkemau neadtahsohettit anogqsog: nah wame 8weseonganuhkauouh.
147.5 Missugken kum-Manitt8mun, kah mishe menuhkesu: 8wohwohtam8wonk matta wo[h]kukkoano.
147.6 Jehováh tahshinau manunnissuoh: unnohteau matchetuoh ohkekontu.
147.7 Ket8homok Jehovah nashpe tabuttántamóonk: ket8homok tabuttantam8ongash ut harput en kum-Manitt8munnonut.
147.8 Noh pâdtahgúhh8k kesukquash nashpe matokqs, noh quoshauwehtog sokanon wutche yeu ohke: noh ayig moskehtuash negkinut ut wadchuut.
147.9 Assamau puppinnashimwussoh, kah konkontuwémesoh mauunit.
147.10 Matta weekontam8 ummenuhkesuonk horses: matta weekontam8 wuhkontash wosketomp.
147.11 Jehovah weeteánumau neh quoshhukqutcheh, neh anoantamunutcheh ummonaneteáonk.
147.12 Waeenom8k Jehovah, woi Jersualem: tabuttantamau kum-Manitt8m, woi Zion.
147.13 Newutche menehketeau neepattúhquonk kussquontamut: wunnanumau keneechanoh ut kuhhogkat.
147.14 Wunnóhteahuau ut wohkóeu: kah kenumwameechumuhkónuk nish wanegukish wheatash.
147.15 Ann8nau wuttinn8waonguh ut ohkekontu: wuttinn8waonk kenupshau.
147.16 Magou k8nah onatuh w8ll: seáhwhau t8puoh onatuh pukquéit.
147.17 Sohwhohteau ukkuppádtinumoh onatuh kodchuhke petukqunneganit: howan woh neepauut wussónquayeumut?
147.18 An8nau wuttinn8waonguh, kah nah wussâuppaswoh: mshéhtashinehteau, wonk tomógkon.
147.19 Kuhk8tomauau Jakoboh wuttinn8waonk, ukkuhk8waongash, kah 8wauwaongash Israeloh.
147.20 Matta wuttinteauun onkatuk wutohtimóin: kah 8sittum8wongash matta nah 8wáhheóuh; waeeom8k Jehovah.
148.1 WAeenom8k Jehovah: waeenom8k Jehovah wutch kesukqut: waeenom8k ut quanunkquodtehtu.
148.2 Waeenom8k kenaau wame wut-angelsumoh: waeenom8k wame wutáyeuweéhteomoh.
148.3 Waeenom8k kenaau nepâuz kah nepâuzshad: waenom8k kenaau wohsumóeanogqsog
148.4 Waeenom8k kenaau kesukquash kesuk, kah kenaau nippéog ongkouwe kesukquehtu.
148.5 Waeenodtumohettich 8wesuonk Jehovah: newutche noh n8wop onk nag kezheopanneg.
148.6 Onk noh menuhkeheuh nah micheme kah micheme: ayimup ukkúhk8waonk, ne matta pish paumshaumún8g.
148.7 Waeenom8k Jehovah wutche ohket, kenaau dragonsog, kah wame m8nóagish.
148.8 N8tau, & musségon, k8n, kah pukkuttaemes, mehshetahshin, usseog uttoh an8wop.
148.9 Wadchuash kah wame wadchuemesash máhshemechume mahtugquash, kah wame chikupog.
148.10 Puppinashimwog, & wame neetassuog, neg pâpâm8tacheg, & páhpumunont psukses
148.11 Kehtahs8timwog ut ohkeit, kah wame missinninnuog: santimóog kah wame wussittumwaenuog ut ohkeit.
148.12 Naneeswe nunkompaog kah nunksquaog, kutchiog kah mukkiog.
148.13 Waeenodtumohettich 8wesuonk Jehovah: newutche ne wesuonk webe muttáe wunnegen: wussohsumóonk aneukom8 ohkeit kah kesukqut.
148.14 Noh wonk tashinau wutáskon8oh ummissinninnuomoh, 8waweenomuwaongan8 wame 8neetupanatam8moh, wunnaumonuh Israel, missinninnúogpas8sukauóuh: waeenom8k Jehovah.
149.1 Waeeom8k Jehovah: an8hom8k Jehovah wuske an8homáonk, kah wuttabuttantam8onk ummukkinneongan8 waneetupanatogig.
149.2 Israel weekontam8wononch neh kezhikupoh: wunneechanoh Sion weekontam8nàhettich wussantimaum8oh.
149.3 Waeenodtúmwehettich 8wesuonk nashpe puhpeg, an8homauahettich tabuttantam8ongash nashpe timbrel kah harp.
149.4 Newutche Jehovah weeteánumau ummissinninnúmoh: pish 8néheau neh manunnissunutche nashpe wadchanittuonk.
149.5 Wunneetupanatamwog muskouanatamohettich ut sohsumoonganit: mishont8wae 8humahettich wutappinneáont.
149.6 Qunúhqueu tabuttantamauaongash Manit ohtaj wutt8n8wóut: kah togkodteg aéhtae kenag ohtaj wunnutchegan8wout.
149.7 Ussenat wutann8tauwaonk penuwohteuh, kah sasámakouwhittuongash ut missinninnùtu.
149.8 Tahtogkuppinnon kehtahs8timwog m8ôhshagquohtogquosh: kah wutt8owosketompaog m8ôhshagquohtogquosh.
149.9 Néhheoneau n nag neanussukwhosik wussittumóonk: yeu ukquttiantam8ongan8 wame 8neetupanatam8moh: waeenom8k Jehovah.
150.1 Waeenom8k Jehovah, waeenom8k Manit ut 8neetupanatamwe weekit: waeenom8k ut mamahchekesukqut ne ummenuhkesuonk ohtag.
150.2 Waeenom8k wutch ummishanakausuongash: unn8waeenom8k neaunag ummissugkenuonk.
150.3 Waeenom8k nashpe wadtauatonkqussue monopuhpeg; waeenom8k nashpe psaltery kah harp.
150.4 Waeenom8k nashpe timbrel kah puhpeg: waeenom8k nashpe pemeneohtone pequonash kah organsash.
150.5 Waeenom8k nashpe mishontowáe cymbalsash: waeenom8k nashpe mishontowae cymbalsash
150.6 Nishnow oâus wuñahnahshonat waeenomonch Jehovah: waeenom8k Jehovah.
